### [1] [Approximate vortex lattices of atomic Fermi superfluid on a spherical surface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05216)
*Keshab Sony,Yan He,Chih-Chun Chien*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究通过两种基于金兹堡-朗道理论的方法，表征了球形表面上原子费米超流体在有效单极场下的近似涡旋结构，发现随着涡旋数量增加，斐波那契晶格和能量最小化解的阿布里科索夫参数趋近于平面值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平面费米超流体在磁场或有效规范场下会形成阿布里科索夫涡旋晶格，但球形几何结构在超过20个涡旋时无法形成完美晶格。研究旨在表征球形表面上原子费米超流体在有效单极场下的近似涡旋结构，作为平面涡旋晶格问题的类比。

Method: 采用两种基于金兹堡-朗道理论（Ginzburg-Landau theory）的构造方法：第一种是几何方法，使用随机、测地线穹顶和斐波那契晶格（Fibonacci lattices）作为支架，从简并的单极谐波构造序参数；第二种通过数值调整系数最小化自由能，寻找具有最小阿布里科索夫参数（Abrikosov parameter）的解。

Result: 验证了两种构造方法产生的涡旋都是序参数的零点，涡旋核周围存在循环电流。随着涡旋数量增加，斐波那契晶格和能量最小化解的阿布里科索夫参数都外推至平面值。

Conclusion: 研究为薄球形壳几何中的超冷原子系统提供了理论框架，表明在球形表面上可以构造近似涡旋结构，其性质在涡旋数量增加时趋近于平面系统的行为。

Abstract: While planar Fermi superfluids form Abrikosov vortex lattices under magnetic or effective gauge fields, spherical geometry forbids perfect lattices above 20 vortices. We characterize approximate vortex structures of atomic Fermi superfluids under an effective monopole field on a spherical surface as an analogue of the planar vortex-lattice problem by two constructions based on the Ginzburg-Landau theory. The first one is geometric and uses the random, geodesic-dome, and Fibonacci lattices as scaffolds to construct the order parameter from the degenerate monopole harmonics. The second one minimizes the free energy by numerically adjusting the coefficients to find the solution with the minimal Abrikosov parameter. We have verified the vortices from both constructions are zeros of the order parameter with circulating currents around the vortex cores. As the number of vortices increases, the Abrikosov parameters of both the Fibonacci-lattice and minimization solutions extrapolate to the planar value. We briefly discuss implications for ultracold atoms in thin spherical-shell geometry.

</details>


### [2] [Mpemba Effect in an Expanding Lieb-Liniger Bose gas in a hard wall box](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05408)
*Sumita Datta*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究在强相互作用一维玻色气体的Tonks-Girardeau（汤克斯-吉拉尔杜）体系中，通过突然的盒子膨胀实验，观测到了Mpemba型效应（姆彭巴效应），即初始远离平衡态的系统比接近平衡态的系统弛豫更快。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Mpemba效应（姆彭巴效应）作为反直觉的弛豫现象，在经典随机系统和量子系统中均有研究，但其表现强烈依赖于可观测量选择和系统动力学约束。本研究旨在探索该效应在强相互作用一维量子系统中的具体表现。

Method: 研究采用Tonks-Girardeau（汤克斯-吉拉尔杜）体系中的强相互作用一维玻色气体，通过突然的盒子膨胀（从长度L_0到L）来激发密度重分布动力学。定义基于空间区域密度差的物理距离函数来分析弛豫过程。

Result: 基态和激发对称性扇区的弛豫动力学在时间上呈现明显交叉，表明弛豫顺序发生反转。这种Mpemba型效应源于初始态结构、可积性和空间重分布之间的相互作用，创造了不同的弛豫路径。

Conclusion: Mpemba效应并非普遍定律，而是依赖于特定动力学条件的可观测量相关现象。研究澄清了将该效应与牛顿冷却定律相联系的常见误解，明确了可积量子系统中出现此类反常弛豫行为的条件。

Abstract: The Mpemba effect, broadly understood as the counterintuitive phenomenon in which a system initially farther from equilibrium relaxes faster than a system closer to equilibrium, has been widely studied in classical stochastic systems and, more recently, in quantum settings. However, its manifestation is strongly dependent on the choice of observable and the dynamical constraints of the system.
  In this work, we investigate the emergence of a Mpemba-type effect in the density redistribution dynamics of a strongly interacting one-dimensional Bose gas in the Tonks-Girardeau regime undergoing a sudden box expansion from length L_0 to L. By defining a physically motivated distance function based on the difference of densities between spatial regions, we provide evidence that -the relaxation dynamics of the ground and excited symmetry sectors exhibit a clear crossing in time, indicating a reversal in relaxation ordering.
  We emphasize that the Mpemba effect is not a universal law but rather an observable-dependent phenomenon that arises under specific dynamical conditions. In particular, we show that the interplay between initial state structure, integrability, and spatial redistribution leads to distinct relaxation pathways that enable the effect. Our results clarify common misconceptions linking the Mpemba effect to Newton's law of cooling and highlight the conditions under which such anomalous relaxation behavior can emerge in integrable quantum systems.

</details>


### [3] [Rf spectra and pseudogap in ultracold Fermi gases across the BCS-BEC crossover from pairing fluctuation theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06004)
*Chuping Li,Lin Sun,Kaichao Zhang,Junru Wu,Yuxuan Wu,Dingli Yuan,Pengyi Chen,Qijin Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究通过改进配对涨落理论，结合粒子-空穴涨落，对超冷原子气体在BCS-BEC渡越中的赝隙现象进行了定量分析。研究采用全数值卷积方法计算配对磁化率和自能，揭示了赝隙的配对起源机制，并与实验数据达成定量一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 赝隙（pseudogap）现象是强相互作用费米系统（从高温超导体到超冷原子气体）的标志性特征，但其精确起源仍存在争议。研究旨在通过定量分析超冷原子气体在BCS-BEC渡越（BCS-BEC crossover）中的配对机制来阐明赝隙的起源。

Method: 研究改进了配对涨落理论（pairing fluctuation theory），通过纳入粒子-空穴涨落（particle-hole fluctuations）来重整化粒子-粒子通道中的有效相互作用。为实现定量精度，采用全数值卷积（full numerical convolution）方法计算配对磁化率（pair susceptibility）和自能（self-energy），超越了之前的解析赝隙近似。

Result: 计算结果显示，当系统从BCS区域向BEC移动时，赝隙连续出现。配对谱函数表明，在能量高于2Δ时，配对变得扩散，表明配对寿命受虚拟结合和解结合过程控制。研究提取了赝隙Δ、哈特里能量（Hartree energy）和化学势在渡越过程中的演化。计算结果与最近在BCS-BEC渡越（包括幺正性区域）的实验数据达成定量一致。

Conclusion: 研究为赝隙的配对起源机制提供了强有力的支持，表明配对涨落理论能够定量描述超冷原子气体在BCS-BEC渡越中的赝隙现象。数值卷积方法自动捕获了有限配对寿命导致的费米子全谱展宽以及先前被忽略的配对-空穴散射效应。

Abstract: The pseudogap phenomenon is a hallmark of strongly interacting Fermi systems, from high-temperature superconductors to ultracold atomic gases, yet its precise origin remains debated. Here we calculate the spectral function and rf spectra of ultracold atomic gases across the BCS-BEC crossover to quantitatively investigate the pairing mechanism of the pseudogap. We advance our pairing fluctuation theory by incorporating particle-hole fluctuations, which renormalize the effective interaction in the particle-particle channel. To achieve quantitative accuracy, we employ a full numerical convolution for the pair susceptibility and self-energy, moving beyond previous analytic pseudogap approximations. This convolution approach automatically captures two critical effects: (i) the full spectral broadening of fermions due to finite pair lifetime, and (ii) the previously neglected pair-hole scattering effect, which manifests as a substantial Hartree energy. We calculate the spectral function, and use rf spectral intensity maps and energy distribution curves to determine the quasiparticle dispersion. From these, we extract the pseudogap $Δ$, Hartree energy, and chemical potential, mapping their evolution across the crossover. Our results show that the pseudogap emerges continuously as the system moves from the BCS regime toward BEC. Furthermore, the pair spectral function reveals that pairs become diffusive at energies above 2$Δ$, indicating that the pair lifetime is governed by virtual binding and unbinding processes. Our calculations achieve quantitative agreement with recent experiments across the BCS-BEC crossover, including at unitarity, providing strong support for a pairing-based origin of the pseudogap as described by our pairing fluctuation theory.

</details>

# math.DS [[Back]](#toc)

### [4] [Effective stability estimates close to resonances with applications to rotational dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04955)
*Alessandra Celletti,Anargyros Dogkas,Alessia Francesca Guido*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 该研究针对近可积哈密顿系统，在非共振域中利用类Nekhoroshev估计提供作用变量的长期有效稳定性边界，并通过优化算法最大化稳定时间，应用于天体力学中的旋转动力学模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究近可积哈密顿系统在非共振域中的长期稳定性问题，特别关注共振邻域内作用变量的有效稳定性边界，旨在为天体力学中的旋转动力学模型提供稳定性分析工具。

Method: 采用类Nekhoroshev估计（Nekhoroshev-like estimates）在共振邻域内提供作用变量的有效稳定性边界；开发优化算法选择参数以最大化稳定时间；利用微扰理论（perturbation theory）降低扰动函数范数；分析收敛于共振频率的无理（Diophantine）频率序列的稳定性。

Result: 实现了有效稳定性估计与微扰理论的结合程序，应用于两个天体力学旋转动力学模型：由一维时间相关哈密顿量描述的spin-orbit问题，以及由二维时间相关哈密顿量描述的spin-spin-orbit模型；展示了接近这些模型主要共振轨道的稳定性结果。

Conclusion: 该研究为近可积哈密顿系统在非共振域中的长期稳定性提供了有效的分析框架，通过优化参数和降低扰动范数改进了稳定性估计，成功应用于天体力学旋转动力学模型的主要共振轨道稳定性分析。

Abstract: We consider nearly-integrable Hamiltonian systems defined over a non-resonant domain. In the neighborhood of resonances, we use Nekhoroshev-like estimates to provide effective stability bounds for the action variables over long time. The applicability conditions of these estimates allow some freedom in the choice of parameters. Hence, we develop an optimization algorithm for choosing parameters that maximize the stability time. To further improve the stability estimates, we use perturbation theory to reduce the norm of the perturbing function. We implement this procedure (effective stability estimates and perturbation theory) to analyze the stability of sequences of irrational (Diophantine) frequencies converging to frequencies corresponding to resonances. We consider two applications to models describing problems of rotational dynamics in Celestial Mechanics: the spin-orbit problem, described by a 1D time-dependent Hamiltonian, and the spin-spin-orbit model, described by a 2D time-dependent Hamiltonian. We show stability results for orbits close to the main resonances associated with such models.

</details>


### [5] [Families of periodic solutions of the 4- and 6-body problem using a gradient-free continuation method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05653)
*Oscar Perdomo*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无梯度（gradient-free）方法求解方程组，并应用于构建4体和6体问题的两类伪周期平面解族。该方法为仅使用函数评估的随机黑盒（stochastic black-box）过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在开发一种无需梯度信息的数值方法，用于求解天体力学中的多体问题（many-body problem），特别是构建4体和6体问题的伪周期（pseudo-periodic）平面解。

Method: 采用无梯度（gradient-free）的随机黑盒（stochastic black-box）方法，仅依赖函数评估来求解方程组。通过施加旋转和重标记（relabeling）后的返回条件（return conditions）来计算周期解族。

Result: 成功构建了两类伪周期平面解族：对于4体问题，质量1和m₂的物体分别成对反向运动；对于6体问题，质量1和m₂的物体分别位于以原点为中心的两个等边三角形顶点上运动。

Conclusion: 所提出的无梯度方法能有效求解多体问题方程组，成功构造了4体和6体问题的伪周期平面解族，验证了该数值方法在天体力学中的应用潜力。

Abstract: In this paper, we describe a gradient-free method to solve a system of equations, and we use it to construct two families of pseudo-periodic planar solutions of the 4- and 6-body problem. The method is a stochastic black-box procedure that uses only function evaluations. For the 4-body problem, bodies 1 and 2 have mass 1 and move opposite to each other, and bodies 3 and 4 have mass $m_2$ and also move opposite to each other. For the 6-body problem, bodies 1, 2, and 3 have mass 1 and move on the vertices of an equilateral triangle centered at the origin, and bodies 4, 5, and 6 have mass $m_2$ and also move on the vertices of an equilateral triangle. In both cases, we compute families of periodic solutions by imposing return conditions up to rotation and relabeling.

</details>

# cs.RO [[Back]](#toc)

### [6] [ZipFold: Modular Actuators for Scaleable Adaptive Robots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05260)
*Niklas Hagemann,Daniela Rus*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文介绍了一种紧凑、易于制造的折叠式执行器，通过柔性3D打印塑料条的复合折叠和拉链式连接，实现可逆的尺寸和刚度变换，并展示了其在四模块自适应行走机器人中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前机器人需要能够改变形状、尺寸和机械特性以适应不断变化的任务和环境，但现有形状变换系统通常采用定制的、系统特定的机制，难以扩展、重新配置或在不同应用间移植。

Method: 本文提出了一种紧凑、易于制造的折叠式执行器（deployable actuator），通过柔性3D打印塑料条的复合折叠（compound folding）和拉链式连接（zipping）形成方形截面的可展开梁（deployable beams），实现可逆的尺寸和刚度变换。

Result: 该执行器能够在紧凑（柔性）和展开（准刚性）状态之间实现平滑、连续的过渡，当模块组合成更大组件时，能够实现多样的形状和刚度变换。执行器的机械性能得到表征，并展示了包含四模块自适应行走机器人的集成系统。

Conclusion: 这种折叠式执行器提供了一种解决当前形状变换系统局限性的方案，通过简单的驱动方法实现可逆的尺寸和刚度变换，为构建适应性机器人系统提供了新的可能性。

Abstract: There is a growing need for robots that can change their shape, size and mechanical properties to adapt to evolving tasks and environments. However, current shape-changing systems generally utilize bespoke, system-specific mechanisms that can be difficult to scale, reconfigure or translate from one application to another. This paper introduces a compact, easy-to-fabricate deployable actuator that achieves reversible scale and stiffness transformations through compound folding and zipping of flexible 3D-printed plastic strips into square-section deployable beams. The simple actuation method allows for smooth, continuous transitions between compact (flexible) and expanded (quasi-rigid) states, facilitating diverse shape and stiffness transformations when modules are combined into larger assemblies. The actuator's mechanical performance is characterized and an integrated system involving a four-module adaptive walking robot is demonstrated.

</details>


<div id='hep-ph'></div>

# hep-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [7] [Bridging the divide: axion searches and axino phenomenology at colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.07224)
*Gabe Hoshino,Kristin Dona,Keisuke Harigaya,David W. Miller,Jan T. Offermann,Bianca Pol,Benjamin Rosser*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文探讨了超对称DFSZ轴子模型，其中轴微子（axino）与希格斯（Higgs）扇区存在树级耦合。研究表明，在R宇称守恒条件下，大型强子对撞机（LHC）能够探测到较重中性微子（neutralino）衰变为较轻轴微子态的现象，从而有效探测轴子衰变常数低于10¹¹ GeV的参数空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在扩展最小超对称标准模型（MSSM）以包含轴子（axion）及其超对称伙伴轴微子（axino）。研究动机在于探索超对称DFSZ轴子模型中轴微子与希格斯扇区的树级耦合，并评估现有对撞机实验对该类模型的探测能力。

Method: 研究方法基于超对称DFSZ轴子模型，其中较重中性微子态衰变为较轻轴微子态。使用MadGraph进行蒙特卡洛模拟生成，并利用MadAnalysis5框架评估实验灵敏度，包括探测器模拟和运动学选择。

Result: 研究结果显示，当希格斯微子质量低于1 TeV时，大型强子对撞机在140 fb⁻¹积分亮度下能够有效探测轴子衰变常数f_a < 10¹¹ GeV的参数空间。这表明现有对撞机实验能够研究超对称DFSZ轴子模型。

Conclusion: 本文证明超对称DFSZ轴子模型可通过现有对撞机实验进行研究，为直接探测和天体物理搜索提供互补灵敏度，并为更广泛探索超对称轴子场景铺平道路。

Abstract: We discuss a phenomenological model that extends the minimal supersymmetric standard model to contain axions and their supersymmetric partner, the axino. In the supersymmetric DFSZ axion model, the axino has tree level couplings to the higgs sector. In the case where $R$-parity is conserved, collider experiments may be sensitive to displaced decays of heavier neutralino states into lighter, mostly axino states. We present a sensitivity analysis using a model in which mostly higgsino next-to-lightest supersymmetric particle states decay into a mostly axino lightest supersymmetric particle. The model is studied using Monte Carlo simulation produced using $\texttt{MadGraph}$ and estimates of experimental sensitivities to the model, including detector simulation and kinematic selections, are evaluated using the $\texttt{MadAnalysis5}$ framework. For a higgsino mass below 1 TeV, the axion decay constant below $f_{a} < 10^{11}$ GeV can be effectively probed by the Large Hadron Collider with an integrated luminosity of 140 fb$^{-1}$. This work demonstrates that supersymmetric DFSZ axion models can be studied with existing collider experiments, offering complementary sensitivity to direct-detection and astrophysical searches and paving the way for broader exploration of supersymmetric axion scenarios.

</details>


### [8] [Unquenched Radially Excited $P$-wave Charmonia](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04991)
*George Rupp*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究使用共振谱展开（Resonance-Spectrum Expansion）方法，结合所有OZI允许的衰变道，计算了最低P波粲偶素（c\bar{c}）的第一径向激发态，以解释PDG中3.85-3.95 GeV能区五个候选态的不同质量模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 静态（"淬火"）夸克模型能很好地描述基态正宇称粲偶素，但PDG中3.85-3.95 GeV能区的五个P波粲偶素候选态（可能包含上述态的第一径向激发）显示出完全不同的质量模式，且存在两个标量态χ_{c0}(3860)和χ_{c0}(3915)，前者明显很宽。

Method: 采用共振谱展开（Resonance-Spectrum Expansion）方法，在计算中包含了所有OZI允许的衰变道中最相关的粲介子对。使用基于^{3}P_0模型的广义衰变耦合常数计算方案，确保不同正宇称粲偶素允许衰变道的类别差异不会导致谱的畸变。

Result: 论文将展示最低P波c\bar{c}态第一径向激发的初步计算结果，这些结果通过包含所有相关衰变道的共振谱展开方法获得。

Conclusion: 通过包含所有OZI允许衰变道的共振谱展开计算，有望解释PDG中3.85-3.95 GeV能区P波粲偶素候选态的不同质量模式，特别是两个标量态的存在和宽度差异。

Abstract: The ground-state positive-parity charmonia $χ_{c0}(1P)$, $χ_{c1}(1P)$, $h_c(1P)$, and $χ_{c2}(1P)$ are generally well described in static (``quenched'') quark models, in which dynamical effects of actual or virtual strong decay are neglected. In contrast, the five PDG candidates for $P$-wave charmonia in the energy region 3.85-3.95 GeV, probably including the first radial excitations of the above ones, display a totally different and quite disparate mass pattern. Moreover, two scalar states are listed, viz. $χ_{c0}(3860)$ and $χ_{c0}(3915)$, the former one apparently being very broad.
  Preliminary results will be presented here for the first radial excitations of the lowest $P$-wave $c\bar{c}$ states, obtained with the Resonance-Spectrum Expansion while including in the calculation all OZI-allowed decay channels of the most relevant charm-meson pairs. Employing a generalised scheme of computing coupling constants for decays based on the ${}^{3\!}P_0$ model ensures that no distortion of the spectra will occur due to the different classes of allowed decay channels for the various positive-parity charmonia.

</details>


### [9] [$b \to c$ semileptonic sum rule: SU(3)$_{\rm{F}}$ symmetry violation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05186)
*Syuhei Iguro*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究将b→c半轻子衰变求和规则从{B→D^{(*)} lν̄, Λ_b→Λ_c lν̄}扩展到包含{B_s→D_s^{(*)} lν̄, Ξ_b→Ξ_c lν̄}，以提供更有效的交叉检验。虽然求和规则基于重夸克对称性（HQS）和SU(3)味对称性，但实际对称性破缺效应被量化评估，结果显示破缺程度小于预期实验不确定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了澄清b→cτν̄过程中可能的偏差，b→c半轻子求和规则提供了一个有价值的工具。该关系基于重夸克对称性（heavy quark symmetry, HQS）推导，为实验结果提供了一致性检验。本研究旨在扩展先前提出的求和规则，使其包含更多衰变过程，从而增强检验能力。

Method: 将先前提出的针对{B→D^{(*)} lν̄, Λ_b→Λ_c lν̄}的求和规则扩展到包含{B_s→D_s^{(*)} lν̄, Ξ_b→Ξ_c lν̄}。虽然该关系基于重夸克对称性（HQS）和SU(3)味对称性，但通过数值评估量化对称性破缺效应，并与未来实验灵敏度进行比较。

Result: 研究发现对称性破缺程度小于预期实验不确定性。尽管基于手征微扰理论（chiral perturbation theory）预期破缺程度适中，但数值评估确认了求和规则的有效性。因此构建了新的与超出标准模型新物理（new physics）无关的预测性求和规则来检验一致性。

Conclusion: 扩展后的求和规则为b→c半轻子衰变过程提供了更全面的交叉检验工具。对称性破缺效应的量化分析表明，该规则在实验精度范围内保持有效，从而能够可靠地检测可能的超出标准模型新物理信号。

Abstract: To clarify possible deviations in $b\to cτ\overlineν$ processes, the $b\to c$ semileptonic sum rule provides a valuable tool. This relation, derived based on heavy quark symmetry (HQS), offers a powerful consistency check among experimental results. In this work, we extend the previously proposed sum rule for $\{B\to D^{(*)} l\overlineν,\,Λ_b\to Λ_c l\overlineν\}$ to include $\{B_s\to D_s^{(*)} l\overlineν,\,Ξ_b\to Ξ_c l\overlineν\}$, thereby enabling more useful cross-checks. Although the relation is supported by HQS and SU(3) flavor symmetry, both symmetries are broken in reality, and the size of the violation needs to be quantified to assess the validity of the sum rule. While the violation is expected to be moderate based on chiral perturbation theory, we perform a numerical evaluation and compare it with future experimental sensitivities. We find that the violation remains smaller than the expected experimental uncertainty. Therefore another new physics agnostic and predictive sum rules are constructed to check the consistency.

</details>


### [10] [Thermodynamic and Transport Properties of Quark-Gluon Plasma at Finite Chemical Potential with a DNN framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05858)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热系统的特性强烈依赖于其对温度梯度的响应以及组分间的微观相互作用。本研究旨在探索有限重子化学势下夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma, QGP）的热力学和输运性质。

Method: 采用深度学习辅助的准粒子模型（deep-learning-assisted quasi-particle model, DLQPM），使用神经网络训练来复现格点QCD（lattice QCD, lQCD）在零重子化学势附近通过类泰勒展开获得的物态方程结果，从而估计依赖于温度和重子化学势的准粒子热质量。

Result: 训练后的模型作为有效模拟器，能够估计有限重子化学势下的热力学和输运性质。计算了退禁闭介质中的声速、比热、粘度和电导率，结果与现有格点计算和其他唯象模型吻合良好。

Conclusion: 本研究证明基于深度神经网络（DNN-based）的方法为研究有限重子密度下夸克-胶子等离子体的性质提供了一个高效框架。

Abstract: The characteristics of a thermal system depend strongly on its response to thermal gradients and the underlying microscopic interactions among constituents. In the present study, we investigate the thermodynamic and transport properties of the quark-gluon plasma (QGP) at finite baryon chemical potential within a deep-learning-assisted quasi-particle model (DLQPM). The temperature ($\mathrm{T}$) and baryon chemical potential ($μ_B$)-dependent thermal masses of quasi-particles are estimated using neural networks trained to reproduce lattice QCD (lQCD) results for the equation of state, obtained via a Taylor-like expansion around vanishing baryon chemical potential. The trained model acts as an effective emulator, enabling us to estimate the thermodynamic and transport properties at finite $μ_B$. We compute the speed of sound, specific heat, viscosity, and conductivity of the deconfined medium. Our findings are in good agreement with available lattice calculations and other phenomenological models. The present study demonstrates that a DNN-based approach provides an efficient framework for studying the properties of the QGP at finite baryon density.

### [11] [Gravitational Waves from Matter Perturbations of Spectator Scalar Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05078)
*Marcos A. G. Garcia,Angel Garcia-Vega,Sarunas Verner*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究计算了由旁观标量场（spectator scalar field）在二阶扰动下产生的随机引力波背景，该场通过门户相互作用与暴胀子耦合，并在再加热期间经历参数共振放大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索通过门户相互作用耦合的旁观标量场在再加热期间产生的二阶引力波背景，特别是参数共振放大效应及其对引力波信号的贡献。

Method: 方法包括计算二阶爱因斯坦方程中的直接场梯度源项，推导出将谱积分与时间积分因子化的主公式，并采用Hartree近似处理非线性效应，同时与非线性晶格模拟进行对比验证。

Result: 研究获得了引力波峰值振幅的解析标度关系，发现信号对门户耦合强度有强依赖性而对旁观场质量敏感度较弱，在特定参数下可达Ω_GW h² ~ 10⁻¹¹，且四阶自耦合对信号有非单调影响。

Conclusion: 该框架成功描述了旁观标量场通过参数共振产生的二阶引力波背景，Hartree处理与晶格模拟具有互补性，为探索高频引力波信号提供了理论工具。

Abstract: We compute the stochastic gravitational wave background sourced at second order by a spectator scalar field $χ$ coupled to the inflaton $φ$ through a portal interaction $σφ^2χ^2$ and with quartic self-interaction $λ_χχ^4/4!$. In the large portal coupling regime ($σ/λ\gg 1$, with $λ$ the inflaton normalization), parametric resonance during reheating amplifies the spectator power spectrum by many orders of magnitude near the resonance band until Hartree backreaction from the quartic coupling detunes the instability, while the large inflationary effective mass suppresses superhorizon power and ensures compatibility with CMB isocurvature bounds. We focus on the direct field-gradient source $\partial_aχ\,\partial_bχ$ in the second-order Einstein equations and derive a master formula that factorizes into a spectral integral over the frozen, vacuum-subtracted spectator spectrum and a time integral encoding the post-inflationary expansion history. For our benchmark reheating history we obtain analytic scaling relations, including a peak amplitude $Ω_{\rm GW}\propto T_{\rm reh}^{8/3}$, strong dependence on the portal strength, and weak sensitivity to $m_χ$. We validate the framework against nonlinear lattice simulations, demonstrating complementarity: the Hartree treatment captures superhorizon evolution inaccessible to the lattice, while the lattice resolves rescattering and fragmentation near the spectral peak. For $σ/λ\simeq 10^4$ and $T_{\rm reh}=2 \times 10^{14}\,\mathrm{GeV}$, the signal reaches $Ω_{\rm GW}h^2\sim 10^{-11}$ at $f\sim10^{7}$-$10^{8}\,\mathrm{Hz}$. Increasing $λ_χ$ at fixed $σ$ has a non-monotonic effect: small values enhance the signal via rescattering, whereas larger values suppress it by detuning the resonance.

### [12] [Learning to Unscramble Feynman Loop Integrals with SAILIR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05034)
*David Shih*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: SAILIR（Self-supervised AI for Loop Integral Reduction）提出了一种基于Transformer分类器的机器学习方法，用于费曼积分（Feynman integrals）的IBP（integration-by-parts）约化。该方法通过自监督训练和波束搜索（beam search）策略，实现了内存消耗与积分复杂度无关的稳定约化，突破了传统Laporta算法的内存瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于Laporta算法的IBP约化方法在处理高复杂度积分时面临严重的内存瓶颈，其内存消耗随积分复杂度快速增长。这限制了高能物理（high-energy physics）中高精度计算的发展，需要一种能够突破内存限制的新范式。

Method: SAILIR采用基于Transformer的分类器，通过自监督（self-supervised）方式在合成数据上训练。训练数据通过scramble/unscramble过程生成：将已知约化恒等式反向应用构建复杂表达式，分类器学习逆向这些步骤。结合波束搜索和高度并行化、异步的单次约化策略，实现有界内存的在线约化。

Result: 在双圈三角盒拓扑（two-loop triangle-box topology）的16个不同复杂度积分上，SAILIR与最先进的IBP约化代码Kira进行对比。SAILIR的每个工作进程内存消耗基本保持稳定，而Kira的内存随复杂度快速增长。对于最复杂的积分，SAILIR仅使用Kira 40%的内存，同时达到相当的约化时间。

Conclusion: SAILIR展示了IBP约化的全新范式，能够完全克服基于Laporta方法的内存瓶颈。这为目前难以处理的高精度计算打开了可能性，代表了计算高能物理领域的重要进展。

Abstract: Integration-by-parts (IBP) reduction of Feynman integrals to master integrals is a key computational bottleneck in precision calculations in high-energy physics. Traditional approaches based on the Laporta algorithm require solving large systems of equations, leading to memory consumption that grows rapidly with integral complexity. We present SAILIR (Self-supervised AI for Loop Integral Reduction), a new machine learning approach in which a transformer-based classifier guides the reduction of integrals one step at a time in a fully online fashion. The classifier is trained in an entirely self-supervised manner on synthetic data generated by a scramble/unscramble procedure: known reduction identities are applied in reverse to build expressions of increasing complexity, and the classifier learns to undo these steps. When combined with beam search and a highly parallelized, asynchronous, single-episode reduction strategy, SAILIR can reduce integrals of arbitrarily high weight with bounded memory. We benchmark SAILIR on the two-loop triangle-box topology, comparing against the state-of-the-art IBP reduction code Kira across 16 integrals of varying complexity. While SAILIR is slower in wall-clock time, its per-worker memory consumption remains approximately flat regardless of integral complexity, in contrast to Kira whose memory grows rapidly with complexity. For the most complex integrals considered here, SAILIR uses only 40\% of the memory of Kira while achieving comparable reduction times. This demonstrates a fundamentally new paradigm for IBP reduction in which the memory bottleneck of Laporta-based approaches could be entirely overcome, potentially opening the door to precision calculations that are currently intractable.

</details>


### [13] [Gauge coupling unification and doublet-triplet splitting via GUT dynamical breaking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05509)
*Isabella Masina,Mariano Quiros*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文探讨了通过添加d≥5的非重整化算符（non-renormalizable operators）来实现规范耦合统一（gauge coupling unification）的框架，分析了SU(5)大统一理论（grand unified theory）中不同表示（representations）的可行性，特别关注了动力学破缺（dynamical breaking）与双态-三重态劈裂问题（doublet-triplet splitting problem）的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索通过引入非重整化算符来修正规范场动能项，从而实现标准模型（Standard Model）规范耦合统一的新框架。该方法旨在解决传统大统一理论中的耦合常数统一问题，同时探索动力学破缺模式与双态-三重态劈裂问题的潜在联系。

Method: 研究方法包括：首先系统回顾在SU(5)大统一理论背景下，非重整化算符框架的相关现象学（phenomenology）；其次识别为实现耦合统一最有前景的表示；最后分析动力学破缺模式，特别关注费米子凝聚（condensates of fermions）在不同表示中的表现。

Result: 研究结果表明：5表示的费米子凝聚因质子衰变（proton decay）约束而不构成可行模型；相反，10表示和24表示的费米子凝聚能够成功构建可行模型。这揭示了不同表示在满足质子衰变约束条件下的差异性表现。

Conclusion: 结论指出，在SU(5)大统一理论的非重整化算符框架中，10和24表示的费米子凝聚是构建可行统一模型的关键，而5表示因质子衰变约束被排除。该研究为连接规范耦合统一与双态-三重态劈裂问题提供了新的理论途径。

Abstract: An interesting framework to achieve gauge coupling unification consists in adding to the Standard Model Lagrangian non-renormalizable operators of $d \geq 5$, which affect the kinetic term of gauge fields. We first review the phenomenology related to this framework in the context of $SU(5)$, identifying which are the most interesting representations for the sake of achieving coupling unification. Secondly, we point out that in the case of a dynamical breaking pattern, it is possible to relate gauge coupling unification with the doublet-triplet splitting problem. We show that condensates of fermions in the $5$ representation do not lead to viable models because of proton decay constraints. At difference, we point out that successful models can be obtained by considering condensates of fermions in the $10$, as well as in the $24$ representations.

Conclusion: 模不变标准模型扩展中，模场作为暴胀子时，汤川耦合的CP破坏相演化导致希格斯凝聚和增强的宇宙对撞机信号。该理论框架为通过下一代宇宙学实验探测亚普朗克尺度的模场衰变常数提供了可能途径。

Abstract: We consider a modular-invariant extension of the Standard Model. Assuming that the modulus is the inflaton, the CP-violating phases of the Yukawa couplings evolve during inflation. This dynamics favours a Higgs condensate, so that Standard Model fermions mediate a one-loop cosmological collider signal enhanced by chemical potentials. Next-generation experiments can probe sub-Planckian values of the modulus decay constant. We provide precise expressions for Dirac fermions with chemical potentials in de Sitter.

### [15] [Visualizing the interplay of dual electronic nematicities in kagome superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05506)
*Yunmei Zhang,Jun Zhan,Ping Wu,Yun-Peng Huang,Qixiao Yuan,Hongyu Li,Zhuying Wang,Wanru Ma,Shuikang Yu,Kunming Zhang,Wanlin Cheng,Deshu Chen,Minrui Chen,Tao Wu,Ziji Xiang,Xianxin Wu,Zhenyu Wang,Xianhui Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过扫描隧道显微镜（STM）分析CsV3Sb5的温度和Ti掺杂依赖电子结构，揭示了两种向列序（nematic order）的复杂相互作用：一种与电荷密度波（CDW）相关，另一种表现为V-dx2-y2费米口袋的C2畸变而不破坏平移对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kagome超导体AV3Sb5中由几何阻挫和电子关联驱动的交织电子序（intertwined electronic orders）是研究重点，其中三重Q电荷密度波（triple-Q CDW）相内观察到的旋转和/或时间反演对称性破缺具有复杂的温度依赖性，这构成了核心谜题。

Method: 采用扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy, STM）研究CsV3Sb5的电子结构随温度和Ti掺杂的变化，并结合Ginzburg-Landau理论分析，以解析两种不同向列序参数（nematic order parameters）的相互关系。

Result: 研究发现第二种向列序（表现为V-dx2-y2费米口袋的C2畸变）在长程CDW被完全抑制的高掺杂水平和高温度下依然存在；其向列指向（nematic director）在中间掺杂时与CDW诱导的向列性方向不同，而在原始化合物中与强向列CDW序对齐，此时钒轨道准粒子在较低特征温度下变得相干。

Conclusion: 结合Ginzburg-Landau分析，研究揭示了两种可归属于不同kagome晶格轨道的向列序之间的丰富相互作用，为理解该材料家族中神秘的交织序提供了新视角，并建立了一个罕见的双重向列序共存和耦合的材料平台，可产生不寻常的关联现象。

Abstract: Kagome superconductor AV$_3$Sb$_5$ (A stands for K, Rb, and Cs) hosts a wealth of intertwined electronic orders driven by geometric frustration and electron correlations. Among them, the breaking of rotational and/or time-reversal symmetry, observed within the triple-$Q$ charge density wave (CDW) phase yet exhibiting a more complex temperature dependence, remains a central puzzle. Here, by using scanning tunneling microscopy to study the electronic structures of CsV$_3$Sb$_5$ as a function of temperature and Ti doping, we disentangle the interrelation between two distinct nematic order parameters, one associated with the CDW and the other manifested as $C_2$ distortion of the V-$d_{x^{2}-y^{2}}$ Fermi pockets without breaking transition symmetry. The latter persists to high doping levels and high temperatures where the long-range CDW is fully suppressed. Moreover, its nematic director is oriented in a lattice direction distinct from that of the CDW-induced nematicity at intermediate doping, and eventually aligns with the strong nematic CDW order in the pristine compound where the quasiparticles of vanadium orbitals become coherent below a lower characteristic temperature. These observations, combined with Ginzburg-Landau analysis, reveal a rich interplay between two nematic orders that can be assigned to distinct kagome-lattice orbitals. Our results shed new light on the enigmatic intertwined orders in this family and establish a rare material platform in which dual nematic orders coexist and couple to give rise to unusual correlated phenomena.

</details>


### [16] [Tunable superconductivity and spin density wave in La3Ni2O7/LaAlO3 thin films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05590)
*Yu-Han Cao,Kai-Yue Jiang,Hong-Yan Lu,Da Wang,Qiang-Hua Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 通过第一性原理计算和奇异模函数重整化群方法，系统研究了La3Ni2O7/LaAlO3薄膜中Ni-Ni层间距离对超导性的调控作用，揭示了层间距离变化如何驱动系统在C型自旋密度波、G型自旋密度波和s±波超导相之间的转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验发现La3Ni2O7薄膜在LaAlO3衬底上具有超导性，而相同面内晶格常数的块体材料在压力下却不超导，这表明Ni-Ni层间距离对超导性具有关键调控作用。研究旨在系统探索层间距离变化如何敏感地调控系统的基态。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principle calculations）与奇异模函数重整化群（singular-mode functional renormalization group）相结合的方法，在合理的Ni-Ni层间距离范围内系统研究La3Ni2O7/LaAlO3薄膜体系。

Result: 研究发现：较小层间距离时基态为C型自旋密度波（C-type spin density wave），层间自旋铁磁耦合；较大层间距离时为G型自旋密度波（G-type spin density wave），层间自旋反铁磁耦合。在两相之间出现s±波超导性（s±-wave superconductivity），主要配对来自镍3d₃z²-r²轨道。

Conclusion: 该结果解释了薄膜在常压下的超导性，并预测施加压力会降低超导转变温度直至系统进入C型自旋密度波相。实验验证将为理解该体系电子关联性质提供深刻见解，因为C型自旋密度波在巡游电子图像中更自然，而在局域磁矩图像中难以实现。

Abstract: Recently, La3Ni2O7 thin film on the LaAlO3 substrate is shown to be superconducting, while the bulk La3Ni2O7 with the same in-plane lattice constant under pressure does not superconduct. This difference suggests the interlayer distance $d_{\rm Ni-Ni}$ is crucial to control superconductivity, and its variation under pressure may tune the ground state sensitively. We investigate systematically the La3Ni2O7/LaAlO3 thin films in a reasonable range of $d_{\rm Ni-Ni}$, by a combination of the first-principle calculations and the singular-mode functional renormalization group. For smaller (larger) $d_{\rm Ni-Ni}$, the ground state is a C-type (G-type) spin density wave with spins coupled ferromagnetically (antiferromagnetically) across the two layers. Between the two phases, $s_\pm$-wave superconductivity emerges with dominant pairings between nickel $3d_{3z^2-r^2}$ orbitals. The results explain the experimental superconductivity in the thin film under ambient pressure, and predict that the applied pressure will decrease the superconducting transition temperature, until the system enters the C-type spin density wave. Experimental verification would provide profound insights into the nature of electron correlations in this system, since the C-type spin density wave is achieved most naturally in the itinerant picture, while it would be hard in the local moment picture where spins are always coupled antiferromagnetically across the layers.

</details>


### [17] [Band-basis decomposition of superfluid weight in magic-angle twisted bilayer graphene: Quantifying geometric and conventional contributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05994)
*Jian Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究将魔角扭曲双层石墨烯的超流权重分解为常规贡献和几何贡献，发现量子几何在平带子空间中贡献22-26%，考虑远带后几何贡献提升至55-58%，且在超导最强的填充因子附近达到峰值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解魔角扭曲双层石墨烯（MATBG）中超流权重的物理起源，特别是量子几何（quantum geometry）在超导性质中的贡献，这对于理解非常规超导机制具有重要意义。

Method: 采用基于能带的电流算符分裂方法，应用于Bistritzer-MacDonald连续模型，将超流权重分解为常规（能带速度）贡献和几何（带间相干）贡献，并在平带子空间和包含远带的完整能带结构中进行分析。

Result: 在平带子空间中，量子几何贡献占超流权重的22-26%（取决于配对对称性），交叉项可忽略不计；包含远带后几何贡献提升至约55-58%，而常规贡献收敛至2%以内，表明远带主要通过带间相干机制贡献；在超导最强的填充因子ν=±2附近，几何贡献达到峰值27-33%，且在实验相关能隙范围内不敏感。

Conclusion: 量子几何在魔角扭曲双层石墨烯的超流权重中扮演关键角色，远带主要通过带间相干机制贡献，几何贡献在超导最强的填充因子附近达到最大值，这为理解该体系中的非常规超导机制提供了重要见解。

Abstract: We decompose the superfluid weight D_s of magic-angle twisted bilayer graphene (MATBG) into conventional (band-velocity) and geometric (interband-coherence) contributions using a band-basis current operator splitting applied to the Bistritzer-MacDonald continuum model. In the flat-band subspace, quantum geometry accounts for 22-26% of D_s at charge neutrality depending on pairing symmetry, with cross terms vanishing to machine precision. Including remote bands raises the geometric fraction to ~55-58%, while D_s^conv converges to within 2% -- demonstrating that remote bands contribute exclusively through interband coherence. The geometric fraction peaks at ~27-33% near the nu = +/- 2 fillings where superconductivity is strongest, and is insensitive to gap magnitude in the experimentally relevant range.

</details>


### [18] [Numerically Exact Study of Flat-Band Superconductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05997)
*I. S. Tupitsyn,B. Currie,B. V. Svistunov,E. Kozik,N. V. Prokof'ev*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过受控的图蒙特卡洛方法，在具有吸引哈伯德相互作用的Lieb晶格中追踪超流响应的起始，发现在平带半填充情况下，配对响应随温度降低呈线性发散，导致在特征温度T_*处出现向长程关联的急剧交叉。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前平带系统高温超导理论预测转变温度与吸引相互作用呈线性关系T_c(U)=c|U|，但超越平均场和量子几何估计的c值及完整非线性T_c(U)曲线（在大|U|处有最大值）尚不清楚。

Method: 采用受控的图蒙特卡洛（diagrammatic Monte Carlo）技术，在具有吸引哈伯德相互作用（attractive Hubbard interaction）的Lieb晶格中追踪超流响应的起始，特别关注平带半填充情况。

Result: 发现在广泛的U范围内，配对响应随温度降低呈线性发散，导致在特征温度T_*处出现向长程关联的急剧交叉，T_*为T_c提供了受控的上界；当所有三个能带在单个动量点接触时，T_*达到最高值。

Conclusion: 平带半填充情况下的有序机制与BCS和预形成库珀对（preformed Cooper pair）方案有根本不同，特征温度T_*可能对应较高的T_c值，特别是在所有能带在单个动量点接触时。

Abstract: Current theories of high-temperature superconductivity in flat-band systems predict a linear dependence of the transition temperature on the attractive interaction, $T_c(U) = c|U|$. However, neither the value of $c$ nor the full nonlinear $T_c(U)$ curve -- with a maximum at large $|U|$ -- is known beyond mean-field and quantum geometry estimates. Using a controlled diagrammatic Monte Carlo technique, we trace the onset of superfluid response in the Lieb lattice with attractive Hubbard interaction. Focusing on the half-filled flat-band case, where the ordering mechanism differs fundamentally from both BCS and preformed Cooper pair scenarios, we find that the pairing response diverges linearly with decreasing temperature over a broad range of $U$, leading to a sharp crossover to long-range correlations at a characteristic temperature $T_*$, which provides a controlled upper bound on $T_c$. The highest $T_*$ occurs when all three bands touch at a single momentum point, potentially corresponding to high $T_c$ values.

### [19] [Enhanced enantiomer discrimination with chiral surface plasmons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05207)

Main category: physics.optics

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性腔中的强光-物质耦合已被提出作为选择性识别与腔手性模式相同手性对映体的有效方法。本研究旨在探索更高效的手性识别平台。

Method: 开发了量子电动力学（quantum electrodynamics）处理方法，将分子的电偶极矩和磁偶极矩纳入考虑。通过分析具有电导率和手性导率的二维界面支持的表面等离激元，并与手性镜腔进行比较。

Result: 手性表面等离激元的识别因子（discrimination factor）可比最佳手性镜腔提高近一个数量级，这归因于更强的场限制。表面等离激元与偶极在整个平面上的投影耦合，而腔模式仅与单一偏振轴耦合，这种几何差异产生了√2倍的方向平均增强。

Conclusion: 手性保持反射器进一步放大增强效果，为使用扭曲层平台进行手性传感开辟了实用途径。表面等离激元平台在手性识别方面比手性光学腔具有显著优势。

Abstract: Strong light-matter coupling in chiral cavities has been proposed as an effective way to selectively interact with an enantiomer that shares the same handedness as the cavity's chiral mode. We show that surface plasmons supported by a two-dimensional interface with both electric and chiral conductivities discriminate enantiomers more efficiently than chiral optical cavities. A quantum-electrodynamic treatment is developed to incorporate the molecule's electric and magnetic dipole moments. We show that the discrimination factor for a chiral plasmon can exceed that of the best chiral-mirror cavity by almost an order of magnitude due to stronger field confinement. In addition, surface plasmons couple to a dipole's projection onto an entire plane, whereas cavity (or free-space) modes couple only to a single polarization axis. This geometric difference produces a $\sqrt{2}$ orientation-averaged boost in chiral discrimination for chiral surface platforms. A handedness-preserving reflector further amplifies the enhancement, opening a practical route towards chiral sensing using twisted-layer platforms.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于MoOCl₂的巨大光学各向异性（giant optical anisotropy），研究团队实验制备了厚度分别为77nm和98nm的MoOCl₂四分之一波片（quarter-wave plates），并对其性能进行了表征。

Abstract: The miniaturization of polarization-controlling optical components is one of the central pursuits in nanophotonics. While traditional anisotropic materials require large propagation lengths to achieve the desired phase shifts, metasurfaces mitigate this size constraint but often introduce narrow operational bandwidths and high fabrication complexities. To bridge this gap, we introduce MoOCl2 as a promising material for ultracompact and broadband phase retardation. Building on its giant optical anisotropy, we experimentally demonstrate MoOCl2 quarter-wave plates with thicknesses of 77 nm and 98 nm. These flakes exhibit achromatic quarter-wave retardation across broad visible (445 - 525 nm) and near-infrared (730 - 945 nm) spectral windows, surpassing the fundamental thickness and bandwidth limitations of both conventional optical materials and artificial nanostructures. Moreover, MoOCl2 waveplates demonstrate up to lambda/4500 retardance tolerance at central wavelengths. As a result, this study establishes MoOCl2 as a building block for ultracompact polarization optics.

### [21] [Multistability of a chiral semiconductor microcavity: a self-consistent approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05945)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用平均场近似（mean-field approximation）和自洽近似（self-consistent approximation）进行计算，同时考虑了微腔中多个量子阱（multiple quantum wells）之间激子密度（exciton density）的差异。研究针对法向共振相干泵浦（resonant coherent pumping normal to the structure）条件进行计算。

Result: 计算结果表明，线性偏振泵浦能够引起非线性切换，使极化子达到高达90%的圆偏振度（degree of circular polarization）。这一效应在未针对高圆偏振度光致发光优化的系统中仍然显著。

Abstract: We calculate the effects of polariton bi- and multistability in a semiconductor Bragg microcavity with multiple quantum wells and a chiral photonic crystal on the upper mirror for resonant coherent pumping normal to the structure. Even if the system is not optimized for obtaining photoluminescence with a high degree of circular polarization in the spontaneous mode, it is shown that linear-polarized pumping can cause nonlinear switching to states with a degree of circular polarization of polaritons up to 90%. Calculations were performed in both the mean-field and self-consistent approximations, accounting for the difference in exciton density among the microcavity's quantum wells.

### [22] [Information Entropy is a General-Purpose Collective Variable for Enhanced Sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05239)
*Xiangrui Li,Daniel Schwalbe-Koda*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于局部信息熵（information entropy）的通用集体变量（collective variable），用于增强采样方法，能够无监督地发现传统序参数（order parameters）无法捕捉的亚稳态盆地（metastable basins）和反应路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统增强采样方法（enhanced sampling methods）需要预定义集体变量（collective variables），这要求预先了解反应坐标（reaction coordinates），限制了发现未预期的转变机制或中间体的能力。

Method: 该方法将原子系统中的局部信息熵（information entropy）作为通用集体变量，采用良好调温元动力学（well-tempered metadynamics）方法，使模拟偏向于熵变化的构型，从而平衡新颖性和热力学可及性。

Result: 该方法能够无监督地发现亚稳态盆地（metastable basins）和反应路径，包括传统序参数无法获取的竞争转变通道（competing transition channels）。在构象采样、均相成核、玻璃形成和固态相变等五个系统中验证了其通用性。

Conclusion: 局部信息熵作为通用集体变量，通过盲探索势能表面（potential energy surfaces），实现了对未预期转变机制和中间体的发现，突破了传统增强采样方法对预定义反应坐标的依赖。

Abstract: Enhanced sampling methods typically require predefined collective variables (CVs) that presuppose knowledge of reaction coordinates, restricting the discovery of unanticipated transition mechanisms or intermediates. Here, we show that a local measure of information entropy in atomistic systems is a general-purpose CV for rare event sampling across molecular and condensed-phase systems. The method biases simulations toward entropy-changing configurations following a well-tempered metadynamics approach, thus balancing novelty and thermodynamic accessibility. Blind exploration of potential energy surfaces enables unsupervised discovery of metastable basins and reaction pathways, including competing transition channels inaccessible to conventional order parameters. We demonstrate the generality of the method across five systems spanning conformational sampling, homogeneous nucleation, glass formation, and solid-state phase transformations.

### [23] [ORION: Unifying Top-Down and Bottom-Up Chemical Space Sampling for a Universal Organic Force Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05769)
*Zherui Chen,Jiayu Zhang,Yuxuan Tian,Zhoulin Liu,Sining Dai,Yanghui Li,Cong Chen,Dingyuan Tang,Yajun Deng,Qingxia Liu*

TL;DR: ORION是一种基于神经进化势（Neuroevolution Potential, NEP）框架开发的通用机器学习力场，适用于C、H、O、N、S、P系统，在保持计算效率的同时达到接近密度泛函理论（density functional theory）的精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经验力场（empirical force fields）在化学复杂凝聚相系统中的灵活性和可转移性有限，这阻碍了预测性建模的发展。因此需要开发兼具高精度和广泛适用性的通用机器学习力场。

Method: ORION在神经进化势框架内开发，采用综合自上而下（top-down）和自下而上（bottom-up）策略构建化学丰富的数据集进行训练，以增强在不同化学环境中的可转移性。

Result: ORION在测试集上预测原子力的精度显著高于ReaxFF，且在相同硬件条件下运行速度提高215.5倍。该模型能够平衡描述键断裂与形成、芳香环生长、氢键、范德华相互作用和π-堆积等过程。

Conclusion: ORION展示了在反应性和非反应性系统中的强大可转移性，为化学和材料科学中的预测性模拟提供了一个实用且通用的力场，并为开发兼具高精度和广泛适用性的通用机器学习力场提供了有效途径。

Abstract: Empirical force fields remain the primary tool for large-scale molecular simulation, yet their limited flexibility and transferability often hinder predictive modeling in chemically complex condensed-phase systems. Here we present ORION, a universal machine-learning force field for C, H, O, N, S, and P systems developed within the Neuroevolution Potential (NEP) framework. To enhance transferability across diverse chemical environments, ORION was trained on a chemically rich dataset constructed through an integrated top-down and bottom-up strategy, enabling accurate descriptions of complex organic configurations, reactive intermediates, and weak intermolecular interactions. ORION achieves near-density-functional-theory accuracy while retaining the efficiency required for large-scale molecular dynamics simulations. On the test set, it predicts atomic forces with substantially higher accuracy than ReaxFF while running 215.5 times faster under identical hardware conditions, making simulations on the hundreds-of-nanoseconds timescale readily accessible. The model provides a balanced description of bond breaking and formation, aromatic growth, hydrogen bonding, van der Waals interactions, and π-stacking, demonstrating strong transferability across both reactive and nonreactive systems. These results establish ORION as a practical and general force field for predictive simulations in chemistry and materials science, and provide an effective route toward universal machine-learning force fields with both high accuracy and broad applicability.

### [24] [Reference Energies for Non-Relativistic Core Ionization Potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05920)
*Antoine Marie,Loris Burth,Pierre-François Loos*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 该研究建立了基于理论的深度核心电离能（core ionization potentials）基准数据集，通过全组态相互作用（full configuration interaction）计算了84个非相对论值，为方法评估提供了化学精度的参考标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确预测核心电离能（core ionization potentials, IPs）是理论化学的挑战性任务，需要平衡处理轨道弛豫、电子关联和相对论效应。现有方法的评估通常依赖实验比较，其中多种误差来源（基组不完备性、相对论修正、振动效应）相互纠缠，难以分离关联处理的性能。

Method: 研究建立了基于理论的基准数据集，在核心-价电子分离近似（core-valence separation approximation）下，使用增强紧核心和弥散函数的大相关一致基组（aug-cc-pCVXZ），通过全组态相互作用（full configuration interaction）计算了84个非相对论值（73个第二行和11个第三行IPs）。

Result: 这些结果定义了固定有限基组内的理论最佳估计，为方法开发和验证提供了化学精度的参考。该数据集允许进行系统的理论间比较，能够分离关联和弛豫效应与其他物理贡献。

Conclusion: 基于该基准数据集，研究评估了广泛使用的近似方法性能，包括包含四重激发的运动方程耦合簇（equation-of-motion coupled-cluster）方法、单次G0W0方案（one-shot G0W0 scheme）以及态特定方法（state-specific methods）。

Abstract: Deep-lying core electrons carry highly localized, site-specific information that forms the basis of X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy. Accurately predicting their associated core ionization potentials (IPs) is a demanding theoretical task, requiring a balanced treatment of strong orbital relaxation, electron correlation, and relativistic effects. Over the years, a variety of approaches have been developed, ranging from state-specific wave function methods to linear-response formalisms and Green's function techniques. However, their assessment has often relied on comparisons with experiment, where multiple sources of error (basis set incompleteness, relativistic corrections, and vibrational effects) are entangled, making it difficult to isolate the performance of correlation treatments. In the present work, we establish a consistent, theory-based benchmark for core IPs by computing 84 non-relativistic values (73 second-row and 11 third-row IPs) at the full configuration interaction level within the core-valence separation approximation, using large correlation-consistent basis sets augmented with tight-core and diffuse functions (aug-cc-pCVXZ). These results define theoretical best estimates within a fixed finite basis set, providing a chemically accurate reference for method development and validation. Importantly, our dataset allows for systematic, theory-versus-theory comparisons that disentangle correlation and relaxation effects from other physical contributions. On this basis, we assess the performance of widely used approximate methods, including equation-of-motion coupled-cluster approaches up to the inclusion of quadruple excitations, the one-shot $G_0W_0$ scheme, as well as state-specific methods.

</details>


### [25] [The BOS-Lig Dataset: Accurate Ligand Charges from a Consensus Approach for 66,810 Experimentally Synthesized Ligands](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06043)
*Roland G. St. Michel,Ryan J. Jang,Aaron G. Garrison,Ilia Kevlishvili,Heather J. Kulik*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 该研究构建了波士顿开壳层配体（BOS-Lig）数据集，通过迭代电荷平衡工作流程为66,810个配体分配净电荷，并将配体与功能应用领域相关联，为计算筛选和数据驱动的配体设计提供基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 配体性质如净电荷（net charge）对于过渡金属配合物的计算高通量筛选至关重要，但这些信息在晶体学数据集中往往缺失或不一致。研究旨在构建一个实验基础的数据集，连接配体电荷与功能应用领域。

Method: 从剑桥结构数据库（Cambridge Structural Database）中提取126,985个单核过渡金属配合物，使用迭代电荷平衡工作流程（iterative charge-balancing workflow）结合配合物电荷、金属氧化态和晶体学观测共识，为配体分配净电荷。引入纯度指标（purity metric）识别可能错误的电荷分配，并通过主题建模工作流程（topic-modeling workflow）将配体与功能应用领域相关联。

Result: 成功构建了BOS-Lig数据集，包含94,581个独特配体结构，其中66,810个配体获得可靠的净电荷分配。将25,146个配体与反应性、氧化还原化学、生物化学和光物理化学等功能应用领域相关联。工作流程能够处理简单启发式方法（如八隅体规则）可能失败的情况。

Conclusion: 研究提供了一个实验基础的配体化学空间数据集，连接了电荷和功能应用信息，为计算筛选和数据驱动的配体设计奠定了重要基础。该数据集特别关注了配体的金属配位原子和变体情况（如半不稳定性）。

Abstract: Understanding ligand properties is essential for computational high-throughput screening of transition metal complexes. However, ligand properties such as net charge and other information such as their application area are often absent or inconsistently recorded in crystallographic datasets. Here, we construct a ligand dataset from 126,985 mononuclear transition metal complexes curated from the Cambridge Structural Database. Using an iterative charge-balancing workflow that combines complex charges, metal oxidation states, and consensus across crystallographic observations, we confidently assign net charges to 66,810 ligands among 94,581 identified unique ligand structures to curate the Boston Open-Shell Ligand (BOS-Lig) dataset. The workflow assigns ligand charges in homoleptic complexes first and then iteratively propagates these assignments across heteroleptic environments, allowing charges to be inferred even when direct charge information is unavailable. We analyze cases where simple heuristics such as the octet rule would have failed and introduce a purity metric to identify when our charge assignments may be incorrect. Each ligand is also classified in terms of its metal coordinating atoms and whether there are multiple variants (i.e., hemilability). We then link complexes to their associated journal abstracts and apply a topic-modeling workflow to link 25,146 ligands with functional application areas spanning reactivity, redox chemistry, biological chemistry, and photophysical chemistry. Together, we provide an experimentally grounded dataset of ligand chemical space that connects charge and functional application as a foundation for computational screening and data-driven ligand design.

</details>

### [26] [Mass generation in graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05494)
*Ioannis Kleftogiannis,Ilias Amanatidis*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种在图中产生质量激发（massive excitations）的机制，将顶点度（degree）视为标量场，并引入受量子场论中希格斯机制（Higgs mechanism）启发的耦合机制，从而产生无质量基态和有质量激发态，这些激发态可被视为在图中传播的涌现粒子（emergent particles）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索离散物理模型中物质结构涌现的可能性，特别是如何仅基于模型的基本连接性（connectivity）属性，在图中产生具有不同质量特性的类物质结构。

Method: 方法将图中每个顶点的邻居数量（度）视为标量场（scalar field），并引入受量子场论中希格斯机制启发的机制，通过图的关联矩阵（incident matrices）表示的边引入类矢量场（vector-like field），将这两个场耦合（coupling）。研究分析了图的大小及其密度（边与顶点之比）对质量隙（mass gap）和激发态局域化性质的影响。

Result: 耦合产生了无质量基态（massless ground state）和有质量激发态，两者由质量隙分隔。最重的涌现粒子对应质量最大的激发态，局域在高密度区域（即度大的顶点）；最轻的粒子对应质量最小的激发态，局域在少数但度较小的顶点；中等质量的激发态局域性较弱，分布在更多顶点上。

Conclusion: 研究表明，在离散物理模型中，仅依靠模型连接性等少数基本属性，就可能涌现出具有不同质量特性的类物质结构（matter-like structures）。

Abstract: We demonstrate a mechanism for the production of massive excitations in graphs. We treat the number of neighbors at each vertex in the graph (degree) as a scalar field. Then we introduce a mechanism inspired by the Higgs mechanism in quantum field theory(QFT), that couples the degree field to a vector-like field, introduced via the graph edges, represented mathematically by the incident matrices of the graph. The coupling between the two fields produces a massless ground state and massive excitations, separated by a mass gap. The excitations can be treated as emergent massive particles, propagating inside the graph. We study how the size of the graph and its density, represented by the ratio of edges over vertices, affects the mass gap and the localization properties of the massive excitations. We show that the most massive excitations, corresponding to the heaviest emergent particles, localize on regions of the graph with high density, consisting of vertices with a large degree. On the other hand, the least massive excitations, corresponding to the lightest emergent particles localize on a few vertices but with a smaller degree. Excitations with intermediate masses are less localized, spreading on more vertices instead. Our study shows that emergence of matter-like structures with various mass properties, is possible in discrete physical models, relying only on a few fundamental properties like the connectivity of the models.

</details>

### [27] [Introduction to Mechanics and Structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05810)
*Martina Scapin*

Main category: physics.acc-ph

TL;DR: 该工作全面概述了连续介质力学（continuum mechanics）的基本概念，重点分析材料在机械载荷下的行为，包括弹塑性理论及其在压力容器和薄壁轴对称壳体设计中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该工作的动机是系统阐述连续介质力学的基本原理，特别是材料在机械载荷下的弹塑性行为，以及这些理论在压力容器和薄壁轴对称壳体设计中的实际应用。

Method: 采用连续介质力学理论框架，通过胡克定律（Hooke's law）和本构矩阵分析弹性行为，利用屈服面（yield surfaces）、流动法则（flow rules）和硬化定律（hardening laws）处理塑性行为。对于壳体分析，基于壳体理论（shell theory），假设薄壁和轴对称几何，将应力分布简化为薄膜应力（membrane stresses）。

Result: 建立了弹塑性行为的完整理论描述，区分了弹性与塑性的原子起源和宏观表现。针对压力容器和薄壁轴对称壳体，分析了其在内外压力下的力学行为，包括外部压力下的屈曲现象（buckling phenomena）、几何不连续处的二次应力，并参考了EN 13445标准的设计规定。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了连续介质力学基本概念的全面概述，建立了从材料弹塑性行为到工程结构（特别是压力容器和薄壁轴对称壳体）设计的完整理论框架，为相关工程应用提供了理论基础和设计指导。

Abstract: This work provides a comprehensive overview of the fundamental concepts in continuum mechanics, focusing on the behaviour of materials under mechanical loads. It discusses the distinction between elastic and plastic, highlighting their atomic origins and macroscopic implications. Elastic behaviour is examined via Hooke's law and constitutive matrices, while plasticity is treated through yield surfaces, flow rules, and hardening laws, including isotropic and kinematic hardening. In addition, the theoretical foundations and design principles of pressure vessels and thin axisymmetric shells, focusing on their mechanical behaviour under internal or external pressure, is discussed. The analysis is based on shell theory, assuming thin walls and axisymmetric geometry, which simplifies the stress distribution into membrane stresses. The work also addresses buckling phenomena under external pressure, secondary stresses at geometric discontinuities, and design provisions from the EN 13445 standard.

</details>

### [28] [Observation of nuclear suppression in coherent $Υ$(1S) photoproduction off heavy nuclei at the LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05814)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 首次测量了铅-铅超外围碰撞中相干Υ(1S)介子的光生过程，在μ²=22.4 GeV²尺度下观测到核抑制效应，核胶子抑制因子R_g^Pb为0.55±0.14。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在通过测量重核上相干Υ(1S)介子的光生过程，探测核胶子结构。由于Υ(1S)质量较大，该测量达到了相干矢量介子光生过程迄今可及的最高尺度，预期非线性量子色动力学效应最小化。

Method: 利用CMS实验收集的5.02 TeV核子-核子质心能量下的超外围铅-铅碰撞数据，测量相干Υ(1S)介子的光生截面。该过程在核子动量分数x∼10⁻³处探测核胶子结构。

Result: 在|y|<1的Υ(1S)快度范围内，测得的光生截面与忽略核效应的基线模型预测之比为S_Υ(1S)=0.25±0.08，表明该过程中存在核抑制。核胶子抑制因子R_g^Pb(x≈10⁻³, μ²=22.4 GeV²)=0.55±0.14。

Conclusion: 尽管探测尺度μ²相差约两个数量级，测得的R_g^Pb值仅略大于先前相干φ光生过程报告的值，这为核胶子结构在不同尺度下的行为提供了重要约束。

Abstract: The first measurement of coherent $Υ$(1S) meson photoproduction off heavy nuclei is performed using ultraperipheral lead-lead collisions collected by the CMS experiment at a nucleon-nucleon center-of-mass energy of 5.02 TeV. The nuclear gluonic structure is probed at a nucleon momentum fraction of order $x$ $\sim$ 10$^{-3}$, determined by the kinematics of the process. Owing to the large $Υ$(1S) mass, the measurement reaches the highest scale accessible so far through coherent vector-meson photoproduction, $μ^2$ = 22.4 GeV$^2$, where nonlinear quantum chromodynamics effects are expected to be minimal. In the $Υ$(1S) rapidity range $\lvert y\rvert$ $\lt$ 1, the ratio of the measured photoproduction cross section to a baseline model prediction that neglects nuclear effects is $S_{Υ\text{(1S)}}$ = 0.25 $\pm$ 0.06 (stat) $\pm$ 0.02 (syst), thereby demonstrating nuclear suppression in this process. Expressed in terms of a nuclear gluon suppression factor, the result yields $R_\text{g}^\text{Pb}$($x$ $\approx$ 10$^{-3}$, $μ^2$ = 22.4 GeV$^2$) = 0.55 $\pm$ 0.12 (stat) $\pm$ 0.02 (syst). The measured $R_\text{g}^\text{Pb}$ is only slightly larger than the values previously reported for coherent $φ$ photoproduction, despite the probed $μ^2$ differing by approximately two orders of magnitude.

### [29] [Feynman integral reduction with intersection theory made simple](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05025)
*Li-Hong Huang,Yan-Qing Ma,Ziwen Wang,Li Lin Yang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 基于分支表示（branch representation）的费曼积分约化方法，将任意外腿数的L圈费曼积分约化所需变量数降至最多(3L-3)个，相比传统方法显著简化了计算复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于相交理论（intersection theory）的费曼积分约化方法虽提供了传统分部积分（integration-by-parts）的替代方案，但其实际应用受限于计算所需的大量变量。特别是对于多外腿积分，传统方法中变量数随传播子总数增长，导致计算复杂度高。

Method: 采用最近引入的分支表示（branch representation），实现了L圈费曼积分的约化计算。该方法将任意外腿数积分的约化问题转化为最多仅需(3L-3)个变量的相交数计算，显著减少了所需变量维度。

Result: 通过具体计算两圈图例验证了所提方法的有效性。相比传统相交理论方法和标准分部积分约化技术，该方法在计算效率上实现了显著提升，特别是在多外腿积分场景下优势明显。

Conclusion: 基于分支表示的费曼积分约化方法通过将变量需求降至(3L-3)个，为多外腿费曼积分的计算提供了实质性简化，在计算效率上优于现有方法。

Abstract: Feynman integral reduction based on intersection theory provides an alternative to the traditional integration-by-parts method, yet its practical application has been constrained by the large number of variables required in the computation. In this Letter, we demonstrate that by employing the recently introduced branch representation, the reduction of $L$-loop Feynman integrals with an arbitrary number of external legs can be achieved through the computation of at most $(3L-3)$-variable intersection numbers. This constitutes a significant simplification compared to existing approaches, particularly for multi-leg integrals where the number of variables in conventional methods scales with the total number of propagators. We validate the proposed method through explicit calculations of two-loop diagrams, demonstrating substantial improvements in computational efficiency relative to both traditional intersection-theory approaches and standard integration-by-parts reduction techniques.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究AdS₃中热场的量子反作用几何构造，通过膜构造方法将四维体理论与三维膜上的半经典有效理论联系起来。

Abstract: We construct geometries describing the quantum backreaction of thermal fields in AdS$_3$. The solutions are obtained from branes in a four-dimensional AdS C-metric. They can be viewed as solutions of the semiclassical effective theory on the brane, which couples three-dimensional gravity to the CFT dual to the four-dimensional bulk. This brane construction is related by a double analytic continuation to earlier studies of quantum BTZ solutions. There are two families of solutions, labelled by the asymptotic mass. Solutions with negative mass correspond to the back-reaction of a thermal CFT state on global AdS$_3$. Solutions with positive mass have a horizon for zero back-reaction, which is replaced by a smooth origin in the back-reacted solution. We study the thermodynamics and first law on the brane, which we argue is realised in a two-brane setup where we include both the quantum BTZ brane and our quantum soliton brane.

### [31] [Worldline Images for Yang-Mills Theory within Boundaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05082)
*Santiago Christiansen Murguizur,Lucas Manzo,Pablo Pisani*

Main category: hep-th

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开发了一种基于镜像法的世界线技术，该方法能够处理具有边界的流形上的场论问题。分析中同时考虑了矢量场和鬼场，并针对相对或绝对边界条件进行了专门处理。

Result: 作为方法验证，计算了热核渐近的前三个Seeley-DeWitt系数。进一步应用该技术，计算了边界存在时色电场背景下的胶子产生率，展示了该方法在具体物理问题中的应用能力。

Conclusion: 本文成功开发了适用于有边界流形上杨-米尔斯理论的世界线技术，该技术基于镜像法构建，能够处理相对或绝对边界条件，并已通过计算Seeley-DeWitt系数得到验证，最终应用于胶子产生率的计算。

Abstract: In this article we develop a worldline technique based on the method of images to study the effective action associated to Yang-Mills theories on manifolds with boundaries. We consider the possibility of having either relative or absolute boundary conditions, which are particular types of mixed boundary conditions. Both vector fields and ghost fields are taken into account in this analysis. As a check of our construction, we compute the first three Seeley-DeWitt coefficients of the heat kernel asymptotics. Finally, we employ our technique to calculate the rate of gluon production due to a chromoelectric field background in the presence of a boundary.

### [32] [Weak-Field Limits of Black Hole Metrics from the KMOC formalism: Schwarzschild, Kerr, Reissner-Nordström, and Kerr-Newman](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05094)
*Jacobo Hernández C*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: KMOC形式主义（Kosower-Maybee-O'Connell formalism）建立了量子散射振幅与引力系统中经典可观测量之间的桥梁。该研究展示了如何在该框架内重现四种经典黑洞度规（Schwarzschild、Kerr、Reissner-Nordstrom和Kerr-Newman）的弱场极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索KMOC形式主义在连接量子散射振幅与经典引力系统方面的应用潜力。具体目标是验证该形式主义能否重现四种经典黑洞度规的弱场极限，特别是关注引力与电磁相互作用的干涉效应。

Method: 方法基于KMOC形式主义，从具有指数自旋结构（exponential spin structure）的三点振幅出发，计算四点散射振幅并通过KMOC公式提取动量冲量（momentum impulse）。通过将这些结果与一般度规中的测地线运动（geodesic motion）匹配，重构了度规分量在G、a和Q²的领头阶展开。

Result: 成功重现了四种黑洞度规的弱场极限，包括Schwarzschild、Kerr、Reissner-Nordstrom和Kerr-Newman度规。在Kerr-Newman情况下，引力与电磁相互作用的干涉项产生了g_{tφ}中Q²a/r³的贡献，该贡献在单独的Kerr或Reissner-Nordstrom弱场极限中不出现。结果与arXiv:1907.00431和arXiv:1908.04342中的研究一致。

Conclusion: KMOC形式主义能够有效重现经典黑洞度规的弱场展开，但需要强调的是，该方法仅能复现弱场展开而非完整的非线性解。研究验证了该形式主义在连接量子振幅与经典引力物理方面的有效性，特别是在处理引力与电磁相互作用干涉效应方面的能力。

Abstract: The KMOC (Kosower-Maybee-O'Connell) formalism establishes a bridge between quantum scattering amplitudes and classical observables in gravitational systems. In this work, we show how the weak-field limits of the four classical black hole metrics - Schwarzschild, Kerr, Reissner-Nordstrom, and Kerr-Newman - can be reproduced within this formalism. Starting from three-point amplitudes with exponential spin structure for both gravitational and electromagnetic interactions, we compute four-point scattering amplitudes and extract the momentum impulse via the KMOC formula. Matching these results with geodesic motion in a general metric allows us to reconstruct the metric components to leading order in G, a, and Q^2. For the Kerr-Newman case, we include interference terms between gravitational and electromagnetic interactions, which produce a Q^2 a/r^3 contribution to g_{tφ} that does not appear in the Kerr or Reissner-Nordstrom weak-field limits separately. Our results are consistent with those of arXiv:1907.00431 [hep-th], where the Kerr-Newman metric is derived from minimal coupling amplitudes using the KMOC formalism arXiv:1908.04342 [hep-th]. All results are verified through their consistency with the well-known full metrics, though we emphasize that the KMOC formalism as applied here reproduces only the weak-field expansions, not the complete non-linear solutions.

</details>


### [33] [Untwisting the double copy: the zeroth copy as an optical seed](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05103)
*Damien A. Easson,Michael J. Falato*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文为平坦背景下的稳态Kerr-Schild时空提供了一个历史光学基础，并在现代双重拷贝（double-copy）语言中进行解释。研究表明，由Kerr-Schild共形（congruence）的膨胀和带符号扭转构建的复光学种子（complex optical seed）是调和的，其逆服从程函方程（eikonal equation）并代数重构共形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于为稳态真空Kerr-Schild时空提供一个历史光学基础，并将其置于现代双重拷贝框架中进行解释。这旨在展示单个复种子如何构建共形、组织相关时空和规范场，并编码零拷贝（zeroth copy）的几何内容。

Method: 方法基于构建一个复光学种子ρ = -θ - iω，该种子由Kerr-Schild共形的膨胀（expansion）θ和带符号扭转（signed twist）ω组成。该种子是调和的，其逆服从程函方程，并代数重构共形。在稳态Kerr-Schild和Petrov类型-D Weyl双重拷贝框架的重叠部分，该种子提供了零拷贝数据的归一化代表。

Result: 结果表明，局部稳态几何由单个复种子组织。该种子的实部产生Kerr-Schild轮廓（profile），其梯度生成单拷贝（single-copy）规范场强度。构造提供了时空实现，展示了单个复种子如何构建共形、组织相关时空和规范场，并编码零拷贝的几何内容，且无需借助扭量（twistor）方法。

Conclusion: 结论是，该研究为平坦背景下的稳态Kerr-Schild时空提供了一个历史光学基础，并在双重拷贝语言中进行了现代解释。构造展示了单个复光学种子如何统一组织几何结构，为理解Kerr-Schild时空与双重拷贝框架之间的关系提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We present a historical optical foundation for stationary vacuum Kerr--Schild spacetimes on a flat background and interpret it in modern double-copy language. In this setting, a complex optical seed \(ρ=-θ-iω\), built from the expansion and signed twist of the Kerr--Schild congruence, is harmonic, while its inverse obeys an eikonal equation and reconstructs the congruence algebraically. Thus the local stationary geometry is organized by a single complex seed. In the overlap of the stationary Kerr--Schild and Petrov type--D Weyl double-copy framework, this seed furnishes a normalized representative of the zeroth-copy data, while its real part yields the Kerr--Schild profile and its gradient generates the single-copy gauge-field strength. The construction provides, without recourse to twistor methods, a spacetime realization of how a single complex seed builds the congruence, organizes the associated spacetime and gauge fields, and encodes the geometric content of the zeroth copy.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 结果表明，这种重新表述为整个超引力家族提供了统一描述，阐明了正射线欧拉积分（positive-ray Euler integral）与早期轮廓表示之间的关系，并通过相交理论（intersection theory）再现了相同的约化规则。该表述还使具有四和六个超对称的特殊情况特别透明，并为低偶理论产生了简单的埃尔米特多项式构造。

Abstract: We study the double-logarithmic four-graviton Regge sector in $N$-extended supergravity. Its Mellin-space solution is already known in terms of parabolic-cylinder functions. We show that the same answer can be organized as a rank-two twisted period system, meaning that two closely related weighted integrals determine the full Mellin partial wave. These functions satisfy a simple pair of first-order differential equations and a recursion as the number of supersymmetries $N$ changes. This gives a uniform description of the full supergravity family, clarifies the relation between the positive-ray Euler integral and the earlier contour representation, and reproduces the same reduction rule through intersection theory. The reformulation also makes the special cases with four and six supersymmetries particularly transparent and yields a simple Hermite-polynomial construction for the low-even theories.

Abstract: We report a physical origin of tensionless strings, obtained by formulating string dynamics in finite-lifetime settings for the first time. ### [36] [Residual Symmetries and Their Algebras in the Kerr-Schild Double Copy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05262)
*B. P. Holton*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: Kerr-Schild双拷贝（KSDC）在杨-米尔斯理论与引力理论间建立了经典解对应，但该对应并未提供规范理论与引力理论底层对称性结构间的映射关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探究Kerr-Schild双拷贝对应是否能够提供规范理论与引力理论底层对称性结构间的映射关系，这是当前双拷贝研究中尚未充分发展的领域。

Method: 通过分析Kerr-Schild ansatz在杨-米尔斯理论和引力理论中的剩余对称性结构，并构造Weyl补偿的BRST复形来研究对称性的物理意义。

Result: 规范理论侧剩余对称性形成沿零方向的无限维函数代数，而引力侧剩余微分同胚生成S^2上的共形代数。共形Killing矢量（CKV）部分在渐近平坦性和视界正则性条件下产生无限维代数，但通过BRST复形分析表明CKV部分是BRST-精确的。

Conclusion: KSDC在ansatz层面引入了扩大的对称性结构，但经过上同调约化后仅保留物理对称性，揭示了杨-米尔斯理论与引力理论在剩余对称性层面的根本性不匹配。

Abstract: The Kerr-Schild double copy (KSDC) is well-known for relating exact classical solutions between Yang-Mills theory and theories of gravity. However, whether this correspondence provides a more fundamental mapping between the underlying symmetries of gauge theory and gravity remains an underdeveloped area of research in the contemporary double copy program. In this paper, we demonstrate that the KSDC correspondence does not provide a mapping between the residual symmetry structures of the Kerr-Schild ansatz in Yang-Mills theory and gravity. On the gauge theory side, residual symmetries form an infinite-dimensional algebra of functions along null directions. On the gravitational side, residual diffeomorphisms preserving the Kerr-Schild form of the Schwarzschild metric generate a conformal algebra on $S^2$, which decomposes into Killing vectors and proper conformal Killing vectors (CKVs). While the Killing sector reproduces the expected global isometries, the CKV sector yields an infinite-dimensional algebra after imposing asymptotic flatness and horizon regularity. This appears to contradict the fact that the Schwarzschild solution admits no proper conformal symmetries. We resolve this apparent contradiction by constructing a Weyl-compensated BRST complex, showing that the CKV sector is BRST-exact and therefore trivial in cohomology, so that the physical symmetry algebra reduces to the global isometries of Schwarzschild. This demonstrates that the KSDC introduces an enlarged symmetry structure at the level of the ansatz, but preserves physical symmetries after a cohomological reduction, revealing a fundamental mismatch between Yang-Mills and gravity at the level of residual symmetries.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 单拷贝规范场与全息坐标无关，在弯曲背景上满足无源麦克斯韦方程，类似于Schwarzschild双重拷贝中的库仑场。零拷贝标量满足包含额外维度一阶导数项的修正Klein-Gordon方程，通过场重定义可化为具有有效质量$m^2 = 12/l^2$的标准Klein-Gordon方程。替代Kerr-Schild分裂产生物理不等价的双重拷贝。

Abstract: We construct the Kerr-Schild classical double copy of the black string in the Randall-Sundrum II model, deriving the single and zeroth copies, and verifying the associated field equations. The single copy gauge field is independent of the holographic coordinate and satisfies a sourceless Maxwell equation on the curved background, in direct analogy with the Coulomb field of the Schwarzschild double copy. The zeroth copy scalar obeys a modified Klein-Gordon equation with a first-order derivative term along the extra dimension; a field redefinition yields a standard Klein-Gordon equation with effective mass $m^2 = 12/l^2$, induced by the warp factor. We further show that an alternative Kerr-Schild splitting, gravitationally equivalent to the canonical one, produces a physically inequivalent double copy: the gauge field is supported by a conserved but delocalized bulk current, and the zeroth copy satisfies a massless equation that carries no imprint of the warped extra dimension.

### [38] [Phase Transitions in Primary Hair Planar Black Holes and Solitons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05538)

Abstract: We present a new family of Ricci-flat black hole and soliton solutions with primary scalar hair in asymptotically anti-de Sitter (AdS) space in $D$ dimensions. By solving the coupled Einstein-scalar field equations, we obtain analytic planar hairy black hole and soliton geometries. In these solutions, the scalar field and curvature scalars remain regular everywhere. We also derive analytic expressions for the mass and free energy, which indicate that the hairy soliton represents the ground state of the system. We further analyze the phase transitions between the hairy black hole and the hairy soliton, and find that there exists a first-order phase transition between them, with the transition point controlled by the ratio of the periods of Euclidean time and compact spacelike cycle. We further analyze how the scalar hair affects the transition temperature, and find that the temperature window in which the soliton phase remains preferred expands as the hair parameter increases. The hairy soliton solution obtained here is partly motivated by holographic QCD and may provide a useful gravitational background for modeling the confined phase of QCD from a bottom-up holographic perspective.

Abstract: The symmetry-resolved Krylov complexity is a useful tool in studying chaotic properties of systems that are endowed with symmetries. We investigate the conditions under which an invariant operator would have the symmetry-resolved Krylov complexity in a charge subspace identical to the Krylov complexity of the full operator. Further, we study the Krylov complexity of the Uncoloured Tensor Model, a disorder-free kin of the SYK Model which has a plethora of symmetries. We find charge subspaces of the same operator in which the equipartition holds as well as where it doesn't. We also find that within the computational limits, the Krylov complexity averaged over the symmetry subspace is bounded above by that of the operator in the full space.

### [40] [Causal Dynamical Triangulations: New Lattice Theory of Quantum Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05641)
*J. Ambjørn,R. Loll*

Main category: hep-th

Abstract: Causal Dynamical Triangulations (CDT) is a methodology to define and compute the gravitational path integral, whose aim is a fully fledged nonperturbative quantum field theory of gravity and spacetime. Analogous to lattice formulations of nongravitational quantum fields, CDT provides a blueprint for lattice quantum gravity, where - crucially - the dynamical, curved and causal nature of spacetime is built into the structure of the lattices from the outset. The regularized path integral involves a sum over triangulated spacetimes, each assembled from flat, Minkowskian building blocks. The degrees of freedom of general relativity are encoded in a coordinate-free manner in the neighbourhood relations of the building blocks and the length of their edges, which also serves as a short-distance cutoff.
  A well-defined Wick rotation makes this path integral amenable to Monte Carlo simulations. Despite the absence of an a priori preferred background geometry, numerical experiments have revealed the dynamical emergence of a quantum universe near the Planck scale. Its global properties are compatible with those of a de Sitter space, providing strong evidence for a well-defined classical limit. At the same time, large quantum fluctuations lead to unexpected properties on short scales, most prominently, a spectral dimension near 2, replacing the classical value of 4. Computer simulations indicate the presence of an ultraviolet fixed point under renormalization, opening the door to a nontrivial continuum theory. Efforts are under way to construct observables that can elucidate the nonperturbative quantum origins of early-universe cosmology.

*Jun-ichi Sakamoto,Shinya Tomizawa*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究了五维U(1)^3超引力中极值稳态双轴对称黑洞解的Breitenlohner-Maison线性系统生成技术，分析了基于Gibbons-Hawking基的多中心构型，包括BPS和almost-BPS解，并建立了SO(4,4)对偶变换的统一框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于发展基于Breitenlohner-Maison线性系统的解生成技术，以统一处理五维U(1)^3超引力中的极值稳态双轴对称黑洞解，特别是多中心构型如旋转单中心黑洞和双中心黑环（black ring）。

Method: 方法包括将系统维度约化（dimensional reduction）到三维，描述为具有目标空间SO(4,4)/[SO(2,2)×SO(2,2)]的coset sigma模型，其中解由coset矩阵和monodromy矩阵编码；对Bena-Warner BPS解构造了由幂零元（nilpotent elements）支配的指数表示。

Result: 结果显示BPS解的monodromy矩阵通常呈现双极点（double poles），但可利用𝔰𝔬(4,4)的幂零代数显式分解以重构解；将方法扩展到almost-BPS解，发现单中心情况具有交换剩余（commuting residues），而双中心黑环则产生更复杂的结构，包含三阶极点（third-order pole），在施加正则性条件时消失。

Conclusion: 结论表明Breitenlohner-Maison形式主义可作为极值多中心黑洞的统一框架，分析了Rasheed-Larsen解的极值极限，其中快旋转分支由幂等元（idempotent elements）支配，并构造了将慢旋转分支与单中心almost-BPS解相关联的显式SO(4,4)对偶变换（duality transformation）。

Abstract: We study solution-generating techniques based on the Breitenlohner--Maison linear system for extremal, stationary biaxisymmetric black hole solutions in five-dimensional $U(1)^3$ supergravity. Focusing on multi-center configurations over a Gibbons--Hawking base, we analyze both BPS and almost-BPS solutions, including rotating single-center black holes and two-center black rings. After dimensional reduction to three dimensions, the system is described by a coset sigma model with target space $SO(4,4)/[SO(2,2)\times SO(2,2)]$, where solutions are encoded in coset and monodromy matrices. For Bena--Warner BPS solutions, we construct the coset and monodromy matrices and show that they admit an exponential representation governed by nilpotent elements. Although the monodromy matrices generically exhibit double poles, they can be factorized explicitly using the nilpotent algebra of $\mathfrak{so}(4,4)$, reconstructing the solutions. We extend this to almost-BPS solutions and derive the corresponding matrices. While the single-center case exhibits commuting residues, the two-center black ring leads to a more intricate structure with a third-order pole, which disappears when regularity is imposed. Finally, we analyze the extremal limits of the Rasheed--Larsen solution, where the fast-rotating branch is governed by idempotent elements. We also construct an explicit $SO(4,4)$ duality transformation relating the slowly-rotating branch to a single-center almost-BPS solution. These results will provide the BM formalism as a unified framework for extremal multi-center black holes.

</details>

*Raúl Arias,Agustín Tamis*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明纠缠容量（capacity of entanglement）能够在受控因子化岛分支中探测到超出冯·诺依曼熵（von Neumann entropy）的副本结构信息，为岛物理提供了超越n=1极限的新观测视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞岛（black hole islands）通常通过冯·诺依曼熵来诊断，但完整的副本鞍点（replica saddle）包含比n→1极限更多的信息。本文旨在探索如何探测这些额外结构。

Method: 在JT引力（JT gravity）耦合大c浴场（large-c bath）的受控因子化岛分支（controlled factorized island branch）中，研究纠缠容量在晚期高温区域（late-time high-temperature regime）的行为。

Result: 在晚期高温区域，熵平台（entropy plateau）在一阶非平凡修正中保持不变，而纠缠容量获得确定的修正。这表明即使在熵本身看似刚性的情况下，邻近副本数据仍具有物理意义。

Conclusion: 因子化岛鞍点已携带超越熵的有限n信息，纠缠容量是揭示这些信息的自然可观测量。岛物理的物理内容不限于n=1极限，周围副本几何包含关于半经典鞍点如何组装的额外可观测信息。

Abstract: Black hole islands are usually diagnosed through the von Neumann entropy, but the full replica saddle contains more information than survives in the limit $n \to 1$. In this paper we show that the capacity of entanglement can detect that extra structure already within the controlled factorized island branch of JT gravity coupled to a large-$c$ bath. In the late-time high-temperature regime, the entropy plateau remains unchanged at the first nontrivial order, while the capacity acquires a definite correction. This provides a sharp semiclassical example in which nearby replica data are physically meaningful even when the entropy itself appears rigid. Our result shows that the factorized island saddle already carries finite-$n$ information beyond the entropy, and that the capacity is a natural observable for exposing it. More broadly, it highlights that the physics of island saddles is not exhausted by the $n=1$ limit: the surrounding replica geometry can contain additional, and observable, information about how the semiclassical saddle is assembled.

### [44] [Exact WKB analysis of inverted triple-well: resonance, PT-symmetry breaking, and resurgence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05878)
*Syo Kamata,Tatsuhiro Misumi,Cihan Pazarbaşı,Hidetoshi Taya*

TL;DR: 本文在精确WKB框架下研究倒置三势阱的非厄米量子力学，通过识别不同Siegert边界条件对应的三种量子系统（PT对称、共振和反共振），推导精确量子化条件并构建跨级数解，阐明谱的实复性质与物理特性关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
