Method: 采用精确WKB（Wentzel-Kramers-Brillouin）方法，推导三种系统的精确量子化条件，构建跨级数解，识别重整化群结构，并通过中位数求和（median-summed）技术分析谱的性质。

Result: 发现PT对称系统存在对称性破缺，其例外点（exceptional point）表现为反弹（bounce）和双离子（bion）作用的简单代数关系；共振与反共振系统的谱互为复共轭，必然为复数且无例外点，但共享相同的最小跨级数。

Conclusion: 通过保持与路径积分鞍点及重整化群形式理论的明确联系，该分析为非厄米理论的量子化提供了统一且普遍的视角，阐明了非厄米系统中反弹和双离子构型的作用。

Abstract: We study non-Hermitian quantum mechanics of an inverted triple-well potential within the exact WKB framework. For a single classical potential, different Siegert boundary conditions define three distinct quantum problems: the PT-symmetric, resonance, and anti-resonance systems. For each case, we derive the exact quantization condition and construct the associated trans-series solution. By identifying the resurgent structures and cancellations in these non-Hermitian setups, we obtain the median-summed series, clarifying when the spectra are real or complex in accordance with the physical properties of each system. Establishing explicit links to the semi-classical path integral formalism, we elucidate the roles of bounce and bion configurations in these non-Hermitian systems. This analysis predicts PT-symmetry breaking, which we also verify numerically. Using the median quantization conditions, we prove the existence of this symmetry breaking and establish an exact equation for the exceptional point, which emerges as a remarkably simple algebraic relation between the bounce and bion actions. We further show that the median-summed non-perturbative correction to the spectrum vanishes at the exceptional point, while the resurgent structure survives through a universal minimal trans-series. For the resonance and anti-resonance systems, we find that the exact median-summed spectra are related by complex conjugation, representing time reversal in this setting, are necessarily complex, and do not exhibit an exceptional point. Although their spectra differ significantly from the PT-symmetric case, they share the same minimal trans-series. By maintaining explicit links with the path integral saddles and the formal theory of resurgence, our analysis provides a unified and general perspective on the quantization of non-Hermitian theories.

### [45] [Edge modes in Chern-Simons theory on a strip](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05889)
*Erica Bertolini,Michael Doyle,Nicola Maggiore,Conor Murphy,Carlotta Piras*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在条带几何上推导出与Symanzik意义下的幂次计数一致的最一般局部边界条件，通过破坏的规范Ward恒等式将体运动方程与边界自由度联系起来，得到具有相反中心荷的边界Kac-Moody流代数。

Result: 相应的二维边界作用是Tomonaga-Luttinger类型，描述沿两个边界相反方向传播的手性玻色子；一致性条件（全息式体-边界匹配）将陈-西蒙斯耦合常数和边界参数与物理边缘速度联系起来。

Conclusion: 该分析为具有两个边界的陈-西蒙斯理论提供了完整的体-边界对应场论实现，对称设置中两个速度的相等和相反符号直接源于边界结构而非模型依赖的约束势假设，且速度与条带宽度无关。

Abstract: We investigate abelian Chern-Simons gauge theory on a strip geometry with two spatial boundaries. In the presence of boundaries, gauge invariance is broken by boundary conditions, leading to physical edge excitations. By deriving the most general local boundary conditions consistent with power counting in the sense of Symanzik, we show that the bulk equations of motion determine the boundary degrees of freedom through a broken gauge Ward identity, yielding boundary Kac-Moody current algebras with opposite central charges on the two edges. The corresponding two-dimensional boundary actions are of Tomonaga-Luttinger type and describe chiral bosons propagating in opposite directions along the two boundaries. A consistency condition, interpreted as a holographic-like bulk-boundary matching, relates the Chern-Simons coupling constant and the boundary parameters to the physical edge velocities. Within this framework, the equality and opposite sign of the two velocities in a symmetric setup follow directly from the boundary structure rather than from model-dependent assumptions about confining potentials, and the velocities are independent of the strip width. Our analysis provides a fully field-theoretic realization of bulk-boundary correspondence in Chern-Simons theory with two boundaries, with direct applications to edge physics in quantum Hall systems and related topological/hydrodynamic settings.

### [46] [Geodesics from Quantum Field Theory: A Case Study in AdS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05901)
*Vaibhav Burman,Chethan Krishnan,Livesh Parajuli*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究在AdS₃时空中精确实现了量子场论单粒子态的局域化与测地线运动，提出了两种具体方案：基于应力张量期望值的协变质心轨迹，以及基于Klein-Gordon内积的位置算符。研究验证了在适当半经典极限下，自由标量场波包遵循预期的类时和类光测地线运动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子场论中的局域单粒子态在适当半经典极限下应表现出测地线运动，这一预期常被启发式引用但缺乏精确实现。本研究旨在发展两种精确方案，并在AdS₃时空中进行详细测试，以建立量子场论与经典广义相对论中测地线运动之间的严格对应。

Method: 首先，从应力张量算符的期望值定义协变"质心"轨迹，仅利用∇_μ⟨T^{μν}⟩=0证明在单极子近似下该轨迹满足一般时空中的测地线方程。其次，基于Klein-Gordon内积和模完备性构造位置算符，计算其在单粒子波包态中的期望值。最后在空AdS₃中构建具有可调能量和角动量的自由标量场显式正规化波包。

Result: 两种方案均能精确再现预期的径向、圆形和类椭圆类时及类光测地线，通过解析和数值计算验证了波包轨迹与经典测地线的一致性。研究还分离出波包轨迹从类时到类光测地线行为的受控交叉超相对论区域，并确定了局域化测地线解释失效的精确极限。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了量子场论-弯曲时空背景下经典Mathisson-Papapetrou-Dixon框架的推广，建立了量子波包与经典测地线之间的精确对应。在CFT方面，研究表明体局域化（特别是径向数据）由态在双原初算符的全局后代上的分布所捕获。

Abstract: Localized one-particle states of a quantum field theory--whether in flat space or on a curved background--are expected to exhibit geodesic motion in an appropriate semiclassical regime. This expectation is often invoked heuristically: in this work we develop two precise implementations and test them in detail in global AdS$_3$. First, we define a covariant ''center-of-mass'' trajectory from the expectation value of the stress tensor operator and show, using only $\nabla_μ\langle T^{μν}\rangle=0$, that it obeys the geodesic equation in the monopole (sufficiently localized) approximation in a general spacetime. This provides a QFT-in-curved-spacetime generalization of the Mathisson-Papapetrou-Dixon framework in classical general relativity. Second, we construct position operators from the Klein--Gordon inner product and mode completeness, and compute their expectation values in generic single-particle wave packet states. We then build explicit normalizable wave packets of a free scalar field in empty AdS$_3$ with tunable energy and angular momentum, and demonstrate analytically and numerically that both prescriptions reproduce the expected radial, circular, and elliptical-like timelike and null geodesics. Our discussion also isolates a natural ultra-relativistic regime in which the wave packet trajectory exhibits a controlled crossover from timelike to null geodesic behavior. We identify precise limits where the localized geodesic interpretation of the wave packet breaks down. On the CFT side, we show that bulk localization--specifically the radial data--is captured by how the state is distributed over global descendants of the dual primary.

Our result has special significance since order $λ^{5/2}$ is the highest order calculation that can be done with perturbation theory, because there are nonperturbative effects associated with the magnetic mass scale that come into play at order $λ^3$. Motivation: 当前计算规范不变量和规范参数无关量（如有效势、反常维度、重整化群方程）的方法通常需要依赖传统费曼图计算作为补充输入。本文旨在开发一种仅基于背景场动力学就能获得这些结果的新方法。

Method: 该方法结合热核（Heat Kernel, HK）和背景场方法（Background Field Method），通过对热核展开中的开导数和闭导数进行一致处理，实现仅从背景场动力学计算规范不变量。

Result: 该方法成功计算了标准量如β函数，并证明了当背景场在壳时这些量的规范参数无关性。通过标量QED（Scalar QED）和Yukawa理论的示例验证了形式体系，标准模型玻色子部分的完整结果进一步验证了该方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的热核与背景场方法结合的新形式体系，能够独立于传统费曼图计算，仅从背景场动力学获得规范不变且规范参数无关的物理量，为标准模型等理论的计算提供了新途径。

Abstract: We introduce a new method that exploits the combination of the Heat Kernel (HK) and Background Field Method to compute gauge-invariant and gauge parameter-independent quantities such as the effective potential, anomalous dimensions, and renormalization group equations. In contrast to currently employed techniques, these results are obtained exclusively from the dynamics of the background fields, without relying on supplementary input from, e.g., traditional diagrammatic calculations. This is achieved by a consistent treatment of open and closed derivatives in the HK expansions. In this way, we compute the standard quantities such as $β$ functions and their gauge-parameter independence when background fields are on-shell. We demonstrate this formalism for instructive examples such as Scalar QED and Yukawa theory. Full results for the bosonic part of the Standard Model provide further validation of our approach.

</details>


### [51] [Are Black Holes Fuzzballs? Probing Horizon-Scale Structure with LISA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06009)
*Pablo F. Muguruza,Carlos F. Sopuerta*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了如何利用空间引力波探测器LISA观测极端质量比旋近系统（EMRIs）来检验模糊球（fuzzball）提案——一种量子引力启发的克尔黑洞替代模型。通过引入编码潜在对称性破缺的通用多极形变并进行系统参数估计分析，研究预测了LISA约束近视界区域偏离克尔几何的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波为探测强场引力机制提供了独特工具，能够探索超越经典黑洞范式的新物理。研究旨在利用空间引力波观测来检验量子引力启发的模糊球提案，该提案是克尔黑洞的一种替代模型。

Method: 通过引入编码潜在对称性破缺的通用多极形变（generic multipolar deformations），并针对激光干涉空间天线（Laser Interferometer Space Antenna, LISA）观测的极端质量比旋近系统（extreme-mass-ratio inspirals, EMRIs）进行系统参数估计分析。

Result: 研究表明，具有现实信噪比的EMRI信号能够以远超当前电磁和地基引力波界限的数量级水平约束多个高阶多极矩。具体而言，LISA可将通用非轴对称质量四极形变约束在10^{-3}水平，轴对称质量八极形变约束在10^{-2}水平。

Conclusion: EMRI波形的精确测量将使LISA成为基础物理的强大实验室，并为量子引力启致的致密天体模型提供首个直接经验约束。这为识别模糊球几何提供了具体的观测目标，开启了探索视界尺度结构的新观测窗口。

Abstract: Gravitational waves provide a unique probe of the strong-field regime of gravity, offering access to physics beyond the classical black hole paradigm. We explore how space-based observations of extreme-mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) by the Laser Interferometer Space Antenna (LISA) can be used to test the fuzzball proposal, a quantum gravity-inspired alternative to Kerr black holes. By introducing generic multipolar deformations encoding potential symmetry breakings and performing a systematic parameter estimation analysis, we forecast LISA's ability to constrain deviations from the Kerr geometry in the near-horizon region. We show that EMRI signals with realistic signal-to-noise ratios can constrain multiple higher-order multipoles at levels orders of magnitude beyond current electromagnetic and ground-based gravitational-wave bounds, opening a new observational window onto horizon-scale structure. In particular, we find that LISA can constrain generic non-axisymmetric mass quadrupole deformations at the $10^{-3}$ level and axisymmetric mass octupole deformations at the $10^{-2}$ level, providing concrete observational targets for identifying fuzzball geometries. Our results demonstrate that precision measurements of EMRI waveforms will transform LISA into a powerful laboratory for fundamental physics and offer the first direct empirical constraints on quantum-gravity-motivated models of compact objects.

### [52] [$ξRφ^2$ non-minimal coupling, and the long range gravitational potential for different spin fields from 2-2 scattering amplitudes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06062)
*Avijit Sen Majumder,Ayan Kumar Naskar,Sourav Bhattacharya*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在微扰量子引力框架下，研究了曲率-标量场非最小耦合（$ξR φ^2$）的长程引力效应，计算了标量-标量散射振幅及其对应的非相对论极限势能，发现势能具有$r^{-4}$主导行为，并将结果扩展到标量与自旋粒子散射。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究曲率-标量场非最小耦合（curvature-scalar field non-minimal coupling）$ξR φ^2$的长程引力效应，该耦合自然地源于弯曲时空背景下具有四次自相互作用的标量场理论的重整化（renormalisation）。

Method: 在微扰量子引力（perturbative quantum gravity）框架下，假设无量纲耦合参数$ξ$较小，计算了标量-标量散射（scalar-scalar scattering）的费曼振幅（Feynman amplitudes）至${\cal O}(G^2 ξ)$阶，并从振幅的非相对论极限（non-relativistic limit）推导出相应的长程引力势（long range gravitational potential）。

Result: 发现不存在树图阶贡献（tree level contribution），因此单圈${\cal O}(G^2 ξ)$结果是主导的；所得势能具有$r^{-4}$主导行为，并将结果扩展到标量与有质量自旋-1粒子（massive spin-1）和有质量自旋-1/2粒子（massive spin-1/2）的散射，明确展示了二体势（two body potential）的自旋和极化依赖性。

Conclusion: 非最小耦合$ξR φ^2$在微扰量子引力中产生独特的长程引力效应，势能呈现$r^{-4}$标度行为，且结果可推广到不同自旋粒子的散射，这些发现具有潜在的物理意义。

Abstract: In this paper we investigate the long range gravitational effect of curvature-scalar field non-minimal coupling, in the form of $ξR φ^2$, in the perturbative quantum gravity framework. Such coupling is most naturally motivated from the renormalisation of a scalar field theory with a quartic self interaction in a curved spacetime background. This coupling results in two scalar-$n$ graviton vertices which contain no explicit momenta of the scalar, qualitatively different from the usual, e.g. $κh^{μν}T_{μν}$-type minimal matter-graviton vertices. Assuming the dimensionless coupling parameter $ξ$ to be small, we compute the 2-2 scattering Feynman amplitudes between such scalars up to ${\cal O}(G^2 ξ)$. From the non-relativistic limit of these amplitudes, we compute the corresponding long range gravitational potential. There exists no tree level contribution $({\cal O}(ξG))$ here, and hence the one loop ${\cal O}(G^2 ξ)$ result is leading. Recently, the effect of a cosmological constant in such non-minimal interaction and the subsequent gravitational potential was computed. In this work we take the cosmological constant to be vanishing. The resulting potential is found to have $r^{-4}$ leading behaviour. We further extend these results for scalar-massive spin-1 and massive spin-1/2 scattering. Spin and polarisation dependence of the two body potential have been explicitly demonstrated. We discuss some possible physical implications of these results.

</details>


### [53] [Comments on Symmetry Operators, Asymptotic Charges and Soft Theorems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06088)
*Luigi Tizzano*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了量子电动力学（QED）中涌现的1-形式对称性（emergent 1-form symmetries）与软光子定理（soft photon theorems）之间的关系，揭示了在重夸克有效理论（HQET）和软共线有效理论（SCET）描述的动力学区域中，软光子部分存在电性和磁性的1-形式对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索量子电动力学中涌现的1-形式对称性与软光子定理之间的深层联系，理解在特定动力学区域（质量与无质量情况）下对称性结构如何决定软光子的物理行为。

Method: 研究方法基于重夸克有效理论（HQET）和软共线有效理论（SCET）分别描述质量和无质量运动学区域，分析软光子部分的对称性结构，并构建无限维阿贝尔代数（infinite-dimensional Abelian algebra）及其中心扩展（central extension）。

Result: 研究结果表明：1）软光子部分存在电性和磁性的1-形式对称性；2）这些对称性产生具有中心扩展的无限维阿贝尔代数；3）在闵可夫斯基时空（Minkowski spacetime）中，适当的超曲面选择可将这些荷简化为熟悉的渐近对称性荷，并导出领先阶的电性和磁性软光子定理；4）代数中的中心项固定了涉及混合电-磁极化双软光子散射振幅中的接触项（contact term）。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了量子电动力学中1-形式对称性与软光子定理之间的直接联系，并将该构造推广到包含可观测量（inclusive observables），应用于QED光子探测器，为理解软光子的对称性起源提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We study the relation between emergent 1-form symmetries and soft photon theorems in QED. We show that in the relevant massive and massless kinematic regimes, described respectively by HQET and SCET, the soft sector admits electric and magnetic 1-form symmetries. We then show that these symmetries give rise to an infinite-dimensional Abelian algebra of ordinary conserved charges, with a central extension. In Minkowski spacetime, suitable choices of hypersurfaces reduce these charges to the familiar asymptotic symmetry charges and imply the leading electric and magnetic soft photon theorems. We further show that the central term in this algebra fixes a contact term appearing in scattering amplitudes involving two soft photons with mixed electric-magnetic polarizations. Finally, we extend the same construction to inclusive observables and apply it to QED photon detectors.

### [54] [Massive Exchange and the Sign of the Equilateral Bispectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06145)
*Diptimoy Ghosh,Suvashis Maity,Farman Ullah*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究暴胀过程中通过树级交换大质量隐藏扇区标量产生的暴胀三点关联函数（bispectrum）。研究发现，当考虑完整的有效场论算符基时，等边构型三点关联函数的符号不再具有普适性，其正负取决于相互作用系数的临界比值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究表明，在暴胀有效场论中，当暴胀子与隐藏扇区仅通过主导的洛伦兹破缺算符相互作用时，主系列标量交换产生的等边三点关联函数总是负值。本文旨在重新审视这一结论在完整有效场论算符基下的普适性。

Method: 采用自举方法（bootstrap methods）构建德西特不变的四点关联函数种子，并通过权重移动算符（weight-shifting operators）和软极限过程（soft-limit procedure）获得暴胀三点关联函数。研究考虑了完整的有效场论算符基，并分析了减小声速和多重粒子交换的影响。

Result: 当仅存在主导相互作用时，等边三点关联函数保持严格负值；但额外算符会产生独立的立方结构，其在等边构型中相互竞争，导致三点关联函数符号不再具有普适性。研究推导出区分正负等边三点关联函数区域的相互作用系数临界比值，并发现减小声速和多重粒子交换会修改该临界比值。

Conclusion: 大质量交换产生的等边三点关联函数的负值特性并非普适性质，而是反映了暴胀有效场论中算符结构的限制性。在完整算符基下，三点关联函数的符号取决于相互作用系数的特定比值，为观测检验提供了更丰富的可能性。

Abstract: We study the inflationary bispectrum generated by the tree-level exchange of a massive hidden-sector scalar during inflation. When the interaction between the inflaton and the hidden sector arises only from the leading boost-breaking operator of the Effective Field Theory (EFT) of inflation, the equilateral bispectrum for principal-series scalar exchange is known to be universally negative, independent of the sign of the coupling. We revisit this result within the full EFT operator basis. Using bootstrap methods, we construct the de Sitter-invariant seed four-point function and obtain the inflationary bispectrum via weight-shifting operators and a soft-limit procedure. While the equilateral bispectrum remains strictly negative when only the leading interaction is present, additional operators generate independent cubic structures whose contributions compete in the equilateral configuration. As a result, the sign of the bispectrum is no longer universal. We derive a critical ratio of interaction coefficients that separates regions of positive and negative equilateral bispectrum. We further study the effects of reduced sound speed $c_s<1$ and the exchange of multiple particles. In both cases, the critical ratio is modified, and for multi-particle exchange a positive equilateral bispectrum can arise even when the higher-order operator is subdominant. Our results show that the negativity of the equilateral bispectrum from massive exchange is not generic, but reflects a restricted operator structure in the EFT of inflation.

</details>

### [55] [Spectrum-Generating Algebra in Higher Dimensional Gauge Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05763)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强相互作用规范理论（strongly interacting gauge theories）的非平衡性质通常难以用经典模拟方法处理。随着量子模拟技术的发展，研究其在二维空间中的性质变得可行。

Method: 通过将原始规范理论映射到受约束自旋链（constrained spin chain）的对偶化过程（dualization process）来分析模型。提出了一组用于诊断近似谱生成代数的可观测量。

Result: 证明了纯规范场梯子模型（pure gauge plaquette ladder）存在近似谱生成代数，并预测和验证了自旋-1量子链接模型（spin-1 Quantum Link Models）中量子多体疤痕的存在。

Conclusion: 所提出的可观测量有望指导量子模拟器（quantum simulators）探索有趣的物理区域。若无约束条件，系统将具有精确的谱生成代数。

Abstract: Non-equilibrium properties of strongly interacting gauge theories are often intractable with classical simulation methods. Due to recent developments of quantum simulations, studies of their properties in two spatial dimensions are becoming accessible. By demonstrating the existence of an approximate spectrum-generating algebra for a pure gauge plaquette ladder, we predict and verify the existence of Quantum Many-Body Scars in spin-1 Quantum Link Models. The analysis of the model is facilitated by a dualization process that maps the original gauge theory to a constrained spin chain. Was it not for the constraint, the system would have an exact spectrum-generating algebra. We propose a set of observables for diagnosing an approximate spectrum-generating algebra, which is expected to guide quantum simulators toward interesting physical regimes.

### [56] [From Ferrimagnetic Insulator to superconducting Luther-Emery Liquid: A DMRG Study of the Two-Leg Lieb Lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05027)
*Alexander Nikolaenko,Subir Sachdev*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）方法研究二维Lieb梯子上的Hubbard模型，发现不同填充分数下的基态相图，包括半填充时的铁磁性Mott绝缘体、有限填充时的自旋有序态，以及在临界填充nc≈2/3附近出现的sxy波超导Luther-Emery相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group, DMRG）方法分析二维Lieb梯子上的Hubbard模型，系统研究不同填充分数n下的基态性质。

Result: 在半填充时发现铁磁性Mott绝缘基态，符合Lieb定理；偏离半填充时，系统在填充nc≈2/3以上保持有限总自旋和零电荷能隙；低于该填充时，系统表现为具有一个电荷模和一个自旋模的Luttinger液体；在nc≈2/3附近的窄窗口内，发现了具有主导sxy波配对的超导Luther-Emery相。

Conclusion: 二维Lieb梯子Hubbard模型展现出丰富的相图，包括铁磁性Mott绝缘体、自旋有序态、Luttinger液体以及临界填充附近的sxy波超导相，这些发现为理解相关实验现象提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Motivated by recent experiments on ultracold fermionic spin-1/2 $^6$Li atoms in a Lieb lattice at various Hubbard repulsion $U$ and filling fractions $n$ (Lebrat et al., arXiv:2404.17555), we conduct a density matrix renormalization group (DMRG) analysis of the Hubbard model on a two-leg Lieb ladder. At half-filling, we find a ferrimagnetic Mott insulating ground state, consistent with Lieb's theorem. Away from half-filling, a state with finite total spin $\vec{S}^2 \neq 0$ and vanishing charge gap persists down to filling $n_c \approx 2/3$. For lower, incommensurate fillings, the system is described by a Luttinger liquid with one charge and one spin mode. Intriguingly, in a narrow window near $n_c = 2/3$, close to the onset of ferromagnetic order, we identify a superconducting Luther-Emery phase with dominant $s_{xy}$-wave pairing.

### [57] [Decoding Equilibrium and Dynamical Criticality in the 2D Topological Order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05198)
*Xiao-Ming Zhao,Cui-Xian Guo,Gaoyong Sun,Su-Peng Kou*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了二维强相互作用Wen-plaquette模型中，微观静态奇点（static singularities）如何统一解码平衡临界性和非幺正动力学量子相变（DQPTs）。通过将任意子激发映射到一维有效耗散通道，发现静态奇点精确重构宏观平衡拓扑相边界，并在非幺正淬火动力学中强制动量空间排斥，最终通过耗散-相位竞争机制消除DQPTs。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究采用二维强相互作用Wen-plaquette模型，将其任意子激发映射到一维有效耗散通道。通过分析微观单粒子保真度零点（single-particle fidelity zeros）和静态奇点，并与宏观平衡拓扑相边界对比，同时研究非幺正淬火动力学中的动力学Fisher零点（dynamical Fisher zeros）。

Result: 微观单粒子保真度零点精确重构了宏观平衡拓扑相边界。在非幺正淬火动力学中，这些静态奇点强制动量空间排斥，阻止动力学Fisher零点的形成。新发现的耗散-相位竞争机制（dissipation-phase racing mechanism）提前耗尽衰减模式，从根本上消除DQPTs并产生拓扑平凡稳态。

Conclusion: 精确的微观静态奇点可作为宏观非幺正拓扑动力学的通用解码器。该研究建立了静态奇点与动力学量子相变之间的直接联系，揭示了耗散在拓扑动力学中的关键作用，为统一平衡和非平衡拓扑现象提供了新框架。

Abstract: Unifying equilibrium criticality and dynamical quantum phase transitions (DQPTs) under complex driving fields remains a profound challenge. Here, we decode this connection in the 2D strongly interacting Wen-plaquette model. By mapping its anyonic excitations to 1D effective dissipative channels, we reveal that microscopic single-particle fidelity zeros exactly reconstruct the macroscopic equilibrium topological phase boundaries. Beyond equilibrium, we demonstrate that during non-unitary quench dynamics, these very same static singularities enforce an absolute momentum-space exclusion against dynamical Fisher zeros. Furthermore, a newly identified dissipation-phase racing mechanism prematurely depletes the decaying mode, fundamentally annihilating DQPTs and generating topologically trivial steady states. Our results establish exact microscopic static singularities as the universal decoder for macroscopic non-unitary topological dynamics.

### [58] [H-NESSi: The Hierarchical Non-Equilibrium Systems Simulation package](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05319)
*Thomas Blommel,Jeremija Kovačević,Jason Kaye,Emanuel Gull,Jakša Vučičević,Denis Golež*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强关联量子系统的非平衡模拟受到传统双时间公式中传播时间立方标度和内存二次增长的严重限制，这阻碍了长时间和大系统的计算研究。

Method: H-NESSi结合高阶时间步进方案与推迟和较小格林函数的层次非对角低秩表示，实现可控精度；采用离散Lehmann表示高效处理虚时间量，支持多轨道系统和自适应奇异值截断。

Result: 在动态平均场理论中的驱动超导体和二维Hubbard模型上的基准测试表明，与传统实现相比具有有利的标度特性，渐近时间复杂度显著低于非压缩方法的立方标度。

Conclusion: H-NESSi使得以前计算上不可行的关联量子材料长时间和大系统非平衡模拟成为可能，为强关联系统的非平衡研究提供了高效计算工具。

Abstract: We present H-NESSi (The Hierarchical Non-Equilibrium Systems Simulation package), an open-source software package for solving the Kadanoff-Baym equations (KBE) of nonequilibrium Green's function (NEGF) theory using hierarchical low-rank compression techniques. The simulation of strongly correlated quantum systems out of equilibrium is severely limited by the cubic scaling in propagation time and quadratic memory growth associated with conventional two-time formulations. H-NESSi overcomes these limitations by combining high-order time-stepping schemes with hierarchical off-diagonal low-rank (HODLR) representations of the retarded and lesser Green's functions, enabling controllable accuracy at substantially reduced computational cost and memory usage. Imaginary time quantities are efficiently represented using the discrete Lehmann representation (DLR), allowing compact and accurate treatment of thermal initial states. The implementation supports multiorbital systems, adaptive singular value truncation, and both shared-memory (OpenMP) and distributed-memory (MPI) parallelization strategies suitable for large-scale lattice calculations. The workflow closely mirrors established NEGF frameworks while introducing compression transparently into the propagation procedure. Benchmark applications to driven superconductors within dynamical mean-field theory and to the two-dimensional Hubbard model demonstrate favorable scaling compared to conventional implementations, with asymptotic time complexity significantly below the cubic scaling of uncompressed approaches. H-NESSi thus enables long-time and large-system nonequilibrium simulations of correlated quantum materials which were previously computationally prohibitive.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 实验发现，RuBr₃中的长程zigzag序在尼尔温度（T_N）处消失，但zigzag关联（zigzag correlations）在远高于T_N的温度下仍然持续存在。这些持续存在的关联表现出沿层间方向的显著谱权重重新分布（spectral weight redistribution）。

Conclusion: 结果表明，由扩展的Br 4p轨道驱动的增强层间磁相互作用（interlayer magnetic interactions）稳定了RuBr₃中的三维zigzag关联。这解释了RuBr₃相对于RuCl₃更高的尼尔温度，并阐明了其与Kitaev量子自旋液相的不同接近程度。

Abstract: Ruthenium trihalides Ru$X_3$ ($X$ = Cl, Br, I) provide a tunable platform for Kitaev magnetism in two-dimensional van der Waals materials. Despite their similar crystal structures and zigzag antiferromagnetic order, RuBr$_3$ exhibits a higher Néel temperature ($T_N$) than RuCl$_3$, suggesting their distinct proximity to the Kitaev quantum spin liquid phase. Using Ru $L_3$-edge resonant x-ray scattering, we show that, while the long-range zigzag order in RuBr$_3$ disappears at $T_N$, the zigzag correlations that persist well above $T_N$ show a pronounced spectral weight redistribution along the interlayer direction. These results suggest that the enhanced interlayer magnetic interactions driven by the extended Br 4$p$ orbitals stabilize three-dimensional zigzag correlations in RuBr$_3$.

### [60] [Topologically shadowed quantum criticality: A non-compact conformal manifold](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05391)
*Tianyao Fang,Weicheng Ye,Zhengcheng Gu,Fei Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种拓扑量子临界点（tQCPs）理论，用于描述(2+1)维非可逆手征拓扑序之间的相变。核心发现是这些临界点形成非紧致尺度不变流形，其量子动力学由相邻拓扑相的编织角唯一确定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解(2+1)维非可逆手征拓扑序（non-invertible chiral topological orders）之间的拓扑量子临界点。传统临界理论难以描述这类拓扑相变，需要发展新的理论框架来刻画其尺度不变性和拓扑约束特征。

Method: 方法包括：1）提出拓扑量子临界点（tQCPs）的场论描述，形成非紧致尺度不变流形（non-compact scale-invariant manifold）；2）引入拓扑阴影（topological shadowing）概念，利用相邻拓扑相的全局拓扑数据约束临界理论；3）通过重整化群计算（renormalization group calculations）验证尺度不变性，计算达到两圈（two-loop）阶。

Result: 主要结果：1）建立了拓扑角（topological angle）Θ_cft与相邻拓扑相编织角（braiding angles）Θ_1,Θ_2的精确关系：Θ_cft^{-1} = 1/2[Θ_1^{-1} + Θ_2^{-1}]；2）重整化群计算表明理论保持精确尺度不变性（exact scale invariance）；3）在没有超对称性（supersymmetry）条件下，建立了连续固定点流形，当局部结构加强时自然成为共形流形（conformal manifold）。

Conclusion: 结论表明，拓扑量子临界点可由非紧致尺度不变场论描述，其量子动力学完全由相邻拓扑相的拓扑数据决定。这一框架为理解拓扑相变提供了新视角，并展示了拓扑约束如何决定临界行为，无需依赖超对称性即可获得连续固定点流形。

Abstract: We put forward a proposal for topological quantum critical points (tQCPs) separating non-invertible chiral topological orders in $(2+1)$ dimensions. We conjecture that these tQCPs can be captured by a family of scale-invariant field theories forming a non-compact scale-invariant manifold. A central feature of our proposal is topological shadowing: the underlying critical theory is rigorously constrained by the global topological data of the two adjacent gapped phases. These theories can be further projected into quantum field theories with universal non-local structures. Specifically, we show that the quantum dynamics of the $U(1)$ symmetric critical point uniquely characterized by a topological angle $Θ_{\text{cft}}$ -- which is defined by a commutator between two Wilson loop operators on a torus -- is determined by the braiding angles $Θ_{1,2}$ of the adjacent gapped phases via the relation $Θ_{\text{cft}}^{-1} =\frac{1}{2}[Θ_1^{-1} + Θ_2^{-1}]$. Despite the non-locality, our renormalization group calculations (up to two-loop order) strongly suggest that the theory shall maintain exact scale invariance. This establishes, without supersymmetry, a continuous manifold of fixed points that naturally becomes a conformal manifold when the local structure is further enforced.

### [61] [Magnetic toroidal monopoles from relativistic polarization responses to magnetic field gradients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05412)

Abstract: The magnetic toroidal monopole, a time-reversal-odd scalar, has attracted attention through its characteristic responses, such as electric-field-induced nonreciprocal directional dichroism observed in Co$_2$SiO$_4$. However, its evaluation in crystalline solids remains unresolved, as it cannot be defined within conventional multipole expansions or thermodynamic formulations. In this paper, we propose a theoretical framework to evaluate the magnetic toroidal monopole in periodic crystals based on the response of relativistic electric polarization to a magnetic field gradient. By incorporating the magnetic-field-gradient correction to the relativistic polarization, we derive an explicit expression for the magnetic toroidal monopole beyond symmetry arguments. The resulting expression is formulated in terms of geometric quantity such as Berry curvatures and orbital magnetic moment defined in an extended parameter space spanning momentum, magnetic field, and electric field. We further perform model calculations for an antiferromagnetic system hosting a magnetic toroidal monopole and confirm that the proposed quantity is finite. These results provide a practical route to characterize magnetic toroidal monopoles in crystalline solids and clarify their quantum geometric nature.

Abstract: The absence of conventional magnetic order together with anomalous low-temperature magnetic heat capacity is often interpreted as evidence for quantum spin liquid ground states in frustrated magnets. Abstract: Second-harmonic generation (SHG) is a quintessential probe of inversion symmetry breaking in condensed matter. In this Letter, we develop a nonperturbative Floquet-Keldysh theory to describe SHG in two-band systems. Our analysis reveals the emergence of two distinct types of nonperturbative saturation: a transition from the conventional $E^2$ scaling to a linear $E$ dependence, and a stronger saturation regime where the SHG response becomes independent of the field amplitude. These behaviors are analytically shown to be governed by one-photon and two-photon resonance processes, respectively. ### [66] [Quantum spin liquid ground state with the evidence of roton-like excitations at elevated temperatures in the triangular-lattice delafossite YbCuSe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05784)
*K. Bhattacharya,Y. Tokiwa,M. Majumder*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过综合实验手段系统研究了三角晶格（triangular lattice）delafossite YbCuSe₂中磁态随温度的演化，发现其存在动态涨落的量子自旋液体（quantum spin liquid）基态，并首次观测到类roton激发特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探究三角晶格delafossite YbCuSe₂中磁态随温度的演化，特别是探索其是否存在量子自旋液体（QSL）基态以及相关的激发特征，为理解量子磁性材料提供新平台。

Method: 采用高质量单晶样品，通过磁化测量、比热、μ子自旋弛豫（μSR）等综合实验手段，系统研究了YbCuSe₂在低至0.03 K温度下的磁性和热力学性质。

Result: 实验证实YbCuSe₂在低至0.03 K（≤J_avg/250）时仍无磁有序或自旋冻结，表现出动态涨落的量子自旋液体基态。热力学测量揭示了三个特征能量尺度：T_H≈4.5 K、T_L≈1.8 K和T^*≈0.7 K。μSR在T^*以下检测到动力学相分离，大部分自旋形成QSL态，少数自旋形成与主QSL组分解耦的零星无序诱导态。特别值得注意的是，μSR弛豫率的非常规温度依赖表明在T_H和T_L之间出现了类roton激发，这是首次在QSL系统中观测到的特征。

Conclusion: YbCuSe₂被确认为独特的量子自旋液体平台，其观测到的类roton激发为量子磁性研究提供了新视角，为后续实验和理论探索提供了宝贵见解。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive experimental investigation of the temperature evolution of magnetic states in triangular-lattice delafossite YbCuSe$_2$. Magnetization measurements on high-quality single crystals reveal easy-plane anisotropy. Specific heat, magnetization, and muon spin relaxation ($μ$SR) establish the absence of magnetic order or spin freezing down to 0.03 K ($\leq J_{\mathrm{avg}}/250$), demonstrating a dynamically fluctuating quantum spin liquid (QSL) ground state. Thermodynamic measurements uncover multiple characteristic energy scales at $T_H \approx 4.5$ K, $T_L \approx 1.8$ K, and $T^* \approx 0.7$ K. Below $T^*$, $μ$SR detects a dynamical phase separation in which the majority of the spins are forming a QSL state whereas the remaining spins form a sporadic, disorder-induced state decoupled from the dominant QSL component. Remarkably, the unconventional temperature dependence of the $μ$SR relaxation rate indicates roton-like excitations emerging between $T_H$ and $T_L$, a feature not previously observed in any QSL system, preceding the stabilization of the low-temperature QSL at 0.3 K. These findings identify YbCuSe$_2$ as a unique QSL platform, providing valuable insights for further experimental and theoretical exploration.

</details>


### [67] [Quantum phases in the interacting generalized Su-Schrieffer-Heeger model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05928)
*Jing-Hua Niu,Jia-Lin Liu,Ke Wang,Shan-Wen Tsai,Jin Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究分析了半填充广义相互作用Su-Schrieffer-Heeger模型中的量子相，揭示了非相互作用极限下的拓扑相及其在相互作用下的演化，包括对称破缺相、电荷密度波相、Luttinger液体相和具有边缘态的gapless对称保护拓扑相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索半填充广义相互作用Su-Schrieffer-Heeger模型中量子相的丰富相图，特别关注相互作用如何影响和演化非相互作用极限下的对称保护拓扑相，以及强相互作用下新相的出现。

Method: 研究方法基于广义相互作用Su-Schrieffer-Heeger模型，包含胞内、最近邻和次近邻胞间跃迁以及格点间相互作用。通过分析缠绕数、纠缠谱简并度、边界模式、弦序参量、中心荷和临界指数等特征来表征不同量子相。

Result: 研究结果表明：非相互作用极限下存在一个拓扑平庸相和两个对称保护拓扑相；引入相互作用后，这些相演化为具有纠缠谱简并结构、边界模式和非零弦序参量的相互作用拓扑相；强排斥相互作用下出现对称破缺相；强吸引相互作用下产生周期-2和周期-4电荷密度波相；中等吸引相互作用下出现Luttinger液体相、配对Luttinger液体相和具有电流携带边缘态的gapless对称保护拓扑相。

Conclusion: 该研究系统揭示了广义相互作用Su-Schrieffer-Heeger模型中丰富的量子相图，包括拓扑相、对称破缺相、电荷密度波相和gapless相，并通过中心荷和临界指数进一步表征了gapless相及其量子相变。

Abstract: We investigate the quantum phases of a half-filled generalized interacting Su-Schrieffer-Heeger model with intracell, nearest-neighbor, and next-nearest-neighbor intercell hoppings, together with an on-site inter-sublattice interaction. In the noninteracting limit, the model hosts one topologically trivial phase and two symmetry-protected topological (SPT) phases, distinguished under periodic boundary conditions by different winding numbers and under open boundary conditions by two-fold and four-fold entanglement-spectrum degeneracies, respectively. When interactions are introduced, these free-fermion SPT phases evolve into distinct interacting topological phases that retain characteristic signatures such as entanglement-spectrum degeneracy structures, boundary modes, and nonzero string order parameters. For strong repulsive interactions, a symmetry-breaking phase with unequal but spatially uniform sublattice densities appears between the trivial and topological regimes. For strong attractive interactions, period-2 and period-4 charge-density-wave phases emerge from particle clustering. At intermediate attractive interactions, the competition between interaction-induced localization and hopping-induced delocalization gives rise to a Luttinger liquid phase, a paired Luttinger liquid phase, and a gapless symmetry-protected topological (gSPT) phase. The gSPT phase is characterized by a gapless charge mode together with symmetry-protected current-carrying edge states. We further characterize the gapless phases and the associated quantum phase transitions through central charges and critical exponents.

</details>


### [68] [Tractable model for a fractionalized Fermi liquid (FL$^*$) on a square lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06157)
*Piers Coleman,Elio J. König,Aaditya Panigrahi,Alexei Tsvelik*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究构建了一个可解析处理的微观模型，用于描述方晶格上的分数化费米液体（FL*），并探讨其在铜氧化物中的潜在相关性。模型展示了两种相态：一种是分数化费米子与传导电子杂化形成违反传统卢廷格计数的小费米面相，另一种是两者保持解耦。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于对无需对称性破缺的费米面重构（Fermi-surface reconstruction）的持续关注。作者旨在构建一个可解析处理的微观模型来描述分数化费米液体（fractionalized Fermi liquid, FL*），并探讨其在铜氧化物（cuprates）中的潜在相关性。

Method: 方法基于构建一个与Kondo晶格系统相关的微观模型，其中传导电子与Yao-Lee类型的ℤ₂自旋液体（spin liquid）相互作用，该自旋液体具有马约拉纳费米面（Majorana Fermi surface）。相关的ℤ₂规范理论（gauge theory）是静态的，使得模型可在领头对数精度（leading-logarithmic accuracy）下解析求解。

Result: 模型揭示了两种相态：一种是分数化费米子与传导电子杂化形成共同费米面，该费米面违反传统的卢廷格计数（Luttinger count）；另一种是两者保持解耦。研究分析了小费米面相的显著特征，包括解析推导出的动量依赖相干因子（momentum dependent coherence factors），这些因子导致了类Yang-Rice-Zhang费米弧（Fermi arcs）的出现。此外，还探讨了量子与热涨落的影响，包括强抗磁响应（diamagnetic response）以及在赝隙（pseudogap）起始点出现的对数发散索末菲系数（Sommerfeld coefficient）。

Conclusion: 该研究成功构建了一个可解析求解的微观模型，为理解无需对称性破缺的费米面重构提供了理论框架。模型预测的小费米面相及其特征（如费米弧）与铜氧化物中的赝隙现象相关，揭示了分数化费米液体相在强关联电子系统中的潜在重要性。

Abstract: Motivated by the continued interest in Fermi-surface reconstruction without symmetry breaking, we present an analytically tractable microscopic model of a fractionalized Fermi liquid (FL$^*$) on a square lattice and discuss its potential relevance to the cuprates. As in ancilla-qubit constructions, the model is related to Kondo lattice systems, but in this case, the conduction electrons interact with a $\mathbb{Z}_2$ spin liquid of the Yao--Lee type, with a Majorana Fermi surface. The associated $\mathbb Z_2$ gauge theory is static so that the model can be analytically solved to leading-logarithic accuracy. There are two phases: one in which the fractionalized fermions of the spin liquid hybridize with conduction electrons to form a common Fermi surface violating the naive Luttinger count, and one in which they remain decoupled. We discuss the salient features of the small Fermi-surface phase, including analytically derived momentum dependent coherence factors responsible for the appearance of Fermi arcs à la Yang-Rice-Zhang. We further discuss the impact of quantum and thermal fluctuations, including a strong diamagnetic response and a logarithmically divergent Sommerfeld coefficient at the onset of the pseudogap.

### [69] [Temperature Dependent Characteristics of Quasi-vertical AlN Schottky Diodes on Bulk AlN Substrate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05106)
*Md Abdul Hamid,Nabasindhu Das,Advait Gilankar,Brad Lenzen,David J. Smith,Nidhin Kurian Kalarickal*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 该研究报道了在块状AlN衬底上制备的MOCVD生长准垂直AlN肖特基势垒二极管（SBDs）及其温度依赖性表征。器件在室温下表现出超过2 kA/cm²的高电流密度、约3.0 V的开启电压和>10⁹的开/关比，并在高达300°C下保持稳定整流特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究AlN肖特基势垒二极管（Schottky barrier diodes）的高温特性和载流子传输机制，为开发高性能AlN功率器件提供指导。研究关注界面化学、泄漏机制和温度依赖性等关键问题。

Method: 采用金属有机化学气相沉积（MOCVD）技术在块状AlN衬底上制备准垂直AlN肖特基势垒二极管。通过温度依赖性电流-电压（I-V）和电容-电压（C-V）测量进行电学表征，并结合透射电子显微镜（transmission electron microscopy）和能量色散X射线光谱（energy-dispersive X-ray spectroscopy）分析界面结构。

Result: 器件在室温下达到超过2 kA/cm²的电流密度和>10⁹的开/关比，并在高达300°C下保持稳定整流。温度升高导致电流密度增加、肖特基势垒高度（Schottky barrier height）增大和理想因子降低。C-V测量显示净施主浓度（ND-NA）从300 K的~5×10¹⁷ cm⁻³增加到373 K的~1×10¹⁸ cm⁻³。反向偏置特性表明普尔-弗兰克尔发射（Poole-Frenkel emission）是主要泄漏机制，陷阱能量约为0.34 eV。界面分析揭示了~5 nm的AlNxOy界面层。

Conclusion: 该研究深入揭示了AlN肖特基二极管的载流子传输机制、泄漏机制、界面化学和高温特性。界面层对正向和反向传输均有影响，这些结果为开发高性能AlN功率器件提供了重要指导。

Abstract: We report on the fabrication and temperature-dependent characterization of MOCVD-grown quasi-vertical AlN Schottky barrier diodes (SBDs) on bulk AlN substrates. The SBDs exhibited high current densities exceeding 2 kA/cm2 at 10 V, with a turn-on voltage of ~3.0 V (at 1 A/cm^2) and an on/off ratio >10^9 at room temperature. Stable rectifying operation was maintained up to 300 C (the highest measured temperature), with a pronounced increase in current density at elevated temperatures due to thermally activated carrier transport, accompanied by an increase in extracted Schottky barrier height and a reduction in ideality factor. Capacitance voltage measurements showed strong temperature dependence due to the deep donor nature of Si in AlN, resulting in an increase in the net donor concentration (ND-NA) from ~5x10^17 cm-3 at 300 K to ~1x10^18 cm-3 at 373 K. Temperature-dependent reverse-bias characteristics were consistent with Poole-Frenkel emission as the dominant leakage mechanism, with an estimated trap energy of ~0.34 eV. Characterization using transmission electron microscopy and energy-dispersive X-ray spectroscopy revealed a ~5 nm AlNxOy interfacial layer at the metal/semiconductor junction, which likely influences both forward and reverse transport. These results provide insight into carrier transport, leakage mechanisms, interface chemistry, and high-temperature characteristics, and guidance for the future development of high-performance AlN power devices.

### [70] [Experimental measurements and modeling of characteristic time scales in single iron particle ignition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05073)
*Liulin Cen,Yong Qian,XiaoCheng Mi,Xingcai Lu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究结合数字在线全息术与超高速单色高温测量技术，首次获得了微米级球形铁颗粒在热氧化环境中燃烧时的固相氧化特征时间，并建立了基于抛物线速率定律的固体相铁氧化动力学点火模型。

Method: 采用数字在线全息术（digital in-line holography）结合超高速单色高温测量技术（ultra-high-speed single-color pyrometry），在明确定义的热氧化环境中测量球形微米级铁颗粒的燃烧过程。建立了基于抛物线速率定律（parabolic rate law）的固体相铁氧化动力学点火模型，并结合外部氧传输限制描述进行模拟。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了首个FeO和Fe熔化过程的直径分辨数据集，表明该建模框架能够定量预测金属燃料应用中单铁颗粒的特征时间，为燃烧器和反应器设计提供了关键数据支持。

Abstract: Recyclable metal fuels such as iron are promising carbon-free energy carriers for heat and power. In such systems, particle ignition characteristics strongly affect combustion efficiency and combustor stability, making them critical for burner and reactor design. However, predictive ignition modelling remains limited by the lack of time-resolved data for single-particle solid-phase oxidation and phase transitions. In this work, digital in-line holography combined with ultra-high-speed single-color pyrometry is used to resolve characteristic solid-phase oxidation times of spherical micron-sized iron particles burning in well-defined hot oxidizing environments. Three temperature plateaus are identified, corresponding to FeO melting, the γ-Fe to δ-Fe transition, and Fe melting, from which pre-melting oxidation times and melting durations are extracted. An ignition model based on solid-phase iron oxidation kinetics following a parabolic rate law, coupled with external-oxygen-transport-limited description, is used to simulate these characteristic times. The model accurately captures the FeO-scale pre-melting oxidation time, which is nearly independent of oxygen concentration, while the FeO, γ-Fe to δ-Fe, and Fe melting stages show strong oxygen-concentration dependence consistent with external-oxygen-transport-limited reaction rates. These measurements and simulations provide the first diameter-resolved dataset for FeO and Fe melting processes and show that this modelling framework can quantitatively predict characteristic times for single iron particles in metal-fuel applications.

### [71] [Zr Concentration-Dependent Sub-Lattice Phase-Field Model of Hf1-xZrxO2: Analysis of Phase Composition and Polarization Switching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05184)
*Tae Ryong Kim,Sumeet K. Gupta*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一个包含锆（Zr）浓度依赖性的Hf1-xZrxO2亚晶格相场模型，成功再现了从铁电（FE）到反铁电（AFE）的转变过程，并揭示了中间浓度下的混合相行为和空间交错极化反转机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究开发了包含锆浓度依赖性的亚晶格相场模型（sub-lattice phase-field model），将时间依赖的金兹堡-朗道方程（time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau equation, TDGL）扩展到亚晶格层面，并引入了浓度依赖的相互作用参数和梯度系数。

Result: 模型成功再现了实验观测到的电荷-电压（Q-V）特性演化，解释了不同锆浓度下的相变行为：低浓度（x=0.5-0.6）时正交相（orthorhombic phase, o-phase）主导的铁电行为；高浓度（x=0.9-1.0）时四方相（tetragonal phase, t-phase）稳定的反铁电转变；中间浓度（x=0.7-0.8）时出现混合相组成和空间交错极化反转。

Conclusion: 该亚晶格相场模型通过将能量景观与空间场效应联系起来，为理解Hf1-xZrxO2中铁电到反铁电的交叉转变提供了重要见解，特别是揭示了中间浓度下由畴壁附近杂散场引起的非均匀电场分布对相变行为的决定性影响。

Abstract: We develop a sub-lattice phase-field model of Hf1-xZrxO2 incorporating zirconium (Zr) concentration (x)-dependence. Our framework expands the time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau (TDGL) equation to the sub-lattice level and incorporates x-dependent interaction parameters and gradient coefficients. Our experimentally calibrated model captures the evolution of charge-voltage (Q-V) characteristics for x ranging from 0.5 to 1.0. The sub-lattice formulation explains the thermodynamic preference and kinetic transition barriers of competing orthorhombic phase (o-phase) and tetragonal phase (t-phase), while the phase-field framework enables spatially resolved analysis of polarization (P) and electric-field (E-field) profiles, allowing multi-domain (MD) polarization and mixed-phase states to emerge naturally. Our model reproduces the experimentally observed ferroelectric (FE)-to-anti-ferroelectric (AFE) transition as x increases from 0.5 to 1.0. At low Zr concentration (x = 0.5-0.6), the o-phase dominates, yielding distinct FE behavior. At high concentration (x = 0.9-1.0), the t-phase is stabilized, leading to AFE transitions. A key finding of our work is the unique behavior at intermediate Zr concentrations (x = 0.7-0.8). Here, the o- and t-phase energies are comparable, making the system strongly influenced by local variations in the electric field (E-field), which arise from stray fields near the domain walls. This non-uniform field distribution results in a mixed-phase composition and spatially staggered polarization reversal, which manifests as a more gradual Q-V evolution compared to other values of x. By linking energy landscapes to spatial field effects, the model provides insights into the FE-to-AFE crossover in Hf1-xZrxO2.

### [72] [Understanding insulating ferromagnetism in LaCoO3 films under tensile strain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05193)
*Ali Barooni,Murod Mirzhalilov,Mohit Randeria,Patrick M. Woodward,Maryam Ghazisaeidi*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已有大量实验和计算研究，但外延拉伸应变下LaCoO3薄膜中铁磁绝缘态的微观起源仍未得到充分理解。本研究旨在通过系统计算揭示这一现象的物理机制。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory）计算，系统研究在SrTiO3衬底等效外延应变下化学计量比LaCoO3的磁性基态。

Result: 计算识别出铁磁绝缘基态，其特征是高自旋（high-spin, HS）和低自旋（low-spin, LS）Co3+离子的独特有序排列，形成2×2柱状结构。电子结构分析确认了绝缘带隙的存在，超交换相互作用（superexchange interactions）分析显示90度铁磁相互作用通过抗磁性LS Co3+离子的空σ*（eg）轨道实现。

Conclusion: 铁磁绝缘态的稳定源于90度铁磁相互作用的强度和数量足以克服竞争的180度反铁磁相互作用。这种独特的自旋态有序排列为理解应变诱导的磁性转变提供了微观机制。

Abstract: LaCoO3 thin films grown under epitaxial tensile strain exhibit a robust ferromagnetic insulating state that is absent in the bulk. Despite many studies, both experimental and computational, the microscopic origin of this phenomenon is not well understood. In this work, density functional theory calculations are used to systematically investigate the magnetic ground state of stoichiometric LaCoO3 under epitaxial strain equivalent to that imposed by a SrTiO3 substrate. The results identify a ferromagnetic insulating ground state characterized by a unique ordered array of high-spin (HS) and low-spin (LS) Co3+ ions. The spin state ordering is best described as 2 x 2 columns that consist of alternating HS and LS Co3+ ions, separated by planes of LS Co3+ ions. This leads to HS-LS-LS repeating sequence of Co3+ ions in both pseudocubic [100] and [010] directions. Analysis of the electronic structure confirms the presence of an insulating gap. Evaluation of the superexchange interactions reveal ferromagnetic interactions between HS Co3+ ions via 90 degree paths, and antiferromagnetic interactions via 180 degree paths, both of which are facilitated by empty sigma* (eg) orbitals on the diamagnetic LS Co3+ ions. The strength and number of 90 degree ferromagnetic interactions are sufficient to overcome the competing 180 degree antiferromagnetic interactions stabilizing a ferromagnetic insulating state.

### [73] [Many-body description of two-dimensional van der Waals ferroelectric $α-$In$_2$Se$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05220)
*Denzel Ayala,Dimitar Pashov,Tong Zhou,Kirill Belashchenko,Mark van Schilfgaarde,Igor Žutić*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维范德华铁电体（2D van der Waals ferroelectrics）在存储器、逻辑器件和神经形态计算等领域具有重要应用潜力，但传统密度泛函理论可能无法可靠描述其基态性质，需要验证和改进计算方法。

Method: 通过扩展开源Questaal软件包中格林函数（Green function）实现的能力，开发了准粒子自洽GW近似（quasiparticle self-consistent GW approximation）这一高保真多体理论方法，并将其应用于In₂Se₃双层和三层系统的研究。

Result: 研究发现，即使复杂的杂化泛函（hybrid functional）方法也可能无法预测双层In₂Se₃的非零带隙，其计算的电荷密度、极化和能带偏移与多体理论结果存在显著偏差。多层系统的电子结构强烈依赖于极化结构，准确计算具有挑战性。

Conclusion: 这些计算进展对二维铁电体未来研究具有重要意义，表明需要超越传统密度泛函理论方法，采用更精确的多体理论来可靠描述二维范德华铁电体的电子性质。

Abstract: Two-dimensional (2D) van der Waals ferroelectrics are recognized for enabling many applications, from memory and logic to neuromorphic computing, as well as transforming other materials to control electronic phase transitions and topological states. While these materials are typically weakly correlated and expected to have their ground-state properties well described with the commonly used density functional theory, by focusing on bilayers and trilayers of In$_2$Se$_3$ we show that this approach may not be reliable. The underlying electronic structure strongly depends on the polarization structure of the multilayer system and is surprisingly challenging to accurately calculate, requiring a high-fidelity many-body theory of the quasiparticle self-consistent \textit{GW} approximation. We develop this underlying description by extending the capabilities of Green function implementation within the open-source Questaal package. We show that even a sophisticated hybrid functional approach may fail to predict a nonvanishing gap in a bilayer In$_2$Se$_3$ and yields charge density, polarization, and band offsets that strongly deviate from the many-body picture. We discuss the implications of these computational advances for future opportunities in 2D ferroelectrics.

### [74] [Stability and superstructural ordering of alkali-triel-pnictide clathrates A$_8$T$_{27}$Pn$_{19}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05264)
*Frank Cerasoli,Xiaochen Jin,Genevieve Amobi,Kirill Kovnir,Davide Donadio*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过高通量密度泛函理论计算探究了非常规包合物A₈T₂₇Pn₁₉家族的稳定性条件，揭示了客体碱金属原子电离势对电子精确包合物稳定性的影响，并发现含重元素（如铋）的包合物稳定性强烈依赖于常被忽略的自旋轨道效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 包合物（clathrates）作为一类包含化合物，展现出超导性、热电性及高密度离子存储潜力等多种有用且令人惊奇的现象。研究旨在探究非常规包合物A₈T₂₇Pn₁₉家族的稳定性条件，以理解其形成机制和性质调控规律。

Method: 采用高通量密度泛函理论（density functional theory）计算研究形成能、结构和电子性质趋势。结合电子结构计算和第一性原理分子动力学（first-principles molecular dynamics）模拟分析客体碱金属原子的电离势对稳定性的影响。尝试从元素前驱体进行定向反应合成，并分析自旋轨道效应（spin-orbit effects）在含重元素包合物稳定性中的作用。

Result: 电子结构计算和分子动力学模拟表明，客体碱金属原子的电离势（ionization potential）强烈影响电子精确包合物的稳定性并影响其"rattler"行为。定向合成尝试获得了两种新型三元化合物，但未获得目标包合物相。进一步分析揭示含重元素（如铋）的ATPn包合物稳定性强烈依赖于常在高通量研究中被忽略的自旋轨道效应。最后描述了与原型I型包合物晶胞中Wyckoff位点相关的化学诱导超结构有序化现象。

Conclusion: 研究表明包合物稳定性受多种因素调控：客体原子的电离势影响电子精确包合物的稳定性，而含重元素的包合物稳定性则强烈依赖于自旋轨道效应。这些发现强调了在计算研究中考虑自旋轨道效应的重要性，并为理解包合物家族的结构-性质关系提供了新见解。

Abstract: Clathrates are a class of inclusion compounds that offer various useful and surprising phenomena, including superconductivity, thermoelectricity, and the potential for high-density ion storage. Stability conditions within the Alkali-Triel-Pnictide A$_8$T$_{27}$Pn$_{19}$ family of unconventional clathrates are investigated with high-throughput density functional theory calculations, establishing trends in formation energy, structural and electronic properties. Electronic structure calculations and first-principles molecular dynamics simulations show that the ionization potential of guest alkaline atoms strongly influences the stability of electron-exact clathrates and affects their rattler behavior. Targeted reactive synthesis from elemental precursors is attempted, resulting in two novel ternary compounds. However, the targeted clathrate phases are not obtained. Further analysis reveals that the stability of ATPn clathrate compounds containing heavy elements, such as bismuth, depends strongly on spin-orbit effects, which are often neglected in high-throughput studies that compute formation energies. Finally, chemically induced superstructural ordering is described in relation to Wyckoff sites in the prototypical type-I clathrate unit cell.

### [75] [Historical Foundation and Practical Guideline for Ferroelectric Switching Kinetic Studies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05328)
*Yi Liang,Pat Kezer,John T. Heron*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了电路因素对铁电开关动力学测量的显著影响，特别是在亚纳秒（sub-ns）区域，指出忽略时变电压波形会导致对开关动力学的非物理解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁电开关动力学（ferroelectric switching kinetics）的电学测量被广泛用于探究极化反转（polarization reversal）的动力学过程，但测量电路的影响常被低估。现有研究往往忽视电路与铁电电容器（ferroelectric capacitors）相互作用产生的失真效应。

Method: 研究分析了铁电电容器与电路元件（circuit elements）的相互作用如何产生失真的时变电压波形（time-dependent voltage waveforms）。通过考察这些电路贡献对从PUND测量中提取的极化瞬态（polarization transients）的影响，评估了现有成核与生长模型（nucleation and growth models）。

Result: 电路引起的失真随电源电压（supply voltage）、电容器尺寸和集总电路元件（lumped circuit elements）而变化，但常规实验分析或解析模型拟合（analytical model fitting）未考虑这些因素。忽略时变电压分布（time-varying voltage profile）会导致对开关动力学的非物理解释，特别是在提取的由Avrami指数（Avrami exponent）表示的生长维度（growth dimensionality）方面。

Conclusion: 研究为未来研究提供了指导方针，强调需要直接电压监测和考虑电路的解嵌（circuit-aware de-embedding），以及基于本征材料参数（intrinsic material parameters）构建包含电压依赖性成核与生长速率（voltage-dependent nucleation and growth rates）的建模框架。

Abstract: Electrical measurements of ferroelectric switching kinetics are widely used to probe the dynamics of polarization reversal, yet the influence of the measurement circuit is often underappreciated. In this paper, we show that the interplay between ferroelectric capacitors and circuit elements produces distorted, time-dependent voltage waveforms across the device, particularly in the sub-ns regime. We examine how these circuit contributions affect polarization transients extracted from PUND measurements. The resulting distortions scale with supply voltage, capacitor dimensions, and lumped circuit elements, but are not accounted for in conventional experimental analyses or analytical model fitting. We then critically assess existing nucleation and growth models and show that neglecting the time-varying voltage profile can lead to unphysical interpretations of switching kinetics, most notably in the extracted growth dimensionality represented by the Avrami exponent. Finally, we outline guidelines for future studies, emphasizing the need for direct voltage monitoring and circuit-aware de-embedding, as well as modeling frameworks that incorporate voltage-dependent nucleation and growth rates based on intrinsic material parameters.

### [76] [Chemical Short-Range Order Regulates Hydrogen Energetics and Hydrogen-Dislocation Interactions in CoNiV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05352)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 化学短程有序（chemical short-range order, CSRO）作为浓合金的关键结构特征，其与氢的耦合机制尚不明确。研究旨在探究CSRO如何调控CoNiV合金（具有强抗氢脆性能）中的氢能学和位错行为。

Method: 开发了Co-Ni-V-H系统的机器学习原子间势函数（machine-learning interatomic potential），用于研究CSRO对氢能学和位错行为的调控机制。

Result: 发现强V中心有序化抑制V-V团簇，显著重塑氢溶解能分布。与化学随机合金相比，有序态具有更高的平均氢溶解能和更少的强结合位点，表明体相氢吸收降低。在部分位错处，氢优先偏聚于拉伸核心区域，表现为浅层可逆陷阱。

Conclusion: 局部化学有序强烈调控氢-位错耦合，为调控浓CoNiV合金中氢辅助变形提供了原子尺度理解。CSRO通过改变氢溶解能分布和位错陷阱特性，影响合金的抗氢脆性能。

Abstract: Chemical short-range order (CSRO) has emerged as a critical structural feature in concentrated alloys, yet its coupling with hydrogen remains an active discussion. Here, we develop a machine-learning interatomic potential for the Co-Ni-V-H system and investigate how CSRO regulates hydrogen energetics and dislocation behavior in CoNiV, an alloy with reported strong resistance to hydrogen embrittlement. We identify strong V-centered ordering that suppresses V-V clustering and significantly reshapes the hydrogen solution landscape. Compared to a chemically random alloy, the ordered state exhibits higher average hydrogen solution energies and a reduced population of strongly binding sites, indicating lower bulk hydrogen uptake. At partial dislocations, hydrogen preferentially segregates to tensile core regions, acting as a shallow, reversible trap with a much weaker effect compared to chemical trapping states. These results demonstrate that local chemical order strongly regulates hydrogen-dislocation coupling and provide an atomistic understanding for tuning hydrogen-assisted deformation in concentrated CoNiV alloys.

### [77] [Rationalizing defect formation energies in metals and semiconductors with semilocal density functionals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05385)
*Jorge Vega Bazantes,Timo Lebeda,Akilan Ramasamy,Kanun Pokharel,Ruiqi Zhang,John Perdew,Jianwei Sun*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究评估了多种密度泛函近似（DFA）方法在材料缺陷形成能计算中的性能，包括八种面心立方金属的单空位缺陷和硅-金刚石半导体中的间隙原子缺陷。研究发现，对于金属体系，局域密度近似（LDA）表现最佳；对于硅半导体，Lebeda-Aschebrock-Kummel（LAK）元广义梯度近似（meta-GGA）精度最高，甚至超过杂化泛函方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 材料缺陷研究对技术应用和新材料设计至关重要。本研究旨在系统评估不同密度泛函近似（density functional approximations）在典型缺陷体系中的计算性能，为材料缺陷形成能的准确预测提供理论指导。

Method: 研究采用多种密度泛函近似方法计算缺陷形成能（defect formation energies），包括局域密度近似（LDA）、Perdew-Burke-Ernzerhof广义梯度近似（PBE GGA）、SCAN和r2SCAN元广义梯度近似（meta-GGAs）、LAK元广义梯度近似以及Heyd-Scuseria-Ernzerhof屏蔽杂化泛函（HSE）。研究对象为八种面心立方（fcc）金属的单空位（monovacancies）和硅-金刚石半导体中的间隙原子（interstitials）。

Result: 对于金属体系，局域密度近似（LDA）相比其他近似方法表现出更好的性能。对于硅半导体，Lebeda-Aschebrock-Kummel（LAK）元广义梯度近似（meta-GGA）展现出卓越的准确性，超越了杂化泛函（hybrid functional）方法，接近计算成本更高的量子蒙特卡洛（Quantum Monte Carlo）方法的结果。通过分析原始结构和缺陷结构中的半局域成分（semilocal ingredients）rs、s和α，研究识别了影响缺陷形成能趋势的关键区域。

Conclusion: 不同密度泛函近似方法在金属和半导体缺陷体系中的性能差异显著，局域密度近似（LDA）在金属体系中表现优异，而LAK元广义梯度近似（meta-GGA）在硅半导体中精度最高。研究结果为理解密度泛函近似的性能差异提供了物理洞察，并为改进密度泛函近似方法指明了方向。

Abstract: The study of defects in materials is of utmost importance for technological applications and the design of new materials. In this work, we analyze the performance of density functional approximations on two prototypical sets of defective systems: monovacancies in eight fcc metals, and interstitials in the semiconductor Si-diamond. Specifically, we compute defect formation energies using the local density approximation, the Perdew-Burke-Ernzerhof generalized gradient approximation, the meta-generalized gradient approximations (meta-GGAs) strongly constrained and appropriately normed (SCAN), its regularized version (r2SCAN), the Lebeda-Aschebrock-Kummel (LAK) meta-GGA, and the Heyd-Scuseria-Ernzerhof screened hybrid functional. For metals, the local density approximation shows better performance compared to the other approximations, whereas for silicon, the meta-generalized gradient approximation Lebeda-Aschebrock-Kummel yields outstand- ing accuracy, surpassing the hybrid functional and approaching the results of more computationally demanding Quantum Monte Carlo methods. To rationalize the different performances, we study the semilocal ingredients rs, s and α in both the pristine and defective structures. We identify critical regions that indicate the observed trends of the defect formation energies and pave the way for improving density functional approximations.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在建立固体中光学活性（optical activity）的从头算多体理论，以克服独立粒子近似和简单局域场修正的局限性，准确描述固体中光学活性的光谱色散特性。

Method: 在GW-BSE框架内发展固体光学活性的从头算多体理论，提出两种互补的介电空间色散（dielectric spatial dispersion）描述形式：激子包络调制（exciton envelope modulation）和激子态求和展开（sum-over-exciton-states expansion）。

Result: 在α-石英中的应用表明，包络调制公式能准确捕捉低频区域的光学活性，而激子态求和公式对再现正确的全频率依赖性至关重要。与独立粒子近似和简单局域场修正的比较进一步凸显了激子多体效应对固体光学活性光谱色散的决定性作用。

Conclusion: 本文发展的GW-BSE框架为固体光学活性提供了可靠的多体理论描述，两种互补公式分别适用于不同频率区域，激子多体效应在塑造固体光学活性光谱色散中起决定性作用。

Abstract: We present an ab initio many-body theory of optical activity in solids within the GW-BSE framework. Dielectric spatial dispersion is formulated in two complementary forms: exciton envelope modulation and sum-over-exciton-states expansion. Our application to $α$-quartz reveals that the envelope-modulated formulation captures the low-frequency region, whereas the sum-over-exciton-states formulation is essential to reproduce the correct full frequency dependence. Comparisons with the independent-particle approximation and simple local-field corrections further highlight the decisive role of excitonic many-body effects in shaping the spectral dispersion of optical activity in solids.

### [79] [A coupled fully kinetic hydrogen transport and ductile phase-field fracture framework for modeling hydrogen embrittlement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05574)
*Abdelrahman Hussein,Yann Charles,Jukka Kömi,Vahid Javaheri*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一个耦合完全动力学氢传输模型与几何相场断裂方法的综合化学-力学框架，用于模拟氢脆（hydrogen embrittlement）现象。该模型成功预测了氢依赖的损伤起始位置变化、多重表面开裂行为、以及加载速率与扩散动力学之间的竞争关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氢脆（hydrogen embrittlement, HE）建模是一个长期存在的工程挑战。当前研究在模拟氢在位错处的偏聚动力学效应、以及延性撕裂与氢致脆性断裂之间的相互作用方面存在空白，需要开发更全面的建模框架。

Method: 研究开发了一个综合化学-力学（chemo-mechanical）框架，将完全动力学氢传输模型（fully kinetic hydrogen transport model）与几何相场断裂方法（geometric phase-field fracture method）相耦合。提出了一种新的驱动力，利用应力三轴性（stress triaxiality）的双曲正切函数，确保塑性耗散仅在拉伸条件下对断裂有贡献，从现象学上代表空穴驱动的延性损伤。

Result: 模型成功预测了氢依赖的损伤起始位置从试样核心向表面的转变。氢在位错处的偏聚（hydrogen segregation at dislocations）被证明对模拟颈缩区域实验观察到的多重表面开裂至关重要。该框架捕捉了加载速率与扩散动力学之间的竞争关系，解决了从高应变速率下的多重周向表面开裂向低速率下中心起始单裂纹的转变。模型还再现了紧凑拉伸试样的实验J阻力曲线（J-resistance curves），显示了从延性撕裂向脆化裂纹的转变。

Conclusion: 该研究开发的综合化学-力学框架成功模拟了氢脆的关键现象，包括氢偏聚动力学效应、损伤起始位置转变、多重开裂行为以及速率依赖的断裂模式转变，为氢脆建模提供了更全面的解决方案。

Abstract: Modeling hydrogen embrittlement (HE) is a long-standing engineering challenge, which has experienced significant developments in recent years. Yet, there is a gap in modeling the effect of the kinetics of hydrogen segregation at dislocations and the resulting interaction between ductile tearing and hydrogen-induced brittle fracture. In this work, a comprehensive chemo-mechanical framework is developed by coupling the fully kinetic hydrogen transport model with the geometric phase-field fracture method. A novel driving force is proposed that utilizes a hyperbolic tangent function of stress triaxiality to ensure that plastic dissipation contributes to fracture only under tensile conditions, phenomenologically representing void-driven ductile damage. The model successfully predicts the hydrogen-dependent shift in damage initiation from the specimen core to the surface. More importantly, hydrogen segregation at dislocations was shown to be crucial for modeling the multiple surface cracking experimentally observed at the necking region. Furthermore, the framework captures the competition between loading rates and diffusion kinetics, resolving the transition from multiple circumferential surface cracking at high strain rates to center-initiated single crack at lower rates. Finally, the model reproduced the experimental J-resistance curves for compact tension specimens, showing the transition from ductile tearing to embrittled crack.

### [80] [A Physics-Informed Chemical Rule for Topological Materials Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05586)
*Xinyu Xu,Arif Ullah,Ming Yang*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一种物理启发的化学规则，在可解释的线性框架中整合成分、轨道和晶体学描述符。该方法明确编码电子填充（electron filling）、空间群对称性（space-group symmetry）和轨道分辨化学环境（orbital-resolved chemical environments），仅使用元素特性将材料的拓扑倾向简化为单一物理可解释分数。

Result: 模型实现了优异的预测性能，同时保持了物理透明度。该方法能够识别传统对称性指标（symmetry indicators）失效的候选拓扑材料，将材料的拓扑倾向简化为单一可解释分数，支持快速高通量评估。

Conclusion: 该框架实现了对复杂材料空间的快速可解释探索，为下一代拓扑和量子材料的智能发现建立了可扩展范式（scalable paradigm）。

Abstract: Topological phases of matter$\unicode{x2013}$comprising both insulators and semimetals$\unicode{x2013}$offer great potential for quantum applications, but identifying new candidates remains challenging due to expensive first-principles simulations and labor-intensive experimental workflows. Here we introduce a physics-informed chemical rule that integrates compositional, orbital and crystallographic descriptors within an interpretable linear framework. By explicitly encoding electron filling, space-group symmetry and orbital-resolved chemical environments, our method overcomes a fundamental limitation of composition-only heuristics$\unicode{x2013}$their inability to distinguish polymorphs with identical stoichiometry but different crystal structures. Using only elemental characteristics, our approach reduces a material's topological propensity to a single, physically interpretable score, enabling rapid and high-throughput assessment. The model achieves superior predictive performance while maintaining physical transparency, and identifies candidate topological materials where conventional symmetry indicators fail. Consequently, our framework enables rapid and interpretable exploration of complex materials spaces, establishing a scalable paradigm for the intelligent discovery of next-generation topological and quantum materials.

### [81] [The effect of Nb and O on the martensitic transformation in the Ti-Nb-O alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05725)
*Kristián Šalata,Dalibor Preisler,Josef Stráský,Jiří Kozlík,Lukáš Horák,Václav Holý*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了铌和氧对Ti-Nb-O合金相稳定性、晶体结构和马氏体相变路径的影响。通过系统实验和先进的XRD取向模拟方法，揭示了铌主要通过稳定β相和改变α"结构对称性来调控相变，而氧则通过间隙原子效应改变相变路径。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 制备了Ti-(8-28)Nb-(0-3)O (at.%)合金系列并在β相区进行固溶处理。采用X射线衍射、电子显微镜和倒易空间映射表征微观结构和晶体学。开发了2D-XRD取向模拟方法，能够区分来自单一原始β晶粒的所有12个晶体学等效α"马氏体变体，并定量评估描述β→α"相变的原子重排参数y。

Result: 铌主要调控α"马氏体演化：增加铌含量稳定β相并使α"结构向更高对称性转变，表现为晶格参数的系统性变化和重排参数y的增加，表明向六方α'相的转变受到抑制。氧则改变相变路径：在低铌含量下抑制ω相形成并促进β→α"转变，而在高铌含量下抑制长程马氏体相变，导致残留β相或竞争性ω相形成。

Conclusion: 铌和氧在Ti-Nb-O合金中发挥不同的相变调控作用：铌主要通过电子浓度效应稳定β相并改变α"结构对称性，而氧作为间隙原子通过局部晶格畸变改变相变路径选择。这些发现为钛合金的相变工程提供了重要理论基础。

Abstract: This study examines the influence of niobium and oxygen on phase stability, crystal structure, and martensitic transformation pathways in Ti-Nb-O alloys. A series of Ti-(8-28)Nb-(0-3)O (at.%) alloys were prepared and solution-treated in the $β$-phase field. Microstructure and crystallography were characterized by X-ray diffraction, electron microscopy, and reciprocal-space mapping.
  A 2D-XRD orientation simulation approach was applied to distinguish all 12 crystallographically equivalent $α"$ martensitic variants originating from a single prior $β$ grain, enabling detailed diffraction analysis. This method further allowed quantitative evaluation of the atomic shuffle parameter y, describing the $β\rightarrowα"$ transformation.
  The results demonstrate that Nb primarily governs $α"$ martensite evolution. Increasing Nb stabilizes the $β$ phase and shifts the $α"$ structure toward higher symmetry, as reflected by systematic changes in lattice parameters and increasing shuffle parameter y, indicating suppression of transformation toward the hexagonal $α'$ phase.
  Oxygen, in contrast, modifies transformation pathways. At lower Nb contents, it suppresses the $ω$ phase formation and promotes $β\rightarrowα"$ transformation, while at higher Nb levels it inhibits long-range martensitic transformation, resulting in retained $β$ or competing $ω$ phase. These effects are attributed to local lattice distortions induced by interstitial oxygen.

</details>


### [82] [Near 13% efficient semitransparent Cu(In,Ga)S2 solar cells with band gap of 1.6 eV on transparent back contact](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05837)
*Kulwinder Kaur,Arivazhagan Valluvar Oli,Michele Melchiorre,Wolfram Hempel,Wolfram Witte,Jan Keller,Susanne Siebentritt*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用In₂O₃:Sn (ITO)作为透明背接触，通过NaF共蒸发或仅依赖玻璃扩散两种方式供应钠；比较不同生长温度（Tsub = 630°C高温与低温）对吸收层质量的影响；分析GaOx界面层的形成及其对背接触的钝化作用。

Abstract: Wide-gap Cu(In,Ga)S2 solar cells with In2O3:Sn (ITO) as transparent back contact are evaluated for the application as top cells in tandem devices. An efficiency of 12.7% is achieved for a semitransparent solar cell with a band gap of 1.6 eV, with sufficient Na diffusion from glass only, allowed by a thin ITO layer. Absorber grown with additional NaF co-evaporation during Cu(In,Ga)S2 growth on thicker ITO show a comparable efficiency of 12%. High temperature growth at Tsub = 630°C enhances overall absorber quality and results in wide-gap absorbers, with photoluminescence quantum yield improved to 1.5 x 10-5, two orders of magnitude higher than absorber grown at low temperature. NaF co-evaporation is effective in suppressing deep defects, thereby reducing non-radiative recombination and enhancing photoluminescence quantum yield further. A GaOx interfacial layer is formed at the rear contact, likely contributing to the passivation of the back contact. With the presence of thick GaOx layer, current blocking effects are visible in the current-voltage curves. On the contrary, a thinner ITO tends to result in thinner GaOx layer and no current blocking is observed.

### [83] [Loss analysis of Low Bandgap (Ag,Cu)(In,Ga)Se2 Solar Cells for Tandem Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05855)
*Francesco Lodola,Sevan Gharabeiki,Maximilian Krause,Shiro Nishiwaki,Romain Carron,Susanne Siebentritt*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究对带隙约1.0 eV的(Ag,Cu)(In,Ga)Se₂串联太阳能电池底部电池进行了完整的损耗分析，发现电压损失主要来自吸收层非辐射复合，填充因子损失源于高二极管因子，电流损失则源于吸收层吸收不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 串联太阳能电池（tandem solar cells）能更高效利用太阳光谱能量，而黄铜矿太阳能电池（chalcopyrite solar cells）因其约1.0 eV的带隙成为高效底部电池的理想选择。为追求更高效率，需要对当前效率约18.5%的电池进行系统损耗分析。

Method: 研究对1.0 eV带隙的(Ag,Cu)(In,Ga)Se₂电池进行完整损耗分析，采用绝对光致发光（absolute photoluminescence）、电致发光（electroluminescence）、JV特性和外量子效率（EQE）测量，分别对吸收层和完整电池进行测试，分析短路电流、开路电压和填充因子的损耗机制。

Result: 电流相关损耗主要源于吸收层吸收损失，只能通过光管理结构（light management structures）缓解。最重要的损耗出现在电压方面，由吸收层非辐射复合（non-radiative recombination）导致；填充因子损失则源于高二极管因子（diode factor）。完整电池的二极管因子显著高于单独吸收层，表明空间电荷区（space charge region）复合的强烈影响。

Conclusion: 对于1.0 eV带隙(Ag,Cu)(In,Ga)Se₂串联太阳能电池底部电池，提升效率的关键在于减少吸收层非辐射复合以改善电压，降低二极管因子以提升填充因子，同时通过光管理结构优化吸收层的光吸收性能。

Abstract: Tandem solar cells can better harness the energy of the solar spectrum. Chalcopyrite solar cells have drawn attention, being the only highly efficient devices with bandgap around 1.0 eV, suitable for bottom cells. In the quest for better efficiencies, we conduct a complete loss analysis of 1.0 eV bandgap (Ag,Cu)(In,Ga)Se2 cells with efficiencies around 18.5%. We perform absolute photoluminescence, electroluminescence, JV and EQE measurements on the absorber and the finished cells to analyze losses of short-circuit current, open-circuit voltage and fill factor. The relevant losses in current are due to absorption losses in the absorber and could only be mitigated by light management structures. But the most significant losses are found in the voltage, due to non-radiative recombination in the absorber, and the fill factor, due to a high diode factor. The diode factor of the cells is significantly higher than in the absorber alone, indicating a strong influence of recombination in the space charge region.

*Bekcy Joseph,Shivam Singh,Nathaniel P. Gallop,Fabian Eller,Alexander Ehm,Julius Brunner,Dietrich R. T. Zahn,Eva Herzig,Boris Rivkin,Yana Vaynzof*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用紫外光电子能谱（ultraviolet photoemission spectroscopy）结合氩气团簇离子束深度剖析（argon gas cluster ion beam depth profiling）技术，探测光降解前后给体（PM6）和受体（Y12）能级的深度分辨演化。同时利用先进的X射线衍射（X-ray diffraction）表征技术分析纳米结构变化。

Abstract: Solvent additive engineering is a common strategy in organic photovoltaic (OPV) fabrication to improve film morphology and enhance device performance by controlling phase-separation kinetics and crystallinity. However, its effect on photostability, particularly with respect to the evolution of the energetic landscape under operational stress, remains unclear. This study investigates the impact of the additive 1-chloronaphthalene (1-CN) on the evolution of the device's energetic landscape in PM6:Y12 bulk heterojunction organic solar cells upon photoaging. Ultraviolet photoemission spectroscopy combined with argon gas cluster ion beam depth profiling is employed to probe the depth-resolved evolution of donor (PM6) and acceptor (Y12) energy levels before and after photodegradation. Our findings show that in additive-free devices, photodegradation leads to a significant 200 meV downward shift in the PM6 highest occupied molecular orbital (HOMO) level, reducing the donor-acceptor HOMO offset and impairing the driving force for hole transfer. As a consequence, the device experiences substantial efficiency loss. On the other hand, the incorporation of 1-CN effectively stabilizes the PM6 HOMO level, preserving adequate driving force for efficient exciton dissociation. Advanced X-ray diffraction characterization reveals more pronounced nanostructural degradation in blends without 1-CN than those with 1-CN upon photoaging. Collectively, these findings identify PM6 as the primary degradation pathway in PM6:Y12 blends and demonstrate that 1-CN enhances device stability by stabilizing PM6 energetics and preserving the nanostructural integrity upon photoaging.

### [85] [ALD Zinc Tin Oxide Buffers for Chalcopyrite Solar Cells: Electrical Barriers and Conduction Band Cliffs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05891)
*Boaz Koren,Francesco Lodola,Zhuangyi Zhou,Trong Tien Le,Kulwinder Kaur,Simon Backes,Michele Melchiorre,Susanne Siebentritt*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了原子层沉积（atomic layer deposition）ZnSnO作为替代传统CdS的缓冲层（buffer layer）在宽禁带硫化物黄铜矿太阳能电池中的应用。通过调控Sn/(Sn+Zn)原子比，分析了缓冲层对电池性能的影响机制，发现锡含量与缓冲层导带最小值（conduction band minimum）呈正相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硫化物黄铜矿Cu(In,Ga)S2因其宽禁带（大于1.5 eV）、优异的光电性能和稳定性，是串联太阳能电池（tandem applications）中有前景的顶电池吸收层（top-cell absorber）。然而，将针对1.0-1.2 eV吸收层优化的器件结构应用于宽禁带吸收层时，需要改进缓冲层设计。

Method: 采用原子层沉积（atomic layer deposition）制备不同组成的ZnSnO缓冲层，通过调控ZnO与SnO循环比例来控制Sn/(Sn+Zn)原子比。使用CuInSe2、Cu(In,Ga)Se2和Cu(In,Ga)S2三种吸收层制备太阳能电池，以便与不同导带最小值（conduction band minimum）进行交叉比较。

Result: 缓冲层变化对电池性能产生两种主要影响：1. 低锡缓冲层降低界面复合（interface recombination）的活化能，减少开路电压，表明存在导带悬崖（cliff）；2. 高锡缓冲层降低所有电池的填充因子（fill factor），并在特定条件下减少短路电流（short circuit current），表明存在电子传输势垒（electron transport barrier）。锡含量与缓冲层导带最小值呈正相关。

Conclusion: 对于不同吸收层，导带悬崖在较低锡含量时出现，而电子传输势垒的影响对于具有较低导带最小值的吸收层更为显著。ZnSnO缓冲层的锡含量调控是实现高效宽禁带太阳能电池的关键参数。

Abstract: Sulfide chalcopyrite, Cu(In,Ga)S2, having wide bandgap (larger than 1.5 eV), favorable optoelectronic properties, and high stability, is a promising top-cell absorber for tandem applications. Adapting device structures optimized for 1.0 - 1.2 eV absorbers to wide bandgap absorbers requires modification of the buffer layer. This work investigates atomic layer deposition of ZnSnO as an alternative buffer layer to conventional CdS. A critical parameter for bufferperformance is the conduction band offsets on both sides of the buffer. To investigate these buffers we electrically characterize solar cells utilizing different compositions of ZnSnO. The Sn/(Sn+Zn) atomic ratio is controlled by the ratio of ZnO to SnO cycles during atomic layer deposition. Solar cells were fabricated utilizing CuInSe2, Cu(In,Ga)Se2, and Cu(In,Ga)S2 absorbers, allowing cross-comparison with a variety of conduction band minimum energies. Buffer variation has two primary effects on cell performance: 1. Low tin buffers decrease the activation energy of interface recombination, reducing open circuit voltage. These observations indicates a cliff, a decrease of the conduction band minimum from absorber to buffer. 2. High tin buffers reduce the fill factor for all measured cells, and reduce the short circuit current under certain conditions. This observation indicates an electron transport barrier, conduction band offsets which limit the transport of electrons across the buffer, in either direction. We conclude that tin content correlates positively with the conduction band minimum of these buffers. Comparing different absorbers, cliffs occurs at lower Sn contents and the effects of barriers are more dramatic for absorbers with lower conduction band minima.

### [86] [Lattice location of ion-implanted 6He in diamond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05951)
*U. Wahl,J. G. Correia,A. Costa,B. Biesmans,G. Magchiels,S. M. Tunhuma,A. Lamelas,A. Vantomme,L. M. C. Pereira,the ISOLDE Collaboration*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在通过实验确定⁶He在金刚石中的晶格位置，验证理论预测中He在金刚石中倾向于占据四面体间隙位的假设。同时探究温度对⁶He位置稳定性的影响，为理解He在金刚石中的长期存在机制提供实验依据。

Method: 采用β发射沟道方法（beta emission channeling method）在CERN的ISOLDE设施进行实验。将30 keV能量的⁶He离子注入单晶人造金刚石样品，温度范围从30°C到800°C。通过比较不同晶向的测量发射沟道图案与多种可能位点的模拟产额，确定⁶He的晶格位置。

Result: 实验结果表明注入的⁶He占据四面体间隙位（tetrahedral interstitial sites），与理论预测一致。800°C注入导致四面体间隙分数下降20%，表明扩散开始发生。估算的He间隙迁移活化能为1.63-2.89 eV，与文献中的理论预测值（1.41 eV、1.97 eV、2.35 eV和2.36 eV）相符。

Conclusion: ⁶He在金刚石中优先占据四面体间隙位，但约2 eV的活化能意味着简单间隙He在地质时间尺度上无法稳定存在。因此，He若要长期保留在金刚石中，必须与材料中的缺陷结合，或以其他形式存在，如其他矿物或液体包裹体，或可能形成小He气泡。

Abstract: We report on the lattice location of the short-lived ion implanted nuclear probe 6He (t1/2=807 ms) in diamond, which was performed using the beta emission channeling method at CERN's ISOLDE facility. 6He was implanted with 30 keV into a single-crystalline artificial diamond sample kept at a temperature ranging from 30 deg C up to 800 deg C. By means of comparing the measured emission channeling patterns along different crystallographic directions with simulated yields for a variety of possible sites, we conclude that the implanted 6He occupies tetrahedral (T) interstitial sites, in agreement with theoretical predictions that T sites should be the preferred position of He in diamond. Implantation at 800 deg C resulted in a drop in the tetrahedral interstitial fraction by 20%, which we interpret as the onset of diffusion, 6He thus being able to change to lattice sites of low crystallographic symmetry, or reach the surface of the sample or escape to the bulk during its lifetime. We estimate the activation energy for interstitial migration of He to be around 1.63-2.89 eV, which agrees with theoretical predictions of 1.41 eV, 1.97 eV, 2.35 eV and 2.36 eV from the literature. Activation energies around 2 eV would mean that simple interstitial He cannot be stable in diamond on geological time scales, thus to remain inside, it should be bound to some defect in the material or exist in another form such as within inclusions of other minerals or liquids, or possibly small He bubbles.

### [87] [Composition design of refractory compositionally complex alloys using machine learning models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05968)
*Tao Liang,Eric A. Lass,Haochen Zhu,Carla Joyce C. Nocheseda,Philip D. Rack,Stephen Puplampu,Dayakar Penumadu,Haixuan Xu*

Method: 采用集成成分设计框架，结合理论引导的机器学习（ML）模型，利用前向顺序特征选择（SFS）确定特征选择，建立成分-力学性能关系，并在九种难熔金属体系中进行验证。

Abstract: Refractory compositionally complex alloys (RCCAs) are considered the next generation high-temperature materials. However, their high-dimensional composition spaces are too large to explore by traditional density functional theory or experimental means, making new RCCA discovery slow and cumbersome. This work has addressed these challenges with an integrated composition design framework that can efficiently and exhaustively explore the relationship between the compositions and two fundamental aspects: 1) the phase stability, including the target body-centered cubic (BCC) phase and its competing phases (hexagonal closed-pack (HCP) structures, Laves and B2 intermetallic phases), and 2) the mechanical properties. This framework is demonstrated with RCCAs within nine refractory metals (Ti, V, Cr, Zr, Nb, Mo, Hf, Ta, and W). Theory-guided machine learning (ML) models were employed to find the composition-mechanical property relationship of RCCAs, where the established theory is used to supplement the yield strength data at ultra-high temperature, and a forward sequential feature selection (SFS) is used to determine feature selection. The resulting ML model for temperature-dependent yield strength was found to have an R_squared value of 0.98 over the entire temperature range (from 0 to 2000 K). The impact of each constituent element on the six key properties is evaluated. The addition of Nb tends to stabilize the BCC phase and the addition of Ti improves the ductility of RCCAs. Combined with all methods involved in this framework, the on-demand designer allows the alloy designers to have all properties for any RCCA compositions and narrow down the composition space by applying custom screening criteria. The output from the predictor and screener provides valuable guidance for our experimental study of RCCAs and accelerates the pace of materials discovery.
