### [88] [Spin-Phonon Renormalization in CrSBr](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06042)
*Jayajeewana N. Ranhili,Chamini S. Pathiraja,Brody Brogdon,John Cenker,Xiadong Xu,Daniel Chica,Xavier Roy,Stefano Agrestini,Mirian Garcia-Fernandez,Ke-Jin Zhou,Yi-De Chuang,Trinanjan Datta,Byron Freelon*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过软X射线光谱实验，首次在CrSBr中直接观测到自旋-声子耦合（spin-phonon coupling）的证据。在低温反铁磁相中观察到布里渊区中心光学声子，其能量随温度升高而消失，这归因于自旋-声子重整化效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在通过实验手段直接探测CrSBr中的自旋-声子耦合现象。先前研究可能缺乏对此类材料中自旋与晶格振动相互作用的直接实验证据，因此需要利用先进的软X射线光谱技术进行验证。

Method: 采用软X射线光谱技术，具体使用Cr L-edge共振非弹性X射线散射（resonant inelastic x-ray scattering, RIXS）分析温度依赖性光谱。结合密度泛函理论（density functional theory）和声子模式计算，识别观测到的振动模式。

Result: 在低温反铁磁相中，沿a轴和b轴分别观测到约43.5 meV和43.1 meV的光学声子模式（σ偏振），以及约42.1 meV的模式（π偏振）。这些被识别为键弯曲光学声子模式，其室温下消失归因于自旋-声子重整化对L-edge电子-声子RIXS机制的影响。

Conclusion: 研究提供了CrSBr中自旋-声子耦合的直接实验证据，揭示了低温反铁磁相中光学声子模式的存在及其温度依赖性行为，为理解此类材料中自旋与晶格相互作用的微观机制提供了重要见解。

Abstract: We provide direct experimental evidence, based on soft x-ray spectroscopy, on the presence of spin-phonon coupling in CrSBr. We analyze the temperature dependent Cr L-edge resonant inelastic x-ray scattering (RIXS) spectrum. Zone-center optical phonons are observed exclusively in the low-temperature antiferromagnetic phase as energy loss features. Under σ-polarization, these modes are located at approximately 43.5 meV and 43.1 meV along the a and b axes, respectively, while a mode at approximately 42.1 meV is observed under π-polarization. Density functional theory and phonon mode calculations identify these as bond-bending optical phonon modes, which arise in the RIXS spectra. Room temperature melting of these low-energy RIXS peaks is explained in terms of a spin-phonon renormalization effect on the L-edge electron-phonon RIXS mechanism.

</details>


### [89] [Large Language Model Assisted Discovery of Optimal Dopants for Enhanced Thermoelectric Performance in CoSb$_3$ Based Skutterudites](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06048)
*Yagnik Bandyopadhyay,Dylan Noel Serrao,Houlong L. Zhuang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统热电材料设计方法效率有限，本研究旨在开发一种数据驱动方法，通过整合大规模文献数据和先进计算技术来加速高性能CoSb₃基方钴矿热电材料的发现过程。

Method: 方法包括：1）从300多篇研究文章中整理包含各种填充元素（filler elements）的方钴矿成分综合数据集；2）利用大语言模型（large language models, LLMs）提取和嵌入成分表示；3）训练回归头（regression head）预测热电优值（thermoelectric figure of merit）；4）使用训练模型提出新型填充成分；5）通过密度泛函理论（density functional theory）和分子动力学（molecular dynamics）计算评估预测候选材料的电导率和热导率。

Result: 基于大语言模型的模型相比依赖原子半径（atomic radii）等元素描述符的传统深度神经网络，实现了显著更低的均方误差损失（mean-squared error losses）。模型成功提出了具有良好热电性能的新型填充成分，并通过量子模拟验证了这些预测候选材料的性能。

Conclusion: 该数据驱动方法展示了结合自然语言处理、机器学习和量子模拟在热电材料设计中的潜力，为加速高性能热电材料的发现提供了有效途径。

Abstract: We present a data-driven approach for accelerating the discovery of high-performance CoSb$_3$-based skutterudites by curating a comprehensive dataset of compositions with various filler elements from over 300 research articles. Leveraging large language models (LLMs), we extract and embed compositional representations, which are then used to train a regression head for predicting thermoelectric figure of merit. Compared to traditional deep neural networks relying on elemental descriptors such as atomic radii, our LLM-based model achieves significantly lower mean-squared error losses. We further employ the trained model to propose novel filler compositions with promising thermoelectric properties. Finally, we support these predicted candidates through density functional theory and molecular dynamics calculations to assess their electrical and thermal conductivity. This data-driven approach demonstrates the potential of combining natural language processing, machine learning, and quantum simulations for thermoelectric materials design.

### [90] [The HTC-Claw: Automating Discovery through High-Throughput Computational Campaigns](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06076)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文提出并实现了HTC-Claw智能高通量计算平台，基于OpenClaw框架构建。关键创新包括：1）基于代理的框架，用于将高层次研究目标自动分解为可并行任务集；2）集成实时分析和报告的闭环执行引擎；3）基于中间结果的自适应决策和工作流迭代能力；4）解耦的模块化架构，将调度系统与功能模块分离，增强可扩展性和鲁棒性。

Result: 案例研究表明，HTC-Claw能够在材料探索中实现从用户意图到最终报告的智能端到端工作流。

Conclusion: HTC-Claw平台通过智能化的任务分解、闭环执行和自适应决策机制，解决了传统高通量计算工具缺乏智能性的问题，为材料发现提供了更高效、更可靠的计算工作流解决方案。

Abstract: With the advancement of the Materials Genome Initiative, high-throughput computation has become central to accelerating materials discovery. However, conventional first-principles workflows are cumbersome and error-prone. Existing high-throughput tools, while efficient at batch job submission, lack intelligence: they cannot automatically plan tasks based on scientific objectives or dynamically adapt workflows according to intermediate results. To address these limitations, this paper proposes and implements HTC-Claw, an intelligent high-throughput computational platform built upon the OpenClaw framework. The key innovations of HTC-Claw are: 1) An agent-based framework for automatic decomposition of high-level research goals into parallelizable task sets; 2) A closed-loop execution engine that integrates real-time analysis and reporting; 3) Adaptive decision-making and workflow iteration capabilities based on intermediate results; and 4) A decoupled, modular architecture that separates the scheduling system from functional modules, enhancing extensibility and robustness. Case studies demonstrate that HTC-Claw enables an intelligent, end-to-end workflow from user intent to final reporting in materials exploration

### [91] [Ultrafast nonlinear Hall effect in black phosphorus](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06083)
*Maciej Dendzik,Andrea Marini,Samuel Beaulieu,Shuo Dong,Tommaso Pincelli,Julian Maklar,R. Patrick Xian,Enrico Perfetto,Martin Wolf,Gianluca Stefanucci,Ralph Ernstorfer,Laurenz Rettig*

TL;DR: 该研究通过飞秒激光脉冲在中心对称黑磷中实现了超快非线性霍尔效应，利用动态对称破缺机制，为选择性光-电流转换开辟了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非线性霍尔效应（nonlinear Hall effect, NHE）通常需要破坏反演对称性，这限制了适用系统范围和应用潜力。本研究旨在探索在中心对称材料中通过动态对称破缺实现NHE的可能性。

Method: 采用飞秒（femtosecond）激光脉冲在中心对称黑磷中实现动态对称破缺，结合动量分辨光电子能谱（momentum-resolved photoemission spectroscopy）和第一性原理计算（ab-initio calculations）分析激发载流子动力学和诱导场。

Result: 超快非线性霍尔效应仅在光偏振方向与扶手椅（armchair）高对称方向对齐时被观测到，且持续时间超过300飞秒，实现了选择性光-电流转换。

Conclusion: 通过飞秒激光脉冲在中心对称材料中实现动态对称破缺，成功观测到超快非线性霍尔效应，为选择性、超快光-电流转换技术提供了新思路。

Abstract: The nonlinear Hall effect (NHE) is a recently discovered member of the Hall effect family in which the Hall voltage shows a nonlinear behavior when a transverse electric field is applied. While the NHE does not require broken time-reversal symmetry, such as that induced by a magnetic field, it requires broken inversion symmetry, which limits the range of suitable systems and potential applications. Here, we demonstrate an ultrafast NHE in centrosymmetric black phosphorus through dynamical symmetry breaking using femtosecond light pulses. We provide a detailed microscopic picture of excited carrier dynamics and induced fields using momentum-resolved photoemission spectroscopy combined with \textit{ab-initio} calculations. The ultrafast NHE is observed exclusively for the light polarization aligned with the armchair high-symmetry direction and persists over 300 fs, which opens new possibilities for selective and ultrafast light-to-current conversions.

### [92] [Key Role of Charge Disproportionation in Monoclinic Semiconducting Fe$_2$PO$_5$, a Room-Temperature d-Wave Altermagnet Candidate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06114)
*Zhen Zhang,Mohd Anas,Andrey Kutepov,Parashu Kharel,Vladimir Antropov*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验与理论结合，确认了β-Fe₂PO₅的单斜结构和半导体带隙，揭示了其电子不稳定性源于DFT+U计算中的电荷不均等分布，最终形成室温d波交变磁体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: β-Fe₂PO₅是一种新兴的室温d波交变磁体（d-wave altermagnet），具有准一维晶体和磁结构、正交自旋输运通道以及大能带自旋劈裂，是下一代自旋电子学和磁子学的有前景材料。然而，其晶体和电子结构仍存在争议。

Method: 采用联合实验与理论研究，结合密度泛函理论（density functional theory）和哈伯德U修正（Hubbard U correction）的DFT+U方法，考虑对称性破缺的能量降低通道——电荷不均等分布（charge disproportionation）和结构畸变。

Result: 研究发现四方金属态存在电子不稳定性，导致电荷不均等分布，进而稳定了单斜畸变并形成窄带隙。若约束四方对称性计算则仅得到金属态。β-Fe₂PO₅被确认为关联和杂化辅助、畸变耦合、电荷不均等分布的半导体。

Conclusion: β-Fe₂PO₅代表了一种罕见的室温半导体d波交变磁体，为研究准一维系统中交变磁性（altermagnetism）与电荷密度波（charge density wave）的共存提供了独特平台。

Abstract: $β$-Fe$_2$PO$_5$ is an emerging room-temperature d-wave altermagnet featuring quasi-one-dimensional crystal and magnetic structures, orthogonal transport channels for opposite spins, and large band spin splitting, which is a promising material for next-generation spintronics and magnonics. However, its crystal and electronic structures remain inconclusive. Here, joint experimental and theoretical studies confirm and explain the appearance of its monoclinic structure and semiconducting band gap. We discover that an electronic instability appears in the tetragonal metallic state as the joint effect of density functional theory and Hubbard U correction (DFT+U) and results in a charge disproportionation, which in turn stabilizes the monoclinic distortion with narrow gap formation. The successful capture of this effect within DFT+U requires accounting for the relevant symmetry-breaking energy-lowering channels -- charge disproportionation and structural distortion; otherwise, tetragonal-symmetry-constrained calculations yield only a metallic state. Fe$_2$PO$_5$ is thus best described as a correlation- and hybridization-assisted, distortion-coupled, charge-disproportionated semiconductor. It represents a rare room-temperature semiconducting d-wave altermagnet. It also provides a rare platform for studying the coexistence of altermagnetism and charge density wave in quasi-one-dimensional systems.

### [93] [Energy-Based Dynamical Models for Neurocomputation, Learning, and Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05042)
*Arthur N. Montanari,Francesco Bullo,Dmitry Krotov,Adilson E. Motter*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本教程综述了控制理论、神经科学和机器学习交叉领域的最新进展，重点介绍了基于能量动力学模型的神经启发计算方法，旨在提升计算系统的可扩展性、鲁棒性和能效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索动力学系统执行计算的新机制，以弥合人工系统与生物系统之间的差距。这些进展旨在改进模型学习与训练、记忆检索、数据驱动控制和优化等任务的可扩展性、鲁棒性和能效。

Method: 方法聚焦于基于能量的动力学模型（energy-based dynamical models），通过梯度流（gradient flows）和能量景观（energy landscapes）编码信息。从连续时间Hopfield网络和玻尔兹曼机（Boltzmann machines）等经典公式出发，扩展到现代发展，包括用于高容量存储的密集关联记忆模型（dense associative memory models）、用于大规模优化的基于振荡器的网络（oscillator-based networks），以及用于复合和约束重构的近端下降动力学（proximal-descent dynamics）。

Result: 教程展示了控制理论原理如何指导下一代神经计算系统的设计，将讨论范围扩展到传统的前馈和基于反向传播的人工智能方法之外。这些方法为模型学习、训练、记忆检索、数据驱动控制和优化提供了新的计算框架。

Conclusion: 结论强调控制理论原理能够引导下一代神经计算系统的设计，推动人工智能研究超越传统的前馈和反向传播方法。基于能量的动力学模型为构建更可扩展、鲁棒和能效的计算系统提供了有前景的途径。

Abstract: Recent advances at the intersection of control theory, neuroscience, and machine learning have revealed novel mechanisms by which dynamical systems perform computation. These advances encompass a wide range of conceptual, mathematical, and computational ideas, with applications for model learning and training, memory retrieval, data-driven control, and optimization. This tutorial focuses on neuro-inspired approaches to computation that aim to improve scalability, robustness, and energy efficiency across such tasks, bridging the gap between artificial and biological systems. Particular emphasis is placed on energy-based dynamical models that encode information through gradient flows and energy landscapes. We begin by reviewing classical formulations, such as continuous-time Hopfield networks and Boltzmann machines, and then extend the framework to modern developments. These include dense associative memory models for high-capacity storage, oscillator-based networks for large-scale optimization, and proximal-descent dynamics for composite and constrained reconstruction. The tutorial demonstrates how control-theoretic principles can guide the design of next-generation neurocomputing systems, steering the discussion beyond conventional feedforward and backpropagation-based approaches to artificial intelligence.

### [94] [Quantitative propagation of chaos and universality for asymmetric Langevin spin glass dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05234)
*Manuel Arnese,Kevin Hu*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该论文研究了独立同分布（i.i.d.）无序（disorder）下朗之万（Langevin）自旋玻璃（spin glass）动力学的淬火（quenched）传播混沌（propagation of chaos）定量估计。在先前高斯无序定性收敛的基础上，证明了在T2不等式（T2 inequality）假设下的期望Wasserstein距离收敛速率和Lipschitz可观测量（observables）的定量集中速率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究仅在高斯无序（Gaussian disorder）情况下建立了单个自旋（spin）分布向确定性McKean-Vlasov极限（McKean-Vlasov limit）的定性收敛。本文旨在获得更精确的定量估计，特别是针对独立同分布无序情况下的收敛速率和集中性质。

Method: 证明采用了耦合论证（coupling argument），并结合了测度集中（concentration of measure）、滤波理论（filtering theory）和马利亚万微积分（Malliavin calculus）的技术。这些方法被用来处理T2不等式假设下的定量分析。

Result: 在无序满足T2不等式的假设下，证明了期望Wasserstein距离（expected Wasserstein distance）的收敛速率，以及Lipschitz可观测量（Lipschitz observables）的定量集中速率（quantitative concentration rates）。这些结果为淬火传播混沌提供了严格的定量界限。

Conclusion: 该研究将自旋玻璃动力学的传播混沌分析从定性收敛扩展到定量估计，为独立同分布无序系统提供了收敛速率和集中性质的严格数学证明，深化了对这类复杂系统动力学行为的理解。

Abstract: We obtain quantitative estimates on quenched propagation of chaos for Langevin spin glass dynamics with i.i.d. disorder. Prior work in the case of Gaussian disorder established the qualitative convergence of the law of a single spin to a deterministic McKean-Vlasov limit. We prove convergence rates in expected Wasserstein distance and quantitative concentration rates for Lipschitz observables under the assumption that the disorder satisfies the T2 inequality. The proof uses a coupling argument, together with techniques from concentration of measure, filtering theory, and Malliavin calculus

### [95] [Well-posedness and Hurst parameter estimation for fluid equations driven by fractional transport noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05910)
*Alexandra Blessing Neamtu,Dan Crisan,Oana Lang*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究了环面上由传输型分数布朗噪声驱动的二维不可压缩涡度方程，建立了存在唯一性定理，并分析了流动的统计特性，特别是推导了Hurst参数的估计器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在分析具有持久性、长程相关强迫的二维湍流模型，该强迫与惯性区标度律和湍流涨落的分数布朗近似一致。模型捕捉了符合物理观测的随机驱动特性。

Method: 核心方法包括适用于一类被积函数（包含但不限于传输型结构）的缝合引理（sewing lemma）版本，该结果为构造Young积分提供了灵活工具。通过不动点论证建立解的存在唯一性。

Result: 建立了Hurst参数H∈(1/2,1)时方程解的存在唯一性，并研究了流动的统计特性。特别地，分析了解的二次泛函，并推导了Hurst参数H的估计器。

Conclusion: 该方法不仅解决了特定涡度方程问题，还为分析更广泛的随机偏微分方程（stochastic partial differential equations）提供了基础框架，缝合引理成为处理此类问题的通用工具。

Abstract: We study a two-dimensional incompressible vorticity equation on the torus driven by transport-type fractional Brownian noise with Hurst parameter $H \in (1/2,1)$. The model captures persistent, long-range correlated forcing consistent with inertial-range scaling laws and fractional Brownian approximations of turbulent fluctuations. A central ingredient of our approach is a version of the sewing lemma adapted to a class of integrands that includes, but is not limited to, transport-type structures. This result provides a flexible tool for constructing the Young integral and serves as a basis for analysing a wider class of stochastic partial differential equations. Using this approach, we establish existence and uniqueness of solutions via a fixed point argument and investigate statistical properties of the flow. In particular, we study quadratic functionals of the solution and derive an estimator for the Hurst parameter $H$.

### [96] [REM universality for linear random energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06122)
*Francesco Concetti,Simone Franchini*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该论文证明了随机哈密顿量序列的能量水平分布收敛于泊松点过程，建立了随机能量模型（REM）的普适性，并改进了稀释REM普适性的采样规模限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究随机哈密顿量序列 $H_n(h,σ)=\sum^n_{i=1}h_i(σ_i-m)$ 的能量水平分布，旨在建立随机能量模型（Random Energy Model, REM）的普适性，并改进先前关于局部REM普适性和稀释REM普适性的结果。

Method: 考虑独立同分布随机变量 $h_1,h_2,\cdots$ 构成的随机哈密顿量，分析当随机采样 $e^{O(n)}$ 个构型时，对应能量水平集合的渐近分布特性。

Result: 证明能量水平集合依分布收敛于具有指数强度测度的泊松点过程（Poisson point process），建立了REM普适性；改进了Ben Arous等人关于稀释REM普适性的结果，将采样规模从 $e^{o(\sqrt{n})}$ 提升到 $e^{O(n)}$；并推导了吉布斯权重（Gibbs weight）的渐近分布。

Conclusion: 该研究强化了随机能量模型的普适性理论，不仅刻画了 $O(1)$ 阶涨落的分布特性，还显著扩展了稀释REM普适性的适用范围，为理解随机系统的统计力学性质提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We consider a sequence of random Hamiltonians $H_n(h,σ)=\sum^n_{i=1}h_i(σ_i-m)$, and study the asymptotic ($n\to \infty$) distribution of the energy levels $(H_n(h,σ))_{σ\in \{-1,1\}^n}$, where $h_1,h_2,\cdots$ are i.i.d. random variables. We show that, when $e^{O(n)}$ configurations are sampled at random, the corresponding collection of energy levels converges in distribution to a Poisson point process with exponential intensity measure. This establishes the Random Energy Model (REM) universality for the present model. Our results strengthen earlier works on local REM universality by characterizing the distribution of $O(1)-$order fluctuations of $H_n$. In addition, we improve upon the REM universality by dilution studied by Ben Arous, Gayrard, Kuptsov by allowing an exponentially large number $e^{O(n)}$ of sampled configurations, instead of $e^{o(\sqrt{n})}$. Finally, we derive the asymptotic distribution of the Gibbs weight.

</details>


<div id='hep-ex'></div>

# hep-ex [[Back]](#toc)

### [97] [Measurement of charged-particle production in $\sqrt{s_\text{NN}}=9.62$ TeV proton-oxygen collisions as a probe of cosmic-ray air showers with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05512)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文报告了ATLAS探测器在质心能量$\sqrt{s_\text{NN}}=9.62$ TeV下质子-氧核碰撞中带电粒子产生的测量结果，为宇宙线空气簇射建模提供了精确数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究质子-氧核相互作用对于改进宇宙线空气簇射（cosmic-ray air showers）的建模至关重要，这在天体粒子物理学（astroparticle physics）中具有重要意义。

Method: 使用ATLAS探测器在$\sqrt{s_\text{NN}}=9.62$ TeV质心能量下进行测量，对应634 $\mu$b$^{-1}$积分亮度，从2.46亿个选定事件中分析横向动量$p_\text{T}>500$ MeV和赝快度$|η|<2.5$的径迹。

Result: 测得质子-氧核基准截面为$σ_\text{fid.}^{p\text{O}}=396 \pm 6~(\text{exp.}) \pm 9~(\text{lumi.})~\text{mb}$，外推的非弹性质子-空气截面为$σ^{p+\text{air}}_\text{inel.} = 406 \pm 6~(\text{exp.}) \pm 9~(\text{lumi.}) \pm 28~(\text{th.})~\text{mb}$；带电粒子多重数、$p_\text{T}$和$η$分布的测量精度比强子相互作用模型间的差异高一个数量级。

Conclusion: 这些精确测量结果显著改进了宇宙线空气簇射的建模能力，为天体粒子物理学研究提供了重要实验基础。

Abstract: This Letter presents a measurement of prompt charged-particle production in proton-oxygen interactions at $\sqrt{s_\text{NN}}=9.62$ TeV center-of-mass energy with the ATLAS detector, corresponding to 634 $μ$b$^{-1}$ of integrated luminosity. A total of 246 million selected events have at least one track with transverse momentum $p_\text{T}> 500$ MeV and pseudorapidity $|η|<2.5$. The measured fiducial proton-oxygen cross section is $σ_\text{fid.}^{p\text{O}}=396 \pm 6~(\text{exp.}) \pm 9~(\text{lumi.})~\text{mb}$ and the extrapolated inelastic proton-air cross section is $σ^{p+\text{air}}_\text{inel.} = 406 \pm 6~(\text{exp.}) \pm 9~(\text{lumi.}) \pm 28~(\text{th.})~\text{mb}$. Measurements of charged-particle multiplicity, $p_\text{T}$, and $η$ distributions are an order-of-magnitude more precise than differences between hadronic-interaction models. These results enable improved modeling of cosmic-ray air showers, which is important for astroparticle physics.

</details>

Zhuo,D. Zuliani,G. Zunica*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究通过一种新颖的模型无关方法，在B介子衰变中测量CKM角γ和相关的强相位参数，结合BESIII和LHCb实验数据，获得了迄今为止最精确的单次测量结果γ = (71.3±5.0)°。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在精确测量CKM角γ（CKM angle γ）和相关的强相位参数，这对于理解标准模型中的电荷宇称破坏（CP violation）机制至关重要。采用模型无关方法可以避免理论模型假设带来的系统不确定性。

Method: 使用一种新颖的模型无关方法，分析${B^{\pm}\rightarrow D(\rightarrow K^{0}_{\rm S} h^{\prime+}h^{\prime-}) h^{\pm}}$衰变过程，其中$h^{(\prime)} \equiv π, K$。同时分析BESIII实验在BEPCII上收集的8 fb$^{-1}$电子-正电子对撞数据，以及LHCb实验在LHC上收集的9 fb$^{-1}$质子-质子对撞数据。通过基于D介子衰变相空间振幅变化的逐事例加权来增强对CP破坏可观测量（CP-violating observables）的灵敏度。

Result: CKM角γ被确定为γ = (71.3±5.0)°，这是迄今为止最精确的单次测量结果。该方法成功结合了不同实验的数据集，并提高了对CP破坏参数的测量精度。

Conclusion: 该研究通过创新的模型无关方法和联合数据分析技术，实现了对CKM角γ的高精度测量，为理解标准模型中的电荷宇称破坏机制提供了重要实验依据。这种同时利用不同对撞机数据的方法展示了多实验协作在粒子物理测量中的优势。

Abstract: A measurement of the CKM angle $γ$ and related strong-phase parameters is performed using a novel, model-independent approach in ${B^{\pm}\rightarrow D(\rightarrow K^{0}_{\rm S} h^{\prime+}h^{\prime-}) h^{\pm}}$ decays, where $h^{(\prime)} \equiv π, K$. The analysis uses a joint data sample of electron-positron collisions collected by the BESIII experiment at the Beijing Electron-Positron Collider II during 2010--2011 and 2021--2022, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 8 fb$^{-1}$, and proton-proton collisions collected by the LHCb experiment at the Large Hadron Collider during 2011--2018, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 9 fb$^{-1}$. The two datasets are analyzed simultaneously by applying per-event weights based on the amplitude variation over the $D$-decay phase space to enhance the sensitivity to $C\!P$-violating observables. The CKM angle $γ$ is determined to be $γ= (71.3\pm 5.0)^{\circ}$, which constitutes the most precise single measurement to date.

</details>

Yang,Y. Yang,Y. Yang,Z. Yang,Z. Yang,H. Yeung,H. Yin,X. Yin,C. Y. Yu,J. Yu,X. Yuan,Y Yuan,J. A. Zamora Saa,M. Zavertyaev,M. Zdybal,F. Zenesini,C. Zeng,M. Zeng,S. H Zeng,C. Zhang,D. Zhang,J. Zhang,L. Zhang,R. Zhang,S. Zhang,S. L. Zhang,Y. Zhang,Y. Z. Zhang,Z. Zhang,Y. Zhao,A. Zhelezov,S. Z. Zheng,X. Z. Zheng,Y. Zheng,T. Zhou,X. Zhou,V. Zhovkovska,L. Z. Zhu,X. Zhu,X. Zhu,Y. Zhu,V. Zhukov,J. Zhuo,D. Zuliani,G. Zunica*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文通过联合分析BESIII和LHCb实验数据，采用无模型独立方法测量CKM角γ，获得迄今为止最精确的结果γ = (71.3 ± 5.0)°。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在精确测量CKM矩阵中的CP破坏角γ，这是粒子物理学标准模型（Standard Model）中的关键参数。通过结合不同实验的数据，可以提高测量精度并验证理论预测。

Method: 采用一种新颖的无模型独立（model-independent）方法，联合分析BESIII实验的电子-正电子对撞数据和LHCb实验的质子-质子对撞数据。利用BESIII的量子关联D介子系统测量强相位参数，同时从LHCb的B±衰变中提取CP破坏可观测量。

Result: 通过联合拟合两个数据集，同时确定CP破坏可观测量和强相位参数，得到γ = (71.3 ± 5.0)°的测量结果。该结果是迄今为止最精确的γ测量值，与先前测量和世界平均值一致。

Conclusion: 本研究成功实现了对CKM角γ的高精度测量，验证了标准模型的CP破坏机制。联合分析方法展示了多实验数据协同的优势，为未来更精确的CP破坏研究提供了有效途径。

Abstract: A measurement of the CKM angle $γ$ is performed by applying a novel, unbinned, model-independent approach to datasets of electron-positron collisions collected by the BESIII experiment and proton-proton collisions by the LHCb experiment, corresponding to integrated luminosities of 8 fb$^{-1}$ and 9 fb$^{-1}$, respectively. The $C\!P$-violating phase $γ$ is determined from ${B^{\pm}\rightarrow D(\rightarrow K_{\rm S}^{0} h^{\prime+}h^{\prime-}) h^{\pm}}$ decays in LHCb data, where $h^{(\prime)}$ is either a pion or kaon, while the corresponding strong-phase parameters are measured using doubly tagged ${D\rightarrow K_{\rm S/L}^0 h^{\prime+} h^{\prime-}}$ decays in the quantum-correlated $D\overline{D}$ system present in BESIII data. A joint fit to both datasets, which allows for a simultaneous determination of the associated $C\!P$-violating observables and strong-phase parameters, yields ${γ= (71.3\pm 5.0)^{\circ}}$. The result is the most precise to date and consistent with previous measurements and world averages.

</details>


### [100] [Reactor Antineutrino Oscillations and Geoneutrinos in SNO+](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05746)
*William Parker*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: SNO+探测器利用加拿大地下实验室位置，通过分析2022-2025年数据，精确测量了中微子振荡参数Δm²₂₁，并首次在西半球测量了地球中微子通量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SNO+作为多用途液体闪烁体中微子探测器，旨在利用三个大型核反应堆（基线距离240-350公里）精确测量中微子振荡参数Δm²₂₁和θ₁₂，同时探索地球中微子（geoneutrino）通量测量。

Method: 采用谱分析方法，同时拟合Δm²₂₁、θ₁₂、反应堆反中微子通量、本底速率及相关系统误差。数据采集时间为2022年5月至2025年7月，对应有效运行时间685天。

Result: 获得Δm²₂₁ = (7.93⁺⁰·²¹₋₀·₂₄) × 10⁻⁵ eV²的测量结果，与KamLAND和JUNO的长基线反应堆反中微子测量结果一致。首次在西半球测量地球中微子通量为49⁺¹³₋₁₂ TNU，与地质模型预测相符。

Conclusion: SNO+成功实现了对中微子振荡参数Δm²₂₁的精确测量，验证了现有长基线实验结果的一致性，并开创性地完成了西半球地球中微子通量的首次测量，为地球物理学研究提供了新数据。

Abstract: SNO+ is a multipurpose liquid-scintillator neutrino detector located 2 km underground at SNOLAB, Canada. Three large nuclear reactors at baselines of 240-350 km allow a precise measurement of the neutrino oscillation parameter $Δm^2_{21}$ and, to a lesser extent, $θ_{12}$. A spectral analysis is performed, simultaneously fitting $Δm^2_{21}$, $θ_{12}$, the reactor antineutrino flux, background rates, and associated systematics. Using data collected between May 2022 and July 2025, corresponding to a livetime of 685 days, a value of $Δm^2_{21} = (7.93^{+0.21}_{-0.24}) \times 10^{-5}$ eV$^2$ is obtained. This result is compatible with other long-baseline reactor antineutrino measurements by KamLAND and JUNO. SNO+ has also made the first measurement of the geoneutrino flux in the Western Hemisphere, measuring $49^{+13}_{-12}$ TNU, in agreement with predictions from geological models.

</details>


### [101] [Search for soft unclustered energy patterns produced in association with a W or Z boson in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05996)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究首次在LHC上探索了与W或Z玻色子伴随产生并通过软非团簇能量模式（SUEP）衰变的希格斯玻色子，未发现超出标准模型背景预期的显著信号，并对SUEP模型的参数范围设置了产生截面上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索希格斯玻色子通过软非团簇能量模式（soft unclustered energy pattern, SUEP）衰变的新物理过程，这种衰变模式在先前研究中尚未被充分探索，特别是在与W或Z玻色子伴随产生的背景下。

Method: 分析基于LHC在2016-2018年收集的质子-质子对撞数据，对应积分亮度为138 fb⁻¹。首次探索了包含轻子型W或Z玻色子衰变与大量低动量带电粒子的末态，针对SUEP模型的不同参数范围进行了系统研究。

Result: 结果显示未发现超出标准模型背景预期的显著过剩信号。研究对希格斯玻色子衰变为SUEP的产生截面设置了上限，这些上限覆盖了SUEP模型的一系列参数范围。

Conclusion: 该分析为希格斯玻色子通过SUEP衰变的新物理过程提供了首次实验约束。提供的材料将有助于后续对结果的进一步解释，并为相关理论研究提供实验依据。

Abstract: A search for a Higgs boson produced in association with a W or Z boson and decaying via a soft unclustered energy pattern (SUEP) is presented. The analysis is based on proton-proton collision data corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 138 fb$^{-1}$ collected between 2016 and 2018 at the LHC. Final states with a leptonic W or Z boson decay associated with a high multiplicity of low-momentum charged particles are explored for the first time. The results show no significant excess over the standard model background expectation. Limits are set on the production cross section of a Higgs boson that decays to a SUEP, for a range of parameters of the SUEP model. Material is provided to facilitate further interpretation of the results.

</details>

*E. Aprile,J. Aalbers,K. Abe,M. M. Abu Rmeileh,M. Adrover,S. Ahmed Maouloud,L. Althueser,B. Andrieu,E. Angelino,D. Antón Martin,S. R. Armbruster,F. Arneodo,L. Baudis,M. Bazyk,V. Beligotti,L. Pellegrini,R. Peres,J. Pienaar,M. Pierre,G. Plante,T. R. Pollmann,F. Pompa,A. Prajapati,L. Principe,J. Qin,D. Ramírez García,A. Ravindran,A. Razeto,R. Singh,L. Sanchez,J. M. F. dos Santos,I. Sarnoff,G. Sartorelli,M. T. Schiller,P. Schulte,H. Schulze Eißing,M. Schumann,L. Scotto Lavina,M. Selvi,F. Semeria,F. N. Semler,P. Shagin,S. Shi,H. Simgen,Z. Song,A. Stevens,C. Szyszka,A. Takeda,Y. Takeuchi,P. -L. Tan,D. Thers,G. Trinchero,C. D. Tunnell,K. Valerius,S. Vecchi,S. Vetter,G. Volta,B. von Krosigk,C. Weinheimer,D. Wenz,C. Wittweg,V. H. S. Wu,Y. Xing,D. Xu,Z. Xu,M. Yamashita,J. Yang,L. Yang,J. Ye,M. Yoshida,L. Yuan,G. Zavattini,Y. Zhao,M. Zhong,T. Zhu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: XENONnT实验通过6.77吨×年的曝光量，首次以3.3σ置信度观测到太阳^8B中微子引起的相干弹性中微子-原子核散射（CEνNS），并利用该数据集对轻暗物质和超出标准模型物理进行了约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在利用XENONnT实验探测相干弹性中微子-原子核散射（coherent elastic neutrino-nucleus scattering, CEνNS），这是首次从太阳^8B中微子中观测到该过程。同时，研究试图在"中微子雾（neutrino fog）"背景下探索轻暗物质（light dark matter）信号，并测量弱混合角（weak mixing angle）以检验标准模型。

Method: 研究采用XENONnT实验装置，通过6.77吨×年的曝光量收集数据。该方法利用液态氙时间投影室探测低能核反冲信号，以区分中微子散射和可能的暗物质相互作用。数据分析包括对太阳^8B中微子通量的推断、轻暗物质搜索以及弱混合角的测量。

Result: 实验以3.3σ置信度观测到CEνNS信号，推断太阳^8B中微子通量为(5^{+3}_{-2})×10⁶ cm⁻²s⁻¹，与先前测量一致。在^8B中微子雾背景下未发现轻暗物质证据，且灵敏度随曝光量增加呈现收益递减现象。曝光量增加93%仅使5 GeV/c²弱相互作用大质量粒子-核子截面的中值灵敏度提升10%。在~0.02 GeV/c动量转移下测量了弱混合角。

Conclusion: 该研究首次从太阳^8B中微子中观测到CEνNS过程，验证了标准模型预测。在现有中微子背景下，轻暗物质搜索面临灵敏度瓶颈。数据集为低能区弱混合角测量和超出标准模型物理的约束提供了重要实验依据。

Abstract: We report a 3.3 $σ$ measurement of coherent elastic neutrino-nucleus scattering from solar $^8$B neutrinos using a 6.77 t$\times$yr exposure from the XENONnT experiment, inferring a solar $^8$B neutrino flux of $(5_{-2}^{+3})\times 10^6\,\mathrm{cm}^{-2}\mathrm{s}^{-1}$, consistent with previous measurements. In the presence of the $^8$B "neutrino fog", we find no evidence for light dark matter, and observe diminishing returns in sensitivity with increasing exposure. A 93% increase in exposure from the previous search improves the median sensitivity to 5 GeV/$c^2$ weakly interacting massive particles-nucleon cross section by 10%. The dataset was also used to measure the weak mixing angle at $\sim$ 0.02 GeV/$c$ momentum transfer and constrain physics beyond the Standard Model.

# physics.class-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [103] [Induced-current magnetophoresis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04945)
*V. Kumaran*

Main category: physics.class-ph

TL;DR: 当导电非磁性粒子处于空间变化且振荡的外加磁场中时，会产生稳定的力和力矩，这些效应与粒子形状相关，并导致垂直于磁场方向的浓度波动放大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究导电非磁性粒子在空间变化振荡磁场中的行为，分析涡流（eddy current）产生的洛伦兹力（Lorentz force）及其对粒子的稳定力和力矩效应。

Method: 通过理论分析推导球形和细长杆状粒子在振荡磁场中的力和力矩表达式，考虑磁场空间梯度（spatial gradient）和渗透深度（penetration depth）的影响。

Result: 球形粒子受到与$- μ_0 R^3 \mathcal{G} \cdot \mathcal{H}$成正比的稳定力；细长杆受到与$- μ_0 R^2 L (\mathcal{G} \cdot \mathcal{H} - \tfrac{1}{2} (\mathcal{G} \cdot \hat o)(\mathcal{H} \cdot \hat o))$成正比的稳定力，以及使杆沿磁场方向排列的力矩。粒子相互作用表现为粒子数密度方程中的各向异性扩散项，扩散系数在垂直于磁场平面内为负值。

Conclusion: 空间变化振荡磁场对导电粒子产生稳定力和力矩，这些效应依赖于粒子形状和方向。粒子相互作用导致垂直于磁场方向的浓度波动被放大，表明系统存在不稳定性。

Abstract: When an electrically conducting non-magnetic particle is subjected to a spatially varying and oscillating applied magnetic field of amplitude $\mathcal{H} + \mathcal{G} \cdot x$ and frequency $ω$, an oscillating eddy current is induced. The Lorentz force density, the cross product of the current density and the magnetic field, consists of a steady component and a component with frequency $2 ω$. If there is a spatial variation in the applied field, there is a steady force on a sphere of radius $R$ proportional to $- μ_0 R^3 \mathcal{G}  \cdot \mathcal{H} $, and a steady force on a thin rod of radius $R$ and length $L$ proportional to $- μ_0 R^2 L (\mathcal{G}  \cdot \mathcal{H}  - \tfrac{1}{2} (\mathcal{G}  \cdot \hat o)(\mathcal{H}  \cdot \hat o))$, where $μ_0$ is the magnetic permeability. There is torque proportional to $μ_0 R^2 L (\hat o \times \mathcal{H} ) (\hat o \cdot \mathcal{H} )$ on a thin rod which tends to align the rod direction of the magnetic field. The coefficients in the force and torque expressions are functions of the dimensionless ratio of the radius and the penetration depth of the magnetic field, $βR = \sqrt{μ_0 ωκR^2}$, where $κ$ is the electrical conductivity. It is shown that the effect of particle interactions can be expressed as an anisotropic diffusion term in the equation for the particle number density. The diffusion coefficient is negative, and concentration fluctuations are amplified, in the plane perpendicular to the magnetic field.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.mes-hall'></div>

# cond-mat.mes-hall [[Back]](#toc)

### [104] [Predicting spin-orbit coupling in hole spin qubit arrays with vision-transformer-based neural networks on a generalized Hubbard model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05052)
*Jacob R. Taylor,Katharina Laubscher,Sankar Das Sarma*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于神经网络的方法，能够从标准电荷稳定性图中预测空穴量子点阵列的有效自旋轨道耦合强度，实现了对自旋翻转隧穿振幅的高精度预测（R²≈0.94）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子点阵列中自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling, SOC）的精确表征对于空穴自旋量子比特（hole spin qubit）的自动化表征至关重要。传统方法难以在未知其他系统参数的情况下准确预测有效SOC强度。

Method: 采用基于神经网络（neural-network-based）的机器学习方法，通过数值模拟的电荷稳定性图（charge stability diagrams）进行训练。研究基于广义自旋轨道耦合哈伯德模型（generalized spin-orbit coupled Hubbard model），考虑了包括随机位点和键相关无序在内的所有系统参数。

Result: 神经网络能够高保真度地预测SOC诱导的自旋翻转隧穿振幅（spin-flip tunneling amplitudes），从而确定有效SOC强度（R²≈0.94）。该方法还能准确预测其他哈伯德模型参数，即使在所有参数未知的情况下也能保持高精度。

Conclusion: 基于神经网络的方法可作为空穴自旋量子比特阵列自动化表征的强大工具，为量子点系统的参数提取提供了高效可靠的解决方案。

Abstract: We introduce a neural-network-based machine learning method to predict the effective spin-orbit coupling (SOC) strength in hole quantum dot arrays from standard charge stability diagrams. Specifically, we study a $2\times 2$ Ge hole quantum dot array described by a generalized spin-orbit coupled Hubbard model that incorporates random site- and bond-dependent disorder in all system parameters, including onsite potentials, Coulomb interaction strengths, interdot tunneling amplitudes, as well as the direction and angle of the SOC-induced spin rotations accompanying interdot tunneling. We train the neural network on numerically simulated charge stability diagrams from nearest-neighbor pairs of quantum dots for different chemical potentials and out-of-plane magnetic fields, and show that this enables us to predict the SOC-induced spin-flip tunneling amplitudes -- and, thus, the effective SOC strength -- with high fidelity ($R^2\approx 0.94$) even when all other Hubbard model parameters are unknown. Furthermore, our neural network can also predict the other Hubbard model parameters with high fidelity, demonstrating that neural-network-based approaches can be a powerful tool for the automated characterization of hole spin qubit arrays.

</details>

We investigate structures consisting of up to three layered, coated heterostructure of two-dimensional (2D) materials with a dielectric medium or vacuum interface. The dielectric media serves to inhibit charge transfer between layers for the case when a pair of 2D layers serve as coatings for a dielectric film. Our results revise the established picture for the dispersion equation for two layers of reduced dimensionality surrounded by dielectric media. An impinging electromagnetic field incident on the surface leads to Coulomb coupled plasma excitations in the structure which are yielded by the SRF. This is achieved by employing Maxwell's equations and linear response theory. We use these results to investigate the plasmonic properties of tilted semi-Dirac materials both analytically and numerically. Closed-form analytical expressions are derived for the plasmon dispersions in the long wavelength limit for single and double layers. We numerically obtain density plots of the loss functions and observe anisotropic behavior in different momentum directions. For the cases when there are two or three layers, we observe two plasmon branches corresponding to in-phase and out-of-phase charge density oscillations, where the in-phase optical modes have higher intensity than the out-of-phase acoustic modes. Possible applications include durable protection coatings providing UV resistance, chemical protection and improving upon traditional ceramic coatings.

### [106] [Controlled topological dilution drives cooperative glassy dynamics in artificial spin ice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05132)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过在人工方形自旋冰（artificial square spin ice）中引入随机移除（random decimation）的受控无序，系统性地从随机位置移除纳米磁体，从而改变顶点拓扑（vertex topology）并逐步增强自旋网络中的受挫（frustration）。使用基于同步辐射的光发射电子显微镜（photoemission electron microscopy）和时间分辨的温度依赖成像技术进行分析。

Abstract: It has long been known that disorder, perturbing the energy landscape of magnetic systems, can introduce glassy dynamics. However, the controlled role of increasing disorder in driving glass formation remains difficult to isolate in naturally occurring materials. Artificial spin ice offers a unique model platform in which geometry, interactions, and disorder can be engineered at the nanoscale. Here, we investigate the impact of controlled disorder introduced through random decimation in artificial square spin ice. By systematically removing nanomagnets from random sites, we modify the vertex topology and progressively increase frustration in the spin network. Synchrotron-based photoemission electron microscopy reveals that decimation enhances the population of higher energy vertices and increases the configurational entropy of the system. Time-resolved temperature-dependent imaging further shows the emergence of slow cooperative dynamics at higher decimation, characterized by aging, a finite Edwards--Anderson order parameter, and enhanced dynamical heterogeneity quantified by the four-point susceptibility. The relaxation dynamics transition from thermally activated behavior at low decimation to Vogel--Fulcher--type freezing at higher decimation. These results demonstrate that random decimation drives artificial spin ice from long-range order to a glass-like magnetic state, establishing artificial spin systems as a tunable platform for studying glassy dynamics in frustrated matter.

### [107] [Edge universality in Floquet sideband spectra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05244)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于线性探测链与Floquet散射矩阵之间的桥梁关系，通过相称门控（commensurate gating）分离单体关联函数的单一相干阶块，推导出离散贝塞尔核的精确表达式。

Result: 在任意驱动振幅下，尖锐费米边处的出射边带占据由离散贝塞尔核精确描述；大振幅极限下该核在A^{1/3}尺度上收敛于随机矩阵理论的Airy核，导致光辅助散粒噪声斜率偏离其高偏压平台的行为由Airy核对角元决定。

Abstract: We show that, for non-interacting fermions under a monochromatic phase drive (Tien--Gordon regime), the outgoing sideband occupations at a sharp Fermi edge are governed by the discrete Bessel kernel -- an exact result at any drive amplitude~$A$. In the large-amplitude regime the edge of this kernel converges, on the $A^{1/3}$ scale, to the Airy kernel of random matrix theory. This universality has a direct transport consequence: the deficit of the photo-assisted shot-noise slope from its high-bias plateau collapses onto the Airy-kernel diagonal. The derivation rests on a bridge between the linear detection chain and the Floquet scattering matrix: commensurate gating isolates a single coherence-order block of the one-body correlator. We identify the crossover temperature below which the Airy scaling is sharp, extend the analysis to biased two-terminal occupations, and argue that multi-tone drives make Pearcey-kernel cusps accessible in Floquet--Sambe space.

Method: 通过计算系统的温度-贝里通量（temperature-versus-Berry flux）相图，分析有限角动量激子态的形成条件。随后转向多层菱面体石墨烯（multilayer rhombohedral graphene）模型，考察三角畸变（trigonal warping）效应。

Abstract: Van der Waals (vdW) materials provide a rich platform for exploring the interplay of interactions, topology, and paired-electron phases. By computing the temperature-versus-Berry flux phase diagram of the system, we find parameter ranges where finite angular momentum excitons are favored, including chiral states. Strikingly, the condensed angular momentum channel evolves with Berry flux, revealing a pairing problem with no analogue in a hydrogen atom in a uniform magnetic field, where angular momentum states never cross. We then turn to a model of multilayer rhombohedral graphene and examine the effects of trigonal warping. Once continuous rotational symmetry is broken, excitons mix multiple angular momenta, and for a range of parameters we find a variety of linear combination of angular momenta ($s, p, f$ and $g$) in the ground state. ### [111] [Nonlinear thermal gradient induced magnetization in $d^{\prime }$, $g^{\prime }$ and $i^{\prime }$ altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05454)
*Motohiko Ezawa*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究证明在无线性温度梯度分量情况下，特定类型的交替磁体（altermagnets）中可通过二阶非线性温度梯度诱导磁化，其中d'波、g'波、i'波交替磁体产生响应，而d波、g波、i'波则无此响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在无任何线性分量的非线性温度梯度作用下是否能诱导磁化，这是一个高度非平凡的问题。研究旨在通过具体实例验证这种响应是否确实存在。

Method: 分析不同波对称性的交替磁体（altermagnets）的自旋分裂能带结构：d波、g波、i'波由k^N_X sin N_X φ描述，而d'波、g'波、i'波由k^N_X cos N_X φ描述。研究这些系统在二阶非线性温度梯度下的响应特性。

Abstract: It is a highly nontrivial question whether a magnetization can be induced by applying a nonlinear temperature gradient in the absence of any linear component. In this work, we address this issue and provide explicit examples demonstrating that such a response can indeed arise. The spin-split band structures of $d$-wave, $g$-wave, $i$-wave altermagnets are characterized by $k^{N_{X}}\sin N_{X}φ$, where $N_{X}=2,4$ and $6$, respectively. In contrast, the corresponding $d^{\prime }$-wave, $g^{\prime } $-wave, $i^{\prime }$-wave altermagnets are described by $k^{N_{X}}\cos N_{X}φ$. We show that a finite magnetization is induced in the $d^{\prime }$-wave, $g^{\prime }$-wave, $i^{\prime }$-wave altermagnets under a second-order nonlinear temperature gradient, whereas no such response occurs in the $d$-wave, $g$-wave, $i$-wave altermagnets. This constitutes the leading-order contribution because the linear response is forbidden by inversion symmetry. Furthermore, we derive analytic expressions for the induced magnetization in the high-temperature regime. We also demonstrate that no analogous nonlinear thermal response appears in $p$-wave, $f$-wave, $p^{\prime }$-wave and $f^{\prime }$-wave odd-parity magnets.

Method: 在1.37-2.48 eV能量范围内进行线性偏振反射率测量和扫描光电流测量，以揭示二向色响应。通过空间分辨光电流映射分析光电流对晶体学轴的依赖性。

Conclusion: CrPS₄被确立为具有强线性二向色性和室温偏振敏感光响应的高度各向异性二维半导体，是窄带偏振光电探测器、各向异性光传输以及未来二维自旋电子与磁光器件的理想平台。

Abstract: The crystalline and optical anisotropy of low-symmetry two-dimensional (2D) materials can enable strong dichroic responses, enhancing polarization contrast for photonic and optoelectronic devices. Here, we unveil pronounced optical and optoelectronic anisotropy in chromium thiophosphate CrPS$_4$ arising from the strong coupling between light polarization and its intrinsic crystal symmetry. Linearly polarized reflectivity and scanning photocurrent measurements in the 1.37-2.48 eV range reveal a robust dichroic response. The linear dichroism in reflection RLD reaches ~50, while in photocurrent PCLD it increases to ~60, with a sign reversal of the RLD between 1.6-1.8 eV, enabling strong narrow-band polarization contrast at room temperature. We attribute these anisotropic responses to the interaction between polarized light and Cr$^{3+}$ d-orbital T$_1$ and T$_2$ transitions. Spatially resolved photocurrent mapping further shows that the photocurrent is strongly dependent on the crystallographic axis: a 3-fold enhancement is obtained along the b-axis compared to the a-axis, yielding a clear 180° modulation of photoresponse across different contact orientations. Together, our findings establish CrPS$_4$ as a highly anisotropic 2D semiconductor with strong linear dichroism and polarization-sensitive photoresponse at room temperature. These characteristics highlight CrPS4 as a promising platform for narrow-band polarized photodetectors, anisotropic photo-transport, and future 2D spintronic and magneto-optical devices.

In contrast to conventional chiral or helical edge modes, FMEBs form isolated, momentum-separated counterpropagating Majorana modes detached from the bulk continuum. We identify a minimal mechanism for their emergence via anisotropic Wilson masses in a two-band Bogoliubov-de Gennes (BdG) model, and demonstrate their microscopic realization in a quantum anomalous Hall (QAH) insulator proximitized by a $d$-wave superconductor. Using nonequilibrium Green's function (NEGF) simulations, we uncover clear transport fingerprints: a quantized total thermal conductance in two-terminal devices, and a robust half-quantized plateau in four-terminal geometries that cleanly distinguishes FMEBs from chiral $\mathcal{N}= \pm 2$ QAH phases. Our findings establish FMEBs as an experimentally accessible route toward helical-like Majorana transport in systems without time-reversal symmetry, with direct implications for topological quantum computation.

Abstract: Chiral magnets host topologically protected spin textures whose nonequilibrium dynamics are crucial in phase transitions and domain evolution, yet ultrafast defect-mediated processes remain poorly understood. Here, we investigate photothermally induced helical-to-paramagnetic phase transition in Co$_9$Zn$_9$Mn$_2$ using pump-probe Lorentz transmission electron microscopy (LTEM). Space-time group includes novel intertwined non-symmorphic spatial-temporal symmetries such as time-glide reflection and time-screw rotation. Abstract: We demonstrate, using computer simulations and a non-equilibrium Greens function approach, that the sign of the out-of-equilibrium interlayer exchange coupling (ooeIEC) can change in the presence of an externally applied electrical bias. When the exchange coupled trilayer contains a quantum-well state confined in the hybridisation gap (HG) of the FM, we find that a relatively small applied electrical bias can switch the lowest energy state of the tri-layer between parallel (P) and anti-parallel (AP) configurations. We consider three cases for the insulating section; a single tunnelling barrier, a resonant tunnelling barrier and an amorphous insulating barrier and, in each case, show that the bias dependence of the ooeIEC is strongly dependent on the system conductance.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用线性响应理论（linear response theory）框架，使用紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）进行理论分析，并应用拉格朗日乘子法（Lagrange multiplier method）推导解析表达式。

Result: 在紧束缚模型中识别出三种特征临界频率：伙伴频率（partner frequencies）、尖峰频率（sharp-peak frequency）和截止频率（cutoff frequency）。这些频率在对应的线性化k·p模型中均不存在，其中尖峰频率和截止频率对能带倾斜和狄拉克点移动的变化具有鲁棒性。

Abstract: Within the framework of linear response theory, we theoretically investigated the interband longitudinal optical conductivities (LOCs) in two-dimensional (2D) tilted Dirac bands using a tight-binding (TB) model, incorporating the effects of band tilting and Dirac-point shifting. We identified three characteristic critical frequencies in the interband LOCs of the TB model: the partner frequencies, the sharp- peak frequency, and the cutoff frequency. In contrast to conventional critical frequencies, these three types are consistently absent in the corresponding linearized $k\cdot p$ model. Notably, the sharp-peak frequency and cutoff frequency remain robust against variations in band tilting and Dirac-point shifting. By employing analytical expressions derived via the Lagrange multiplier method, we elucidate the origins of the conventional critical frequencies and their partner counterparts. In contrast, the sharp-peak frequency and cutoff frequency are associated with interband optical transitions at high-symmetry points of the energy bands, arising from the Pauli exclusion principle and the finite boundaries of the Brillouin zone. Our theoretical predictions are intended to guide future experimental studies on tilt-dependent optical phenomena in 2D tilted Dirac systems.

Importantly, the 90$^{\circ}$ domains can be reversibly toggled solely by reversing the direction of the thermal gradient, demonstrating all-optical switching without the need for electric currents.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维拓扑绝缘体（3D topological insulators）的体态绝缘而表面导电的特性使其成为独特的研究对象，但如何可靠分离体态与拓扑表面态（topological surface states）的光学响应仍存在争议。高次谐波产生（high-order harmonic generation）作为探测凝聚态系统电子结构和动力学行为的强大工具，为研究这一问题提供了新途径。

Method: 研究以原型三维拓扑绝缘体Bi₂Se₃为对象，通过调控薄膜样品厚度（6 nm超薄膜和50 nm较厚膜）来控制体态与表面态对谐波发射的贡献。同时应用准静态太赫兹扰动场（quasi-static terahertz perturbing field）来分离体态与表面响应。

Result: 超薄（6 nm）薄膜显著增强了表面态对高次谐波产生的贡献，而较厚（50 nm）薄膜中体态主导谐波产生。通过太赫兹扰动场成功分离了体态与表面响应，并揭示了表面态的位移矢量（shift vector）和贝里曲率（Berry curvature）对高次谐波产生的显著影响。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了从体态响应中分离拓扑表面态光学响应的有效方法，为解决"能否可靠提取高次谐波产生中的拓扑特征"这一持续争议打开了大门，为拓扑材料的光学表征开辟了新途径。

Abstract: The discovery of topological phases has introduced a new dimension to materials science. Three-dimensional (3D) topological insulators (TIs) are a remarkable class of matter that is insulating in the bulk while hosting conductive topological surface states (TSSs) with unique charge and spin properties. High-order harmonic generation (HHG) has emerged as a powerful tool to probe condensed matter systems by providing insights into their electronic structure and dynamic behavior. Here, we investigate HHG in the prototype 3D-TI Bi$_2$Se$_3$. We demonstrate that the contributions of bulk and surface states to the harmonic emission can be controlled by tuning the thickness of thin film samples. An ultrathin (6 nm) film substantially enhances HHG from the surface states, while the bulk states dominate HHG in a thicker (50 nm) film. By applying a quasi-static terahertz perturbing field, we disentangle the bulk and surface responses and reveal the significant impact of the surface states' shift vector and Berry curvature on HHG. Our study provides effective methods for isolating the optical responses of TSSs from those of the bulk, which opens the door to resolving an ongoing debate regarding whether it is possible to reliably extract topological signatures in HHG.

</details>


### [122] [Solving the Peierls-Boltzmann transport equation with matrix product states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06153)
*Sangyeop Lee,Hirad Alipanah,Juan José Mendoza-Arenas*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究提出使用矩阵乘积态（MPS）数值模拟Peierls-Boltzmann输运方程（PBE），通过基于散射事件的MPS配置和无量纲形式增强张量间相关性局域性，实现维度约简。采用最优配置和密度矩阵重整化群启发式求解器，在硅晶体中求解PBE，计算成本随网格点数亚线性增长，计算时间相比稀疏矩阵有限体积法减少约一个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Peierls-Boltzmann输运方程（PBE）因其包含实空间和模态空间的高维相空间而面临维度灾难（curse of dimensionality）问题。需要开发有效的数值方法来降低计算复杂度，实现非平衡声子输运的高效模拟。

Method: 采用矩阵乘积态（matrix product states, MPS）进行PBE数值模拟，提出基于散射事件的MPS配置结合无量纲解形式以增强张量相关性局域性。研究MPS中索引排序的影响，发现最优配置是实空间和模态空间的张量链从最粗网格向MPS中心相互连接。使用密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group）启发的求解器，结合有限体积法（finite volume method, FVM）离散化求解PBE。

Result: 在硅晶体中求解PBE，涵盖弹道（ballistic）、准弹道（quasi-ballistic）和扩散（diffusive）输运区域。压缩比为10⁻³的截断MPS足以高保真地复现参考解。计算成本在实空间和模态空间中均随网格点数亚线性增长，相比稀疏矩阵操作的FVM，计算时间减少约一个数量级。

Conclusion: MPS方法能有效缓解PBE的维度灾难问题，通过优化配置实现显著的计算效率提升。该方法为高维相空间输运问题的数值模拟提供了有效解决方案，在保持计算精度的同时大幅降低计算成本。

Abstract: The Peierls-Boltzmann transport equation (PBE), which governs non-equilibrium phonon transport, suffers from the curse of dimensionality due to its high-dimensional phase space including both real and modal spaces. We explore the use of matrix product states (MPS) for numerical simulation of the PBE. We show that an MPS configuration based on scattering events combined with a dimensionless form of the solution can drastically increase the locality of correlations between tensors in the MPS representation, enhancing its effectiveness in dimension reduction. We further examine the effects of index ordering in an MPS and find that the highest locality is achieved when tensor chains associated with both real and modal spaces are connected from the coarsest grid to each other in the center of the MPS. Using this optimal configuration and a solver inspired by the density matrix renormalization group, we solve the PBE discretized by a finite volume method (FVM). The solution is obtained for crystalline silicon across ballistic, quasi-ballistic, and diffusive transport regimes. An MPS truncated to the compression ratio of $10^{-3}$ suffices to reproduce reference solutions with high fidelity. The computational cost scales sublinearly with the number of grid points in both real and modal spaces, achieving roughly an order of magnitude reduction in computational time compared to the FVM with sparse matrix operation.

</details>

### [123] [FluxMC: Rapid and High-Fidelity Inference for Space-Based Gravitational-Wave Observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04957)
*Bo Liang,Chang Liu,Hanlin Song,Tianyu Zhao,Minghui Du,He Wang,Haohao Gu,Sensen He,Yuxiang Xu,Wei-Liang Qian,Li-e Qiang,Peng Xu,Ziren Luo,Mingming Sun*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: FluxMC（Flow-guided Unbiased eXploration Monte Carlo）是一种机器学习增强的贝叶斯推断框架，通过结合流匹配（Flow Matching）与并行回火MCMC（Parallel Tempering MCMC），将推断范式从盲目的局部搜索转变为全局引导传输。在空间引力波天文学应用中，该方法在5小时内实现稳健收敛，而传统方法数百小时仍无法收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物理科学中的贝叶斯推断面临根本性挑战：高保真物理建模需求与随机采样算法的内在局限性之间存在冲突。复杂的高维参数空间暴露了传统方法（如马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛MCMC）的普遍弱点，包括似然评估的过高计算成本和陷入局部最优的风险。

Method: FluxMC框架整合了流匹配（Flow Matching）与并行回火MCMC（Parallel Tempering MCMC），将生成式AI的全局预见性与基于温度的采样的严格渐近收敛性和局部鲁棒性有效结合。该方法旨在将推断范式从盲目的局部搜索转变为全局引导传输。

Result: 在基于空间的引力波（gravitational-wave, GW）天文学应用中，针对大质量黑洞双星使用高保真波形（IMRPhenomHM），FluxMC在5小时内实现稳健收敛，而传统并行回火MCMC数百小时仍无法收敛，产生高达O(10⁻¹)的Jensen-Shannon散度（JSD）。该方法将分布误差降低了2-3个数量级，对于计算高效模型（IMRPhenomD）则消除了局部最优陷阱导致的系统偏差。

Conclusion: FluxMC消除了在模型精度与分析速度之间妥协的必要性，建立了一个新的计算基础，使科学发现仅受观测数据质量限制，而非算法能力限制。该方法为具有挑战性的参数反演问题提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Bayesian inference in the physical sciences faces a fundamental challenge: the imperative for high-fidelity physical modeling often clashes with the intrinsic limitations of stochastic sampling algorithms. Complex, high-dimensional parameter spaces expose the universal vulnerability of conventional methods, e.g., Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC), which struggle with the prohibitive costs of likelihood evaluations and the risk of entrapment in local optima. To resolve this impasse, we introduce FluxMC (Flow-guided Unbiased eXploration Monte Carlo), a machine learning-enhanced framework designed to shift the inference paradigm from blind local search to globally guided transport. It integrates Flow Matching with Parallel Tempering MCMC, effectively combining the global foresight of generative AI with the rigorous asymptotic convergence and local robustness of temperature-based sampling. We showcase the efficacy of this framework through the lens of space-based gravitational-wave (GW) astronomy -- a field representing the frontier of challenging parameter inversion. In the analysis of massive black hole binaries using high-fidelity waveforms (IMRPhenomHM), FluxMC achieves robust convergence in under five hours, whereas traditional Parallel Tempering MCMC fails to converge even after hundreds of hours, yielding high Jensen-Shannon divergences (JSD) of $O(10^{-1})$. Our method reduces the distributional error by two to three orders of magnitude. Furthermore, for computationally efficient models (IMRPhenomD), it eliminates systematic biases caused by local-optima entrapment. Ultimately, FluxMC removes the necessity to compromise between model accuracy and analysis speed, establishing a new computational foundation where scientific discovery is limited only by observational data quality, not by algorithmic capacity.

Method: CHRONOS探测器集成多项关键技术：扭杆（torsion bar）、速度计（speed meter）和低温镜（cryogenic mirror），以提升低频灵敏度。同时，在台湾国立中央大学组装了迈克耳孙干涉仪作为CHRONOS的部分组件进行调试。

Abstract: Gravitational waves from intermediate-mass black-hole (IMBH) binaries is a probe of strong-field gravity and black-hole evolution. Detection of IMBH is challenging because of their typically low frequency where the seismic noise, radiation pressure noise, and thermal noise dominate. The Cryogenic sub-Hz cROss torsion bar detector with quantum NOn-demolition Speed meter (CHRONOS) has been proposed to reach a strain sensitivity of $10^{-18} {\rm Hz}^{-1/2}$ at 2 Hz. It aims to detect GW from IMBH mergers with the mass of $\mathcal{O}(10^4)$ M$_{\odot}$ and to explore stochastic gravitational background of $Ω_{\rm GW} \sim 2\times 10^{-3}$ at 2 Hz. We present the overview of the CHRONOS hardware which is designed to integrate key techniques for improving low frequency sensitivity; torsion bar, speed meter, and cryogenic mirror. As a demonstration of the interferometer operation, we also report the commissioning status of a Michelson interferometer in National Central University in Taiwan which has been assembled as a partial component of CHRONOS.

### [125] [Mirror Dual Symmetry in Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05741)
*Lucas Lamata*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出对量子拉比模型（quantum Rabi model）和狄拉克方程（Dirac equation）采用一种新的对称性解释，即假设总能量始终为零的"镜像对偶对称性（mirror dual symmetry）"，从而避免负能量解带来的理论困境，并可能解决量子引力重整化（renormalization）、暗物质（dark matter）和暗能量（dark energy）等问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在解决量子拉比模型和狄拉克方程中负能量解带来的理论困境。传统量子化方法假设玻色模式存在基态能量，但负能量解可能导致系统能量衰减至负无穷，历史上狄拉克为此构建了高度人工化的狄拉克海（Dirac sea）。作者认为存在另一种基于对称性原理的解释方案。

Method: 作者提出采用"镜像对偶对称性（mirror dual symmetry）"原则，即假设总能量始终为零，并要求每个正能量激发都存在一个镜像的负能量激发。这种方法避免了传统量子化中对基态能量的假设，转而强制执行物理学中一贯成功的对称性原理。

Result: 应用这种对称性原理可以避免负能量解衰减至负无穷的问题，从而无需构建人工的狄拉克海。一个直接结果是零点能量（zero point energy）的自动抵消，这为解决当前物理学中的若干难题提供了可能途径。

Conclusion: 通过假设总对称性原理，许多当前物理学问题如量子引力重整化、暗物质和暗能量可能自动得到解决。这种基于对称性的解释为理解量子模型提供了新的视角，避免了传统方法中的人工构造。

Abstract: The quantum Rabi model has been a useful and pedagogical quantum model in the past decades, sufficiently simple to be solved analytically and intuitively understood, while sufficiently complex as to provide highly non-trivial eigenstates and a practical description of quantum optical platforms for quantum technologies. The Dirac equation, especially when restricted to 1+1 dimensions, is a simple toy model as well, but its easy diagonalization enabled historically to connect the electron spin to the fermionic statistics, among others. Both models share a symmetry at the purely mathematical level, namely, the spectra of each one has a dual equivalent under energy sign change, that I name a mirror dual symmetry. Usually, one quantizes these equations by assuming a ground state energy for the bosonic mode. But there is another option for the interpretation of the Hamiltonian, as I will argue, that is to assume a total symmetry principle, namely, that the total energy is zero at all times, for either the quantum Rabi model or the Dirac equation, and impose the constraint that every positive energy excitation has a mirror excitation of negative energy. This possibility, which was, apparently, ignored in the times when Paul Dirac was studying the implications of his equation, would avoid the worries in the scientific community that the negative energy solutions would decay until minus infinity, thus obviating the necessity to build a highly artificial Dirac sea, and instead impose what has always been successful in Physics, which is the enforcement of symmetry principles. Assuming a total symmetry principle, many of the problems of current Physics, such as renormalization of quantum gravity, dark matter, and dark energy, may possibly be automatically solved. One obvious result would be the automatic cancellation of the zero point energy.

</details>


### [126] [Geometry of Free Fermion Commutants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05031)
*Marco Lastres,Sanjay Moudgalya*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究为自由费米子（free-fermion）系统的k-对易子（k-commutant）提供了几何视角，揭示其与格拉斯曼流形（Grassmannian manifold）和有效海森堡模型（Heisenberg models）的联系，建立了实空间与副本空间（replica space）的二元性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解与k个相同副本酉系综（unitary ensembles）对易的算子结构（即k-对易子）是量子多体物理中的重要问题，对关联函数（correlation functions）和纠缠熵（entanglement entropies）在酉演化下的晚期行为有深远影响。

Method: 通过将k-对易子映射到有效铁磁海森堡模型（ferromagnetic Heisenberg models）的基态，并利用标准表示论（representation theory）方法精确求解。同时揭示系统在O(2k)副本对称性（replica symmetry）下的不可约表示结构。

Result: 发现自由费米子系统的k-对易子与格拉斯曼流形上的相干态（coherent states）存在几何对应，该流形恰好是2k个格点上的费米子高斯态（fermionic Gaussian states）流形。这揭示了实空间与副本空间之间的二元性（duality）。

Conclusion: 该工作为自由费米子的k-对易子提供了几何视角，基于相干态的单位分解（resolution of identity）建立了紧凑的投影公式，有助于分析计算高斯态的非线性泛函平均值，特别是在纠缠熵的计算中具有应用价值。

Abstract: Understanding the structure of operators that commute with $k$ identical replicas of unitary ensembles, also known as their $k$-commutants, is an important problem in quantum many-body physics with deep implications for the late-time behavior of physical quantities such as correlation functions and entanglement entropies under unitary evolution. In this work, we study the $k$-commutants of free-fermion unitary systems, which are heuristically known to contain $SO(k)$ and $SU(k)$ groups without and with particle number conservation respectively, with formal derivations of projectors onto these commutants appearing only very recently. We establish a complementary perspective by highlighting a larger $O(2k)$ replica symmetry (or $SU(2k)$ respectively) that the $k$-commutant transforms irreducibly under, which leads to a simple geometric understanding of the commutant in terms of coherent states parametrized by a Grassmannian manifold. We derive this structure by mapping the $k$-commutant to the ground state of effective ferromagnetic Heisenberg models, analogous to the ones that appear in the noisy circuit literature, which we solve exactly using standard representation theory methods. Further, we show that the Grassmannian manifold of the $k$-commutant is exactly the manifold of fermionic Gaussian states on $2k$ sites, which reveals a duality between real space and replica space in free-fermion systems. This geometric understanding also provides a compact projection formula onto the $k$-commutant, based on the resolution of identity for coherent states, which can prove advantageous in analytical calculations of averaged non-linear functionals of Gaussian states, as we demonstrate using some examples for the entanglement entropies. In all, this work provides a geometric perspective on the $k$-commutant of free-fermions that naturally connects to problems in quantum many-body physics.

</details>


### [127] [Star product for qubit states in phase space and star exponentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05170)
*Jasel Berra-Montiel,Alberto Molgado,Mar Sánchez-Córdova*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过SU(2)的余伴随轨道和Stratonovich-Weyl对应，在球面上构建了量子比特系统的相空间描述，实现了变形量子化。得到的星积再现了复数化四元数的算子代数，其反对称部分诱导出与Kirillov-Kostant-Souriau辛形式相关的Lie-Poisson结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究量子比特（qubit）系统的相空间描述，旨在通过几何方法建立量子动力学的相空间表示。这为理解量子系统的几何结构和动力学提供了新的视角。

Method: 采用SU(2)群的余伴随轨道（coadjoint orbits）和Stratonovich-Weyl对应关系，在球面（sphere）上实现变形量子化（deformation quantization）。通过构造星积（star product）来描述量子算子代数。

Result: 获得的星积精确再现了复数化四元数（complexified quaternions）的算子代数，其反对称部分诱导出与Kirillov-Kostant-Souriau辛形式相关的Lie-Poisson结构。量子动力学可通过哈密顿符号的星指数（star exponentials）在相空间中完全表达，并得到了传播子的显式表示。

Conclusion: 建立了S^2上相干态路径积分（coherent-state path integral）表述与基于星指数的代数描述之间的等价性。该方法为量子比特系统的相空间量子化提供了完整的几何框架，并通过具体示例说明了星指数函数的构造和所得Poisson结构。

Abstract: In this paper, we formulate the phase space description of qubit systems using coadjoint orbits of $SU(2)$ and the Stratonovich-Weyl correspondence, yielding a deformation quantization on the sphere. The resulting star product reproduces the operator algebra of complexified quaternions and its antisymmetric part induces the Lie-Poisson structure associated with the Kirillov-Kostant-Souriau symplectic form. We show that quantum dynamics can be expressed entirely in phase space through star exponentials of Hamiltonian symbols, leading to an explicit representation of the propagator. Further, we establish the equivalence between the coherent-state path integral formulation on $S^2$ and the algebraic description in terms of star exponentials. Some examples illustrating the construction of the star-exponential functions and the resulting Poisson structure are included.

</details>


### [128] [Simulating Thermal Properties of Bose-Hubbard Models on a Quantum Computer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06077)
*Simon Becker,Cambyse Rouzé,Robert Salzmann*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了首个针对玻色多体系统的严格吉布斯采样框架，证明了物理相关的玻色模型具有带隙耗散生成元，从而能够高效制备热态。研究展示了在平均场范围内外的玻色-哈伯德模型中，相关耗散生成元保持正谱隙，确保了向热态的指数收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管近期进展已为有限维系统建立了高效的吉布斯态制备量子算法，但玻色子和其他无限维模型的类似复杂度结果仍未探索。本文旨在填补这一空白，为无限维系统提供首个数学可控的吉布斯采样途径。

Method: 研究引入了首个针对玻色多体系统的通用严格吉布斯采样框架。在多模情况下，论证基于耗散动力学的有限秩约简，通过紧致扰动控制生成元，从而推断谱的离散性和隙的稳定性。研究以玻色-哈伯德模型为例进行说明。

Result: 研究证明物理相关的玻色模型具有带隙耗散生成元，能够高效制备热态。在平均场范围内外的玻色-哈伯德模型中，相关耗散生成元保持正谱隙，确保了向热态的指数收敛。研究结果可应用于量子比特硬件上相应吉布斯态的高效制备。

Conclusion: 该研究为无限维系统提供了首个数学可控的吉布斯采样途径，对量子模拟、热化和多体复杂性具有重要影响，其中可能出现量子优势。研究还提供了计算相关模型热性质的量子算法。

Abstract: While recent advances have established efficient quantum algorithms for preparing Gibbs states of finite-dimensional systems, comparable complexity results for bosonic and other infinite-dimensional models remain unexplored. We introduce the first general rigorous Gibbs sampling framework for bosonic many-body systems, showing that physically relevant bosonic models admit gapped dissipative generators, enabling efficient preparation of thermal states. Although our results hold for broad classes of models, we illustrate them using Bose-Hubbard Hamiltonians, both within and beyond the mean-field regime. In both cases, we show that the associated dissipative generators maintain a positive spectral gap, thereby implying exponential convergence to the thermal state. Our argument in the multi-mode case is based on a finite-rank reduction of the dissipative dynamics, which allows us to control the generator via compact perturbations and deduce the discreteness of the spectrum and the stability of the gap. We apply our results to provide efficient preparation of the corresponding Gibbs state on qubit hardware, and by that a quantum algorithm to compute thermal properties of the associated model. This provides the first mathematically controlled route to Gibbs sampling in infinite-dimensional systems, with implications for quantum simulation, thermalization, and many-body complexity, where quantum advantages may arise.

</details>


### [129] [Gauss law codes and vacuum codes from lattice gauge theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06087)
*Javier P. Lacambra,Aidan Chatwin-Davies,Masazumi Honda,Philipp A. Hoehn*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个基于阿贝尔格点规范理论（Abelian lattice gauge theories）构建量子纠错码（quantum error correcting codes）的综合性框架，使用量子参考系（quantum reference frames）作为统一形式化工具。该框架涵盖任意空间维度、任意紧致阿贝尔规范群，并包含纯规范理论和耦合物质的理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机在于建立量子纠错与规范理论之间的系统性联系，为在含噪量子设备上模拟格点规范理论提供实用优势。通过量子参考系这一统一形式化工具，旨在全面表征量子纠错码的代数结构和可纠正错误集。

Method: 方法基于阿贝尔格点规范理论，使用量子参考系作为统一形式化工具。构建了两类量子纠错码：高斯定律码（Gauss law codes）将码子空间识别为理论的完整规范不变扇区；真空码（vacuum codes）将码子空间限制在规范不变子空间内的物质真空扇区。研究涵盖了任意紧致阿贝尔规范群、任意空间维度的格点，以及纯规范理论和耦合玻色/费米物质的理论。

Result: 结果显示：当规范群有限时，真空码与纯规范理论的高斯定律码是幺正等价的；当群连续时，仅在对真空码进行电荷粗粒化（charge coarse-graining）后这一等价性成立。在耦合物质的模型中，高斯定律码继承了自然的子系统结构，其中规范不变的威尔逊环（Wilson loops）和修饰的物质激发因子化码空间。研究以ℤ₂规范理论以及标量和费米量子电动力学（QED）为例进行了具体说明。

Conclusion: 该框架为量子纠错与规范理论之间的平行性提供了基本见解，并指出了在含噪量子设备上模拟格点规范理论的实用优势。量子参考系为全面表征量子纠错码的代数结构和可纠正错误集提供了系统化工具。

Abstract: We develop a comprehensive framework for constructing quantum error correcting codes (QECCs) from Abelian lattice gauge theories (LGTs) using quantum reference frames (QRFs) as a unifying formalism. We consider LGTs with arbitrary compact Abelian gauge groups supported on lattices in arbitrary numbers of spatial dimensions, and we work with both pure gauge theories and theories with couplings to bosonic and fermionic matter. The codes that we construct fall into two classes: First, Gauss law codes identify the code subspace with the full gauge-invariant sector of the theory. In models with matter coupled to gauge fields, these codes inherit a natural subsystem structure in which gauge-invariant Wilson loops and dressed matter excitations factorize the code space. Second, vacuum codes restrict the code subspace to the matter vacuum sector within the gauge-invariant subspace, yielding codes where errors correspond to gauge-invariant charge excitations rather than to violations of the Gauss law. Despite their distinct setup, we show that when the gauge group is finite, vacuum codes are unitarily equivalent to pure gauge theory Gauss law codes, and that when the group is continuous, this is only true upon a charge coarse-graining of the vacuum code. In all cases, QRFs provide a systematic apparatus for fully characterizing the codes' algebraic structures and correctable error sets. For clarity, we illustrate our general results in $\mathbb{Z}_2$-gauge theory, as well as in scalar and fermionic QED. These findings offer fundamental insights into the parallelism between quantum error correction and gauge theory and point toward practical advantages for simulating LGTs on noisy quantum devices.

</details>


### [130] [Error Correction in Lattice Quantum Electrodynamics with Quantum Reference Frames](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06149)
*Elias Rothlin,Carla Ferradini,Lin-Qing Chen*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究将规范理论（gauge theory）与量子纠错码（QECC）联系起来，证明晶格量子电动力学（lattice QED）可作为超越稳定子码（stabilizer code）的量子纠错码，并展示规范对称性如何提供支持纠错的编码结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探讨规范对称性（gauge symmetry）是否具有更深层的信息论意义，而非仅仅是描述中的冗余。受量子纠错码（QECC）中冗余可作为保护信息资源的启发，该工作试图从类似角度理解规范理论。

Method: 基于并扩展了先前连接规范系统、稳定子码（stabilizer codes）和量子参考系（QRFs）的研究，针对阿贝尔规范群（Abelian gauge groups），使用群论方法为理想和非理想QRFs确定的错误集构建显式恢复操作。在晶格QED中，基于晶格的生成树构建规范场QRF，从物质场构建费米子场QRF。

Result: 在晶格QED中获得了两种QECC结构：一种在纯规范扇区，另一种包含费米子。QRFs解决了与约束测量相关的规范违反错误的简并性（degeneracy），并挑选出可纠正的错误族。这建立了晶格QED作为超越稳定子设置的QECC。

Conclusion: 该工作具体展示了规范对称性如何提供支持纠错的编码结构，将晶格QED确立为超越稳定子码的量子纠错码，证明了规范对称性在信息保护中的实质性作用。

Abstract: Is gauge symmetry merely a redundancy in our description, or does it carry a deeper information-theoretic significance? Quantum error-correcting codes (QECCs) show that redundancy can serve as a resource for protecting information against noise. In this work, we ask whether gauge theories can be understood in similar terms, and make this idea concrete in lattice quantum electrodynamics (QED), building on and extending earlier works that established a bridge between gauge systems, stabilizer codes, and quantum reference frames (QRFs). For Abelian gauge groups, we show that explicit recovery operations can be constructed using group-theoretical methods for error sets determined by both ideal and non-ideal QRFs. Applied to lattice QED, this yields two QECC structures: one in the pure-gauge sector and one including fermions. We construct a gauge-field QRF based on spanning trees of the lattice and a fermionic field QRF from the matter field, thereby making explicit how physical information is encoded. While the syndromes of gauge-violating errors associated with constraint measurements are generically degenerate, QRFs resolve this degeneracy and single out families of correctable errors. This establishes lattice QED as a QECC beyond the stabilizer setting and shows concretely how gauge symmetry provides an encoding structure that supports error correction.

### [131] [Real-time Dynamics in 3D for up to 1000 Qubits with Neural Quantum States: Quenches and the Quantum Kibble--Zurek Mechanism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05032)
*Vighnesh Dattatraya Naik,Zheng-Hang Sun,Markus Heyl*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究建立了神经量子态（Neural Quantum States）作为三维量子动力学的可扩展框架，通过引入针对立方自旋晶格的残差卷积架构，成功模拟了包含1000个量子比特系统的三维横向场伊辛模型动力学，首次实现了三维量子Kibble-Zurek机制的大规模数值演示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多体波函数的指数复杂性限制了实时动力学的精确数值模拟，特别是在一维以上系统中，快速纠缠增长带来了严峻挑战。神经量子态（Neural Quantum States, NQS）虽在二维实时动力学中表现出色，但其在三维系统中的可扩展性和准确性仍是一个未解决的开放性问题。

Method: 研究引入了针对立方自旋晶格（cubic spin lattices）的残差卷积架构（residual-based convolutional architecture），建立了NQS作为三维量子动力学的可扩展框架。重点关注三维横向场伊辛模型（3D transverse-field Ising model），通过重整化群流方程（renormalization-group flow equations）推导至双圈阶（two-loop order）的修正项。

Result: NQS可靠地捕捉了不同的淬火区域，包括崩溃-复兴动力学（collapse-and-revival dynamics）以及最具挑战性的量子临界点（quantum critical point）突然淬火后的动力学。在包含多达1000个量子比特的晶格上实现了有限速率淬火，这是超越一维实时动力学数值模拟前所未有的系统规模。首次大规模数值演示了三维量子Kibble-Zurek机制（quantum Kibble-Zurek mechanism, QKZM），获得了相关函数、过剩能量和量子费舍尔信息（quantum Fisher information）在所有模拟系统尺寸上的稳健数据坍塌。

Conclusion: 研究结果确立了NQS作为探索三维量子物质非平衡现象的可扩展且可靠工具，并为三维量子模拟器提供了数值基准。在伊辛普适类（Ising universality class）的上临界维度中，标准幂律被对数因子和显著的对数修正所修改，所有情况均与预期的标度维度（scaling dimensions）达成令人信服的一致。

Abstract: Exponential complexity of many-body wave functions limits accurate numerical simulations of real-time dynamics, especially beyond 1D, where rapid entanglement growth poses severe challenges. Neural Quantum States (NQS) have emerged as a powerful approach for real-time dynamics in 2D, but their scalability and accuracy in 3D have remained an open challenge. Here, we establish NQS as a scalable framework for 3D quantum dynamics by introducing a residual-based convolutional architecture tailored to cubic spin lattices. Focusing on the 3D transverse-field Ising model, we demonstrate that NQS reliably capture distinct quench regimes, including collapse-and-revival dynamics and, most challengingly, the dynamics following a sudden quench to the quantum critical point. We perform finite-rate quenches to the critical point on lattices containing up to $1000$ qubits, an unprecedented system size for numerical simulations of real-time dynamics beyond 1D. This enables the first large-scale numerical demonstration of the 3D quantum Kibble--Zurek mechanism. The QKZM in 3D is particularly intriguing because it lies at the upper critical dimension of the Ising universality class, where the standard power laws are modified by logarithmic factors together with prominent sub-leading logarithmic corrections. By deriving these corrections from renormalization-group flow equations up to two-loop order, we obtain a robust data collapse across all simulated system sizes for the correlation function, the excess energy, and the quantum Fisher information, the latter revealing universal multipartite-entanglement dynamics. In all cases, we find compelling agreement with the expected scaling dimensions. Our findings establish NQS as a scalable and reliable tool for exploring nonequilibrium phenomena in 3D quantum matter and for providing numerical benchmarks for 3D quantum simulators.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Spin-boson systems have attracted increasing attention as accessible experimental platforms and for their potential applications in designing quantum technologies. In this work, we investigate the properties of mixed eigenstates in spin-boson systems, comparing one-photon interactions with two-photon interactions. We propose a generalized definition of the phase-space overlap index to identify genuine mixed eigenstates. Our study highlights the fundamental differences that arise when two-photon processes are considered compared to one-photon processes and provides complementary evidence supporting the validity of the principle of uniform semiclassical condensation (PUSC) of quasiprobability functions in spin-boson systems.

### [133] [Quantum Hilbert Space Fragmentation and Entangled Frozen States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05218)
*Zihan Zhou,Tian-Hua Yang,Bo-Ting Chen*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究发现局部哈密顿量的秩亏缺（rank deficiency）是导致量子希尔伯特空间碎裂（quantum Hilbert space fragmentation）的关键机制，通过产生局部零方向（local null directions）生成纠缠冻结态（entangled frozen states），从而将经典可移动克里洛夫扇区（Krylov sectors）分裂为可移动量子克里洛夫子空间和纠缠冻结子空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在揭示量子希尔伯特空间碎裂的机制，特别是探究局部哈密顿量的秩亏缺如何导致经典碎裂模型中出现量子碎裂现象，并建立弱量子碎裂（weak quantum fragmentation）与强量子碎裂（strong quantum fragmentation）的区分框架。

Method: 通过分析四个具有递增对称性结构的模型来建立该机制：无对称性的非对称量子比特投影算子（asymmetric qubit projector）、$\mathbb{Z}_2$对称的GHZ投影算子、$\mathbb{Z}_3$对称的循环量子三态投影算子（cyclic qutrit projector）以及Temperley-Lieb模型。对于非对称和GHZ投影算子模型，获得了不可约克里洛夫维度（irreducible Krylov dimensions）、简并度和扇区多重性的闭式表达式。

Result: 研究发现当纠缠冻结子空间（entangled frozen subspace）非空时，可移动经典扇区分裂为可移动量子克里洛夫子空间和纠缠冻结子空间，模型表现出量子碎裂。在弱量子碎裂情况下，不可约块数量保持$\mathcal{O}(1)$，每个块具有高斯正交系综（Gaussian Orthogonal Ensemble, GOE）能级统计，未解析谱遵循$m$GOE分布；在强量子碎裂情况下，不可约块数量随系统尺寸增长，能隙比分布（gap-ratio distribution）在$L\to\infty$时趋近泊松分布。

Conclusion: 局部哈密顿量的秩亏缺是量子希尔伯特空间碎裂的关键机制，通过产生局部零方向生成纠缠冻结态，导致经典可移动扇区的量子分裂。该研究建立了弱量子碎裂与强量子碎裂的区分，为理解量子多体系统中的非遍历行为提供了新视角。

Abstract: We find that rank deficiency of the local Hamiltonian in a classically fragmented model is the key mechanism leading to quantum Hilbert space fragmentation. The rank deficiency produces local null directions that can generate entangled frozen states (EFS): entangled states embedded in mobile classical Krylov sectors that do not evolve under Hamiltonian dynamics. When the entangled frozen subspace is non-empty, the mobile classical sector splits into an mobile quantum Krylov subspace and an entangled frozen subspace, and the model exhibits quantum fragmentation. We establish this mechanism in four models of increasing symmetry structure: an asymmetric qubit projector with no symmetry, the $\mathbb{Z}_2$-symmetric GHZ projector, a $\mathbb{Z}_3$-symmetric cyclic qutrit projector, and the Temperley-Lieb model. For the asymmetric and GHZ projector models, we obtain closed-form expressions for irreducible Krylov dimensions, degeneracies, and sector multiplicities. Further, we introduce the notion of weak and strong quantum fragmentation, the quantum counterpart of the weak-strong distinction in classical fragmentation. After removing the EFS, the mobile quantum Krylov subspace decomposes into irreducible blocks. In the weak case, the number of irreducible blocks remains $\mathcal{O}(1)$, each is individually ergodic with Gaussian Orthogonal Ensemble (GOE) level statistics, and the unresolved spectrum follows an $m$GOE distribution. In the strong case, the number of irreducible blocks grows with system size, and the gap-ratio distribution approaches Poisson as $L\to\infty$.

</details>


### [134] [Quantum advantage in transfer of quantum states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05915)
*Andrei Stepanenko,Kseniia Chernova,Maxim Gorlach*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文发现并证明了一种量子优势（quantum advantage）的新范例：在具有近邻和长程耦合的晶格中，量子粒子同时沿多条轨迹传播的能力显著加速了激发转移过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子优势（quantum advantage）作为量子系统显著超越经典对应物的能力，是当前量子技术研究的核心驱动力。然而，其存在性常受争议，且大规模量子系统的优势领域尚未明确定义，需要寻找能够清晰定义和证明量子优势的新场景。

Method: 研究采用时间最优激发转移（time-optimal transfer of excitations）方法，在同时包含近邻耦合（nearest-neighbor couplings）和长程耦合（longer-range couplings）的晶格系统中进行分析。通过比较量子传播与经典轨迹的性能差异来评估量子优势。

Result: 研究证明量子粒子能够同时沿多条轨迹传播的量子力学特性显著加速了转移过程。量子系统的转移时间比任何单一经典轨迹都短，这为量子优势提供了明确例证。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了一个能够清晰定义和证明量子优势的新领域（novel niche），其中量子系统同时探索多条路径的能力产生了超越经典方法的性能优势，为理解量子优势提供了具体理论框架。

Abstract: Quantum advantage, broadly understood as the ability of quantum systems to significantly outperform their classical counterparts, underpins current interest to quantum technologies and is a topic of active investigation. In many situations, its existence is subject to debate, and the areas of supremacy of large-scale quantum systems are not well defined. Here, we uncover a novel niche where quantum advantage can be clearly defined and proven. We study a time-optimal transfer of excitations in the lattice involving both nearest-neighbor and longer-range couplings. We prove that the quantum-mechanical property of a particle to propagate along several trajectories simultaneously speeds up the transfer process, which takes a shorter time compared to any particular trajectory and thus provides a clear example of quantum advantage.

</details>


### [135] [Exploring bosonic bound states with parallel reaction coordinates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06027)
*Guan-Yu Lai,Friedemann Queißer,Gernot Schaller*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了量子系统与带隙库强耦合时出现的束缚态（bound states），证明了这些耗散弹性态的存在性，并通过弱耦合超系统方法重现了结果。研究发现束缚态稳定性源于其能量位于带隙内，且弱相互作用下束缚态寿命有限但可通过增强系统-库耦合来延长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索量子系统与具有带隙（band gaps）的库强耦合时出现的束缚态特性。这些束缚态具有耗散弹性（dissipation-resilient），在量子信息处理和量子技术中具有潜在应用价值。

Method: 采用两种方法：首先分析了一个精确可解的玻色模型（exactly solvable bosonic model）来研究束缚态存在性；其次通过弱耦合处理（weak-coupling treatment）构建超系统（supersystem），该系统由原始系统和多个反应坐标（reaction coordinates）组成，每个坐标代表库谱函数（spectral function）的小能量区间。

Result: 在微扰超系统处理中，束缚态的稳定性源于其能量位于带隙内部。研究讨论了多带隙（multiple band gaps）情况，并证明即使在弱相互作用（weak interactions）存在时，束缚态寿命也是有限的，但可以通过提高系统-库耦合强度（system-reservoir coupling strength）来延长寿命。

Conclusion: 束缚态作为耗散弹性态存在于量子系统与带隙库的强耦合体系中，其稳定性由能量位于带隙内决定。虽然弱相互作用限制了束缚态的无限寿命，但增强耦合强度可有效延长其存在时间，这为量子态保护提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Bound states are dissipation-resilient states that may emerge when quantum systems are strongly coupled to reservoirs with band gaps. We analyze an exactly solvable bosonic model for bound state existence and reproduce these results by a weak-coupling treatment of a supersystem composed of the original system and multiple reaction coordinates, which are individually representing small energy intervals of the reservoir spectral function. Within the perturbative supersystem treatment, the bound state stability results from its energy being inside the band gap. We discuss cases of multiple band gaps and also show that already in presence of weak interactions the bound state's lifetime is finite -- but can be increased by raising the system-reservoir coupling strength.

</details>
