### [136] [Scale-free congestion clusters in large-scale traffic networks: a continuum modeling study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05439)
*Yuki Chiba,Norikazu Saito,Yuki Ueda,Hiroaki Yoshida*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 该研究证明宏观连续交通流模型能够生成与真实城市拥堵观测相似的无标度时空拥堵簇，其簇大小服从幂律分布并展现出有限尺寸标度行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期实证研究发现城市交通中的时空拥堵簇呈现无标度统计特征，簇大小服从幂律分布。本研究旨在探究宏观连续交通流描述是否能够生成此类无标度时空拥堵模式。

Method: 研究分析了有向网络上具有交叉口耦合的二阶Aw-Rascle-Zhang模型。控制方程采用高阶间断伽辽金（discontinuous Galerkin）格式求解，交叉口通量通过基于优化的耦合程序确定，该程序在交叉口强制执行守恒性和可容许性。

Result: 在不同尺寸的格点网络上进行的数值实验表明，簇大小遵循稳健的幂律分布。当通过二维网络几何固有的线性系统尺寸重新标度时，分布坍缩到近似普适的曲线上，表明存在由线性系统尺寸主导的有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）。

Conclusion: 观测到的幂律统计和有限尺寸标度行为让人联想到自组织临界性（self-organized criticality）特有的尺度不变动力学。这些结果表明宏观连续交通模型能够复现真实城市拥堵动力学中观测到的大尺度统计特征。

Abstract: Recent empirical studies have reported that spatiotemporal congestion clusters in urban traffic exhibit scale-free statistics, with cluster size following a power-law distribution. In this study, we address whether macroscopic continuum descriptions of traffic flow are capable of generating such scale-free spatiotemporal congestion patterns. To this end, we analyze the second-order Aw-Rascle-Zhang model on directed networks under junction coupling. The governing equations are solved by a high-order discontinuous Galerkin scheme, and junction fluxes are determined by an optimization-based coupling procedure enforcing conservation and admissibility at intersections. Congestion is defined by thresholding the road-averaged density, and spatiotemporal clusters are extracted as connected components in space and time. Numerical experiments on lattice networks of varying sizes reveal that the cluster size follows a robust power-law distribution. Moreover, when rescaled by the linear system size inherent to the two-dimensional network geometry, the distribution collapses onto an approximately universal curve, indicating finite-size scaling governed by the linear system size. The observed power-law statistics and finite-size scaling are reminiscent of scale-invariant dynamics characteristic of self-organized criticality. These results demonstrate that macroscopic continuum traffic models can reproduce large-scale statistical features observed in real urban congestion dynamics.

</details>

### [137] [Development of a 3D-CNN-based Prediction Model for Migration Barriers in Plasma-Wall Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05521)
*Seiki Saito,Keisuke Takeuchi,Hiroaki Nakamura,Yasuhiro Oda,Kazuo Hoshino,Yuki Homma,Shohei Yamoto,Yuki Uchida*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于三维卷积神经网络（3D-CNN）的高效替代模型，用于预测氢同位素在钨中的迁移能垒，解决了传统NEB方法计算成本高的问题，为等离子体-壁相互作用的大规模动态建模铺平了道路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解氢同位素在钨等面向等离子体材料中的长期输运对磁约束聚变反应堆的稳态运行至关重要。然而，在连续等离子体辐照下，随着原子结构演化而动态更新动力学蒙特卡洛（kMC）模拟的跃迁参数仍是一个严重的计算瓶颈。

Method: 本文提出了一种使用三维卷积神经网络（3D-CNN）的高效替代模型来预测迁移能垒。该深度学习模型采用双通道体积输入：局部三维势能分布以及初始和最终俘获位点的体素化空间坐标，直接输出迁移能垒作为标量值。

Result: 模型在使用嵌入原子方法（EAM）势评估的钨-氢构型综合数据集上训练，表现出稳健的预测准确性，实现了0.124 eV的平均绝对误差（MAE）和0.890的高决定系数。利用GPU加速，每个能垒的推理时间减少到约2.7毫秒，相比传统NEB计算实现了超过23,000倍的加速比。

Conclusion: 这种非凡的加速有效地解决了跃迁速率评估的计算障碍，为实现实时分子动力学（MD）和kMC混合模拟铺平了道路，为等离子体-壁相互作用的大规模动态建模开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Understanding the long-term transport of hydrogen isotopes in plasma-facing materials, such as tungsten, is critical for the steady-state operation of magnetic confinement fusion reactors. However, dynamically updating the transition parameters for kinetic Monte Carlo (kMC) simulations as the atomic structure evolves under continuous plasma irradiation remains a severe computational bottleneck. Conventionally, calculating these migration barriers requires the iterative and computationally expensive Nudged Elastic Band (NEB) method. To overcome this limitation, this article presents a highly efficient surrogate model for predicting migration barriers using a three-dimensional Convolutional Neural Network (3D-CNN), establishing the final component necessary to realize on-the-fly molecular dynamics (MD) and kMC hybrid simulations. The proposed deep learning model takes a two-channel volumetric input, the local three-dimensional potential energy distribution and the voxelized spatial coordinates of the initial and final trapping sites, to directly output the migration barrier as a scalar value. Trained on a comprehensive dataset of tungsten-hydrogen configurations evaluated using the Embedded Atom Method (EAM) potential, the model demonstrated robust predictive accuracy, achieving a Mean Absolute Error (MAE) of 0.124 eV and a high coefficient of determination of 0.890. Furthermore, utilizing GPU acceleration, the inference time is reduced to approximately 2.7 milliseconds per barrier, achieving a speed-up ratio of over 23,000 compared to conventional NEB calculations. This extraordinary acceleration effectively resolves the computational barrier of transition rate evaluations, paving the way for large-scale, dynamic modeling of plasma-wall interactions.

We prove local well-posedness of strong solutions in Sobolev spaces for general parameters and mean-zero periodic data. In the purely elastic BBM regime we further establish global existence and exponential decay for sufficiently small initial data. We also present a numerical study of the reduced model, including comparisons across different viscoelastic and amplitude regimes, and discuss the observed dynamics in connection with the continuation criterion.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维立方散焦非线性波方程对于低正则性初始数据通常不适定，但通过傅里叶模态截断的高斯随机初始数据可在概率意义上恢复全局时间适定性。这些精细行为尚未得到数值验证。

Conclusion: 通过数值模拟验证了非线性波方程在随机初始数据下的精细行为，为理论预测提供了数值证据，并展示了在能量次临界和超临界区域中范数膨胀与概率适定性共存的现象。

Abstract: The three dimensional cubic defocusing nonlinear wave equation is known to be ill-posed for general low regularity initial data. However, well-posedness can be recovered globally in time on a probabilistic level when considering random Gaussian initial data approximated by truncation of Fourier modes. These fine behaviors of nonlinear wave equations have not yet been observed numerically . In this article we perform numerical simulations of the one dimensional fractional cubic defocusing wave equation in a periodic setting. This allows us to explore energy subcritical and supercritial regimes. Our numerical results suggest that both norm inflation and probabilistic well-posedness can be observed numerically in energy sub-critical and super-critical regimes.

Conclusion: 通过扩展sntools以支持前超新星中微子事件生成，为当前及下一代探测器研究这些中微子提供了统一框架，有助于提升对超新星早期阶段的理解和预警能力。

Abstract: The first detection of supernova burst neutrinos was achieved through the observation of SN1987A, almost four decades ago. However, neutrinos produced during the burning stages of a star prior to core collapse are yet to be detected. Detection of pre-supernova neutrinos could provide an early warning of an imminent supernova and allow the scientific community time to focus their resources on the observation and study of such an event leading to better understanding of these rare phenomena. Integrating pre-supernova models into a neutrino event generator would help to provide a unified framework for studying these neutrinos in current and next generation detectors. sntools is a neutrino event generator for supernova burst neutrinos, originally developed to study supernova model discrimination with Hyper-Kamiokande. Work to add support for pre-supernova event generation to sntools is presented, detailing the adaptations and additions to the code, with emphasis on how time binning can be optimised for a robust simulation, and also detailing the status of the validation process. The current status and capabilities of the package will be explained alongside plans for any further work and the intended use for the new functionality within the Hyper-Kamiokande Collaboration.

### [141] [Kinetic magnetohydrodynamics and Landau fluid closure in relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05058)
*Abhishek Hegade K. R.,James M. Stone*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于理解广义相对论中弱碰撞等离子体（weakly collisional plasmas）的理论框架，通过从Vlasov-Maxwell方程推导相对论漂移动力学方程，并引入新的解析Landau流体闭合来捕捉相对论等离子体中的各向异性热流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超大质量黑洞附近的扩散吸积流本质上是弱碰撞的，其中离子和电子分布函数可能显著偏离热平衡，粒子动力学效应通过驱动压力各向异性、热传导和等离子体不稳定性影响大尺度流体运动。在高度相对论性流动中建模这些等离子体效应对于解释黑洞图像的视界尺度观测至关重要。

Method: 从Vlasov-Maxwell方程推导相对论漂移动力学方程（relativistic drift kinetic equations），提出回旋平均分布函数矩的演化方程，并引入新的解析Landau流体闭合（Landau fluid closure）来捕捉相对论等离子体中的各向异性热流。

Result: 该模型不依赖强碰撞来强制热平衡，并一致地将Landau阻尼（Landau damping）纳入流体闭合中，为理解弱碰撞效应提供了与完全动力学模拟互补的方法。

Conclusion: 本文提出的理论框架为理解低光度相对论性黑洞吸积盘中的弱碰撞效应提供了补充性方法，不同于标准的（碰撞性）广义相对论磁流体动力学或扩展磁流体动力学模型。

Abstract: Diffuse accretion flows near a supermassive black hole are fundamentally weakly collisional. In such weakly collisional plasmas, the ion and electron distribution functions can deviate significantly from thermal equilibrium, and particle kinetic effects can influence large-scale fluid motion by driving pressure anisotropy, heat conduction, and plasma instabilities. Modeling these plasma effects in highly relativistic flows could be important for interpreting horizon-scale observations of black hole images. In this paper, we present a theoretical framework for understanding weakly collisional plasmas in general relativity by deriving the relativistic drift kinetic equations from the Vlasov-Maxwell equations. We present the evolution equations for the moments of the gyroaveraged distribution function and introduce a new analytic Landau fluid closure to capture anisotropic heat flow in relativistic plasmas. Unlike standard (collisional) general relativistic magnetohydrodynamics or extended magnetohydrodynamics, our model does not rely on strong collisions to enforce thermal equilibrium and consistently incorporates Landau damping in a fluid closure. The model introduced in this work provides a complementary approach to fully kinetic simulations in understanding weakly collisional effects in low-luminosity relativistic black hole accretion disks.

</details>


### [142] [Implications of low neutron star merger rates for gamma-ray bursts, r-process production and Galactic double neutron stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05059)
*Maya Fishbach,Alexander P. Ji,Wen-fai Fong,Tom Y. Wu,Jillian C. Rastinejad,Aditya Vijaykumar,Hsin-Yu Chen*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 基于GWTC-4引力波目录的最新分析显示，双中子星（BNS）并合率显著低于先前估计，为28-300 Gpc⁻³yr⁻¹，与短伽马射线暴（SGRB）率、r过程元素产生率及银河系双中子星（DNS）系统率存在明显张力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GW170817作为首个双中子星（BNS）并合的多信使发现，证实了此类事件可产生短伽马射线暴（SGRBs）和r过程元素。然而，后续观测中仅探测到一个额外BNS事件，且并合率随引力波（GW）目录更新持续下调，需要重新评估BNS并合率与相关天体物理现象的一致性。

Method: 分析最新引力波目录GWTC-4的数据，计算总BNS并合率及类似GW170817的~（1.3,1.3）M☉双中子星并合率。将更新后的引力波率与短伽马射线暴（SGRB）率、r过程元素产生率及银河系双中子星（DNS）系统率进行比较。

Result: 总BNS并合率为28-300 Gpc⁻³yr⁻¹，其中类似GW170817的双中子星并合率为53⁺¹⁷⁶₋₄₉ Gpc⁻³yr⁻¹（90%可信度）。与BNS并合率100 Gpc⁻³yr⁻¹相比，宇宙学SGRB率高3.6-18倍，r过程率高0.9-4.1倍，银河系DNS推断率高2.3-5.1倍，表明存在显著张力。

Conclusion: 更新后的引力波率显示BNS（及电磁明亮的中子星-黑洞，NSBH）并合率与SGRB、r过程和银河系DNS率之间存在明显不一致性。这种张力揭示了各种物理过程的不确定性，通过率比较可对这些过程施加约束。

Abstract: The first multimessenger discovery of a binary neutron star (BNS) merger, GW170817, proved that such mergers can source short gamma-ray bursts (SGRBs) and produce \rprocess elements. The initial merger rate from this single event in the first two observing runs of the LIGO-Virgo observatory network, $110$--$3840\,\mathrm{Gpc}^{-3}\,\mathrm{yr}^{-1}$, was found to be broadly consistent with the SGRB rate, the Milky Way (MW) r-process mass, and the Galactic population of double neutron star (DNS) systems that will merge in a Hubble time. However, only one additional BNS merger has been detected since, and the BNS merger rate has been consistently revised downwards with the past few gravitational wave (GW) catalog updates. Analyzing GW data from the latest catalog GWTC-4, we find a total BNS merger rate of $28$--$300\,\mathrm{Gpc}^{-3}\,\mathrm{yr}^{-1}$ (consistent with the most recently published values from LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA) consisting of $53^{+176}_{-49}\,\mathrm{Gpc}^{-3}\mathrm{yr}^{-1}$ in GW170817-like $\sim(1.3,1.3)\,M_\odot$ BNSs (90\% credibility). In light of this updated GW rate, we revisit the consistency of the BNS merger rate with SGRBs, r-process and Galactic DNSs. In all cases, there is an emerging tension with the BNS (and EM-bright neutron star--black hole, NSBH) merger rate. Comparing to a BNS merger rate of $100\,\mathrm{Gpc}^{-3}\mathrm{yr}^{-1}$, the cosmological SGRB rate is a factor of 3.6--18 higher, the r-process rate is a factor of 0.9--4.1 higher, and the rate inferred from Galactic DNSs is a factor of 2.3--5.1 higher than the BNS rate. We discuss how various uncertainties in the inferred rates either alleviate or exacerbate this tension, which point to the various physical processes that can be constrained by such rate comparisons.

### [143] [Approximating the Fourier Transform of Ring-Like Images: the Focal Expansion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05199)
*Filip Niewiński,Michael D. Johnson*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新颖的高维傅里叶变换近似方法，特别针对二维径向集中（环形）函数。该方法通过汉克尔变换和焦点展开，提供了从小到大的空间频率范围内都保持准确的单一近似。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在特定频率范围内存在局限性：基于矩的展开在小频率区域可靠，而大频率渐近展开仅在大频率区域有效。需要一种能够跨越不同频率范围的统一近似方法。

Method: 首先将问题简化为评估图像每个角模式的汉克尔变换（Hankel transforms），然后使用焦点展开（focal expansion）来近似这些剩余的汉克尔变换。该方法特别针对二维径向集中（'ring-like'）函数。

Result: 该方法提供了从小空间频率到大空间频率都保持准确的单一近似，领先的焦点项为广泛函数提供了准确的全局近似。通过黑洞"光子环"玩具模型的干涉测量响应验证了其有效性。

Conclusion: 提出的焦点展开方法为高维傅里叶变换提供了有效的近似框架，特别适用于黑洞探索者等实验中的光子环特征测量应用，展示了从理论到实际实验的桥梁作用。

Abstract: We derive and showcase a novel approach to approximating Fourier transforms in higher dimensions, focusing specifically on the case of 2D radially concentrated ('ring-like') functions. We first reduce the problem to that of evaluating the Hankel transforms of each angular mode of the image and then use our focal expansion to approximate these remaining Hankel transforms. Our method provides a single approximation that remains accurate from small to large spatial frequencies, bridging regimes where moment-based or large-frequency asymptotic expansions are individually reliable. We explore a series of examples, showing that the leading focal term provides an accurate global approximation for a broad range of functions. We demonstrate the utility of this approximation by examining the interferometric response for toy models of a black hole's "photon ring," highlighting the application to experiments designed to measure this feature such as the Black Hole Explorer.

</details>


### [144] [Reconstruction of fast-rotating neutron star observables with the neural network](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05428)
*Wen Liu,Lingxiao Wang,Zhenyu Zhu*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种因果卷积神经网络，用于快速重建中子星（neutron star）在静态、开普勒（Keplerian）和旋转配置下的可观测量，相比传统数值模拟方法实现了约36000倍的加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旋转会显著影响中子星（neutron star, NS）性质，但精确建模快速旋转的中子星需要求解二维轴对称系统，传统计算方法在需要大量模型评估的推断分析中计算成本过高。

Method: 开发了因果卷积神经网络（causal convolutional neural networks），该网络保持了中子星性质对状态方程（equation of state, EoS）的时序依赖性。使用\texttt{RNS}代码生成中子星可观测量数据集，并用于训练神经网络。

Result: 使用三个代表性状态方程（SFHo、SLy4和DD2）验证网络，发现其能准确复现\texttt{RNS}结果。训练后的网络评估单个状态方程的中子星配置仅需约50毫秒，相比典型\texttt{RNS}运行时间约30分钟实现了显著加速。

Conclusion: 该神经网络方法为涉及快速旋转中子星的高效推断分析提供了可行方案，大幅降低了计算成本，使得需要大量模型评估的研究变得可行。

Abstract: Rotation can significantly affect neutron-star (NS) properties, but accurate modeling of rapidly rotating NSs requires solving a two-dimensional, axially symmetric system, making traditional calculations too expensive for inference analyses that demand a large amount of model evaluations. We develop a causal convolutional neural networks that preserve the chronological-like dependence of NS properties on the equation of state (EoS) and rapidly reconstruct observables for static, Keplerian, and rotating configurations. Using \texttt{RNS}, we generate a dataset of NS observables and use it to train our networks. We validate our networks with three representative EoS (SFHo, SLy4, and DD2) and find that the they accurately reproduce the \texttt{RNS} results. The trained networks evaluate NS configurations for a single EoS in $\sim 50$ms, providing a substantial speedup over typical \texttt{RNS} runtimes of $\sim 30$ min and enabling efficient inference analyses involving rapidly rotating NSs.

</details>


### [145] [Remnant recoil and host environments of GWTC-4.0 binary black-hole mergers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05492)
*Joan Llobera-Querol,Eleanor Hamilton,Neha Singh,Marta Colleoni,Felip A. Ramis Vidal,Abbas Askar,Tomasz Bulik,Aleksandra Olejak,Sascha Husa,Yumeng Xu,Jorge Valencia*

TL;DR: 该研究通过分析LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA引力波探测器网络在O4a和O4b观测期探测到的87个双黑洞并合事件，识别出5个最可能起源于动力学形成的事件，并评估其并合残余物在不同天体环境中的保留可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确定双黑洞的天体物理起源及其并合残余物是否保留在诞生环境中，对于理解层级并合（hierarchical mergers）和中等质量黑洞（intermediate-mass black holes）的增长至关重要。

Result: 识别出5个显示动力学起源偏好的事件，包括O4a期质量最大的事件GW231123_135430，但排除了高自旋的O4b事件GW241011_233834。分析事件的典型反冲速度约为数百km/s，具有延伸的高速尾部。这些反冲表明并合残余物很可能从典型的球状星团（globular clusters）中被抛射出去，而在核星团（nuclear star clusters）中的保留虽有可能但不确定。

Conclusion: 研究结果不支持球状星团中高效的层级增长，而核星团仍然是重复并合的可行环境。尽管结果依赖于所采用的天体物理种群模型，但该分析强调了改进和扩大种群模型的重要性，以及未来引力波探测器发展带来的更高质量探测的必要性。

Abstract: Determining the astrophysical origin of binary black holes and whether merger remnants are retained in their birth environments is essential for understanding hierarchical mergers and the growth of intermediate-mass black holes. We considered the 84 events consistent with binary-black-hole (BBH) mergers from the first part of the fourth observing run (O4a) of the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA (LVK) GW detector network, and 3 selected events from the second part (O4b). We compared parameter-estimation posteriors with synthetic population models for field and cluster binaries using Bayes factors, accounting for the relative abundances of these formation channels in the local Universe. We computed recoil-velocity posteriors for all events using the IMRPhenomXPNR waveform model, which incorporates multipole asymmetries. We identified five events showing preference for a dynamical origin, including the most massive O4a event GW231123_135430, while excluding the high-spinning O4b event GW241011_233834. Typical recoil velocities of analyzed events are of order a few hundred km/s, with extended high-velocity tails. These kicks suggest that merger remnants are likely ejected from typical globular clusters, while retention in nuclear star clusters remains possible but not guaranteed. Our results disfavour efficient hierarchical growth in globular clusters, whereas nuclear star clusters remain viable environments for repeated mergers. Although results depend on the adopted astrophysical population models, this analysis highlights the importance of improved and larger population models, as well as higher-quality detections enabled by future developments in GW detectors.

### [146] [On the observational distinguishability of the Kerr and Kerr-Hayward metrics to EHT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06128)
*Nikola Bukowiecka,Angelo Ricarte,Prashant Kocherlakota,Cora Prather*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究证明，无奇点的Kerr-Hayward度规在黑洞偏振图像特征上与标准Kerr度规在事件视界望远镜（EHT）观测中几乎无法区分，为黑洞奇点问题提供了观测上可行的替代方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 天体物理黑洞通常用Kerr度规描述，但该度规存在环状曲率奇点（ring-like curvature singularity）的哲学问题。研究旨在探索能够消除奇点同时保持EHT可观测特征的替代度规。

Method: 研究采用Kerr-Hayward度规进行新的广义相对论磁流体动力学（GRMHD）模拟，并扩展EHT分析框架以在该时空中执行偏振辐射转移。详细描述了将修正时空实现到开源管道中的方法学。

Result: 从磁通参数（magnetic flux parameter）、喷流效率（jet efficiency）等流体量，到偏振模式（polarization pattern）和光子环结构（photon ring structure）等图像量，Kerr-Hayward度规的结果在功能上与Kerr度规无法区分。

Conclusion: 在某些条件下，对Kerr度规的无奇点修正（singularity-free correction）可以产生在EHT测量中实际上无法区分的可观测量，表明观测上可行的无奇点黑洞模型是可能的。

Abstract: Astrophysical black holes appear well-represented by the Kerr metric, but this metric has the philosophical problem of a ring-like curvature singularity. We show that a phenomenological correction to the Kerr metric known as the Kerr-Hayward metric can eliminate the curvature singularity while preserving in detail many features of polarized black hole images now testable by the Event Horizon Telescope (EHT). To establish this, we produce new general relativistic magnetohydrodynamics (GRMHD) simulations of a magnetized plasma in a Kerr-Hayward spacetime, then we extend the EHT analysis framework to perform polarized radiative transfer in this spacetime. We detail our methodology for implementing this modified spacetime into an open-source pipeline. From fluid quantities such as the magnetic flux parameter and jet efficiency, to image quantities such as the polarization pattern and the photon ring structure, our results for the Kerr-Hayward metric appear functionally indistinguishable from the Kerr metric. Our study finds that under certain conditions, the singularity-free correction to the Kerr metric can yield observables that are effectively indistinguishable in EHT measurements.

A comparison of the PHSD model results with available experimental measurements provides a qualitative description of these observables. Our results highlight the importance of baryon stopping, strangeness production, pair production, and baryon-antibaryon annihilation in the high baryon density region. ### [148] [Emergent symmetry and thermodynamic crossovers for supercritical AdS black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04968)
*Zhong-Ying Fan*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于李-杨相变理论（Lee-Yang phase transition theory）的新方法，用于研究超临界AdS黑洞的交叉线（crossover lines），揭示了复杂相空间中涌现的伊辛对称性（Ising symmetry）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 伊辛对称性通常在液-气相之间的临界区域涌现，这一普适性对超临界流体的热力学交叉行为施加了强约束。本文旨在研究超临界AdS黑洞的交叉线，以探索这一对称性在复杂相空间中的表现。

Method: 通过保持模压力（modular pressure）为实数，将李-杨零点（Lee-Yang zeros）解析延拓到超临界区域的复平面中，从而获得一对复交叉线。实交叉线通过将复交叉投影到实相空间来定义。

Result: 获得了一对展现普适标度行为的复交叉线，这些线在复杂相空间中体现了涌现的伊辛对称性。临界点以上的相图被划分为三个不同的区域：类液态、不可区分态和类气态，这与仅包含单一交叉线的情况形成鲜明对比。

Conclusion: 该方法成功揭示了超临界AdS黑洞相图中复杂的交叉结构，证明了伊辛对称性在复杂相空间中的涌现，并为理解超临界区域的热力学行为提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: Ising symmetry typically emerges in the critical domain between liquid-gas phases. Universality of this property imposes strong constraints on the behavior of thermodynamic crossovers for supercritical fluids. In this work, we develop a novel approach to investigate the crossover lines for supercritical AdS black holes using Lee-Yang phase transition theory. We analytically continue Lee-Yang zeros into the complex plane within the supercritical region by keeping a modular pressure real. Consequently, we obtain a pair of complex crossover lines, which exhibit universal scalings and manifest the emergent Ising symmetry in the complex phase space. The real crossover lines are defined by projecting the complex crossovers onto the real phase space. As a result, the phase diagram above the critical point is divided into three distinct regimes: liquid-like, indistinguishable and gas-like states, in sharp contrast to scenarios featuring only a single crossover line.

### [149] [Quantum state randomization constrained by non-Abelian symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05043)
*Yuhan Wu,Joaquin F. Rodriguez-Nieva*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了在具有非对易对称性（如SU(2)）的量子系统中，实验上可实现的Haar随机化程度主要受限于低纠缠初态制备，而非对称性约束的动力学本身。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解幺正量子动力学中随机性的涌现问题，特别关注物理系统普遍存在的对称性约束如何限制希尔伯特空间的可达区域并阻碍纯随机态的生成。

Method: 通过分析具有非对易对称性（如SU(2)）的系统，研究考察了在幺正动力学下时间演化态如何再现Haar随机行为，重点关注有限统计矩层面以及低纠缠初态的影响。

Result: 研究表明，即使处于强量子混沌区域且时间趋于无穷，对于编程量子系统中常用的无纠缠初态，晚期态仍可与Haar随机态区分，其偏离Haar行为随系统尺寸增大保持有限值。

Conclusion: 非阿贝尔对称性结构与实验态制备约束的结合会强烈限制晚期可实现的Haar随机化程度，揭示了实验初始化条件对量子随机性生成的关键制约作用。

Abstract: The emergence of randomness from unitary quantum dynamics is a central problem across diverse disciplines, ranging from the foundations of statistical mechanics to quantum algorithms and quantum computation. Physical systems are invariably subject to constraints -- from simple scalar symmetries to more complex non-Abelian ones -- that restrict the accessible regions of Hilbert space and obstruct the generation of pure random states. In this work, we show that for systems with noncommuting symmetries such as SU(2), the degree of Haar-like randomization achievable under unitary dynamics is strongly constrained by experimental limitations on state initialization, in particular low-entanglement initial states, rather than by the symmetry-constrained dynamics themselves. Specifically, we show that time-evolved states can, in principle, reproduce Haar-like behavior at the level of finite statistical moments (i.e., those accessible under realistic experimental conditions with a finite number of state copies) provided that the initial state matches the corresponding moments of the conserved operators in the Haar ensemble. However, for the unentangled initial states commonly used in programmable quantum systems, this condition cannot be satisfied. Consequently, even at asymptotically long times in strongly quantum-chaotic regimes, late-time states remain distinguishable from Haar-random states in probes such as entanglement entropy, with deviations from Haar behavior that remain finite with increasing system size. We quantify the maximal entanglement entropy achievable and identify the unentangled initial conditions that yield the most entropic late-time states. Our results show that the combination of non-Abelian symmetry structure and experimental constraints on state preparation can strongly limit the degree of Haar-like randomization achievable at late times.

### [150] [Entanglement in the open XX chain: Rényi oscillations, hard-edge crossover, and symmetry resolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05356)
*Miguel Tierz*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究开放边界XX自旋-1/2链的Rényi纠缠熵的精确渐近行为，特别关注费米动量接近能带边缘时的硬边交叉（hard-edge crossover）现象，以及开放边界条件对对称分辨熵（symmetry-resolved entropies）的影响。

Method: 通过将具有Toeplitz-plus-Hankel结构的边界关联矩阵（boundary correlation matrix）行列式映射到具有正权重的Hankel行列式，利用已知的Riemann-Hilbert结果分析其大尺寸渐近行为，并显式计算Szegő函数以获得主要的2k_F振荡振幅和相位。

Result: 推导出闭式渐近公式，发现单一变量s = 2ℓ sin(k_F/2)能组织硬边交叉行为：振荡包络服从s^{±1/α}幂律，ln s是数据塌缩的自然主导对数。对于分离块，振荡振幅与共形交叉比（conformal cross-ratio）的因子化一致。该框架还恢复了开放边界条件下对称分辨熵的均分偏移-½log log ℓ，以及相对于周期链的高斯宽度减半现象。

Conclusion: 该研究为开放边界XX自旋链的纠缠熵提供了系统的渐近分析框架，揭示了硬边交叉的普适标度行为，并建立了开放边界条件对对称分辨熵的定量影响，为理解边界效应对量子多体系统纠缠结构的影响提供了重要见解。

Abstract: We derive closed-form asymptotic formulas for the Rényi entanglement entropies of the open XX spin-$1/2$ chain by mapping the underlying determinant of the boundary correlation matrix (which has Toeplitz-plus-Hankel structure) to a Hankel determinant with a positive weight whose large-size asymptotics follow from known Riemann--Hilbert results. An explicit evaluation of the Szegő function yields the leading $2k_F$ oscillatory amplitude and phase. A single variable $s = 2\ell \sin(k_F/2)$ organizes the hard-edge crossover as the Fermi momentum approaches the band edge: the oscillation envelope obeys $s^{\pm1/α}$ power laws and $\ln s$ is the natural leading logarithm for a clean data collapse. For detached blocks the oscillatory amplitude is numerically consistent with a factorization through the conformal cross-ratio. The same framework recovers the open-boundary-condition (OBC) equipartition offset $-\tfrac{1}{2}\log\log\ell$ for symmetry-resolved entropies, together with the known halving of the Gaussian width relative to the periodic chain.

Conclusion: 该工作不仅填补了临界环模型的关键空白，还揭示了二维统计物理中三种基本方法（转移矩阵、共形场论和概率论）之间的深刻统一性。

Motivation: 研究一维Gross-Pitaevskii平带晶格的基态性质，探索平带几何如何影响玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）的相结构和对称性破缺行为。

Method: 采用全带平（all-bands-flat, ABF）模型和锯齿晶格（sawtooth lattice）作为研究体系，结合Bogoliubov-de Gennes激发和模拟退火（simulated annealing）方法分析系统的基态相变和热选择机制。

Result: 发现当平带几何控制参数θ≥π/8时，即使无限小的在位相互作用也能破坏均匀恒相凝聚体，驱动系统进入具有时间反演对称性破缺的宏观简并向列态。在临界端点θ=π/4处，识别出具有消失相位刚度的密度调制基态，这些相通过无序有序（order-by-disorder）机制在低温下被热选择。

Conclusion: 平带几何能够驱动非平庸的凝聚体相变，产生具有时间反演对称性破缺的向列态和密度调制相。平带凝聚体中的声速对底层几何相结构具有敏感探测能力，这些现象不仅限于ABF模型，在锯齿晶格等体系中同样存在。

Abstract: We investigate the ground-state properties of one-dimensional Gross-Pitaevskii flat-band lattices. We uncover a geometry-driven phase transition into a macroscopically degenerate nematic state with broken time reversal symmetry. Focusing on all-bands-flat (ABF) models, we demonstrate that even infinitesimal onsite interactions can destabilize a uniform, constant-phase condensate, driving the system into a nematic manifold as the flat-band geometry controlled parameter $θ\geq π/8$. At a critical endpoint (\(θ=π/4\)), where the compact localized states exhibit constant amplitudes, we identify an additional pair of density-modulated ground states characterized by vanishing phase stiffness. Utilizing Bogoliubov-de Gennes excitations and simulated annealing, we show that these density-modulated phases are thermally selected at low temperatures via an order-by-disorder mechanism. Finally, we demonstrate that these non-trivial condensate phases extend beyond ABF models, as exemplified by the sawtooth lattice. Our findings also reveal that the sound velocity in flat-band condensates is a sensitive probe of the underlying geometric phase structure.

</details>


### [154] [Quantitative analysis of fluctuating hydrodynamics in uniform shear flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05474)
*Hiroyoshi Nakano,Yuki Minami*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过直接数值模拟（DNS）验证了剪切流中涨落流体动力学的两个经典理论：Lutsko-Dufty非平衡长程关联理论和FNS动态重整化群（RG）理论，证实了它们在超出原始假设范围的非线性区域仍保持定量准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 均匀剪切流中涨落流体动力学的许多理论预测缺乏精确的定量验证，这源于分析近似的定量影响难以先验评估，以及微观粒子模拟的局限性。

Method: 采用剪切周期边界条件，对涨落Navier-Stokes（NS）方程进行直接数值模拟（DNS）。首先模拟线性化涨落NS方程验证Lutsko-Dufty理论，然后模拟完整非线性涨落NS方程测试FNS动态重整化群（RG）理论的预测能力。

Result: Lutsko-Dufty理论的预测从粘性主导的长波区域到剪切主导的短波区域都保持定量有效，远超其原始假设范围。FNS的一圈重整化群（one-loop RG）预测在强非线性区域仍保持定量准确性，而传统微扰理论在此区域失效。

Conclusion: 研究结果巩固了这些经典理论的基础，为使用涨落流体动力学进行定量分析铺平了道路。

Abstract: Many theoretical predictions in fluctuating hydrodynamics under uniform shear flow have lacked precise quantitative verification due to analytical approximations whose quantitative impacts are difficult to assess a priori and the limitations of microscopic particle-based simulations. To address this problem, we perform direct numerical simulations (DNS) of the fluctuating Navier-Stokes (NS) equations with shear-periodic boundary conditions. We provide a decisive quantitative validation of two seminal frameworks: the Lutsko-Dufty theory for nonequilibrium long-range correlations, and the dynamic renormalization group (RG) theory by Forster, Nelson, and Stephen (FNS) for anomalous transport. By simulating the linearized fluctuating NS equations, we demonstrate that the predictions of the Lutsko-Dufty theory are quantitatively valid from the viscous-dominated, long-wavelength regime to the shear-dominated, short-wavelength regime, well beyond their originally assumed limits. Moving beyond the linearized equations, we simulate the full nonlinear fluctuating NS equations to test the quantitative predictive capability of the dynamical RG approach by FNS. Our results show that the one-loop RG prediction remains quantitatively accurate up to a strongly nonlinear regime, where conventional perturbation theory fails. Our findings solidify the foundations of these classical theories, paving the way for quantitative analyses using fluctuating hydrodynamics.

### [155] [Shortcuts to state transitions for active matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05585)
*Guodong Cheng,Z. C. Tu,Geng Li*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文开发了一个捷径框架（shortcut framework），用于在弱活性（weak activity）状态下实现主动系统（active systems）的快速状态转换，通过引入辅助势能（auxiliary potential）引导系统沿预定分布路径运动，并基于耗散功（dissipative work）推导热力学度量来寻找最优协议（optimal protocol）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 被动系统（passive systems）中可通过捷径方案（shortcut schemes）加速准静态过程，但主动系统由于自由能消耗驱动的定向运动而持续远离平衡。本研究旨在为弱活性状态下的主动系统开发实现快速状态转换的捷径框架。

Method: 引入辅助势能引导系统沿预定分布路径运动，从耗散功推导热力学度量并在控制参数空间诱导黎曼流形（Riemann manifold），使最小耗散功的最优协议等同于几何空间中的测地线路径（geodesic path）。针对两种内部势能（吸引谐波耦合和排斥高斯核耦合）分别采用精确推导和变分方法（variational method）获得辅助控制。

Result: 框架在外部谐波势阱（harmonic trap）约束的主动系统中得到验证，分别考虑了吸引谐波耦合和排斥高斯核耦合（Gaussian-core coupling）两种内部相互作用。对于后者，通过变分方法获得了近似的辅助控制。与线性协议相比，测地线协议能有效减少耗散。

Conclusion: 该研究为主动系统的快速状态转换提供了基于几何热力学的捷径框架，通过最小化耗散功的测地线协议实现了比线性协议更有效的耗散减少，为弱活性状态下主动系统的控制策略提供了新方法。

Abstract: Shortcut schemes can accelerate quasi-static processes in passive systems by adding auxiliary controls to realize swift transitions between equilibrium states. In active systems, however, inherently directed motion driven by free energy consumption continually drives the system away from equilibrium. In this work, we develop a shortcut framework to realize swift state transitions for active systems operating in the weak activity regime. An auxiliary potential is introduced to guide the system along a predefined distribution path, allowing it to reach the target state within a finite time. Considering unavoidable energy cost in such a finite-time process, we derive a thermodynamic metric from the dissipative work to induce a Riemann manifold on the space spanned by the control parameters. The optimal protocol with minimum dissipative work is then identical to the geodesic path in the geometric space. We demonstrate this framework by considering active systems confined in an external harmonic trap and interacting via two distinct internal potentials, respectively: an attractive harmonic coupling and a repulsive pairwise Gaussian-core coupling. The strengths of both the external trap and the internal interactions are controllable. For the latter case, since the auxiliary potential can not be derived precisely, we adopt a variational method to obtain an approximate auxiliary control. Compared to linear protocols, the geodesic protocols can effectively reduce dissipation.

</details>


### [156] [Percolation in the three-dimensional Ising model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05772)
*Jinhong Zhu,Tao Chen,Zhiyi Li,Sheng Fang,Youjin Deng*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过蒙特卡洛模拟和理论分析，研究了临界伊辛模型中的几何渗流现象，发现二维临界伊辛模型存在两个连续渗流转变，而三维模型和完全图模型仅存在单一渗流转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 几何表示（geometric representations）为伊辛模型（Ising model）中的临界现象提供了有用视角。先前研究发现二维临界伊辛模型在平行自旋间的键占据概率（bond-occupation probability）增加时，几何自旋团簇（geometric spin clusters）会经历两个连续的渗流转变（percolation transitions）。

Method: 采用广泛的蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）研究三维临界伊辛模型，并对完全图（complete graph）上的伊辛模型进行理论分析。此外，还研究了嵌入三维临界伊辛模型中的二维层系统（layer system）。

Result: 三维临界伊辛构型仅显示单一渗流转变，完全图模型分析也得到相同结论。对于二维层系统，估计得到红键指数（red-bond exponent）$y_p = 0.426(6)$，最大团簇、外壳和最短路径的分形维数（fractal dimensions）分别为$d_f = 1.8926(20)$、$d_{\rm hull} = 1.663(4)$和$d_{\rm min} = 1.080(10)$。

Conclusion: 这些数值表明，通过耦合面外临界关联（out-of-plane critical correlations），二维层系统诱导了一个独特的普适类（universality class）。二维临界伊辛模型的双渗流转变现象在三维中不持续存在。

Abstract: Geometric representations provide a useful perspective on critical phenomena in the Ising model. In a recent study [Phys. Rev. E 112, 034118 (2025)], we found that the two-dimensional critical Ising model exhibits two consecutive percolation transitions for geometric spin clusters as the bond-occupation probability $p$ between parallel spins increases. Here, through extensive Monte Carlo simulations, we show that this phenomenon does not persist in three dimensions, where we observe only a single percolation transition on critical Ising configurations. Further theoretical analysis of the Ising model on the complete graph also yields the same scenario. In addition, we study percolation on a two-dimensional layer embedded in the three-dimensional critical Ising model. For this layer system, we estimate the red-bond exponent $y_p = 0.426(6)$ and the fractal dimensions of the largest cluster, hull, and shortest path as $d_f = 1.8926(20)$, $d_{\rm hull} = 1.663(4)$, and $d_{\rm min} = 1.080(10)$, respectively. These values indicate a distinct universality class induced by coupling to out-of-plane critical correlations.

### [157] [Generalized hydrodynamics of free fermions under extensive-charge monitoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05850)
*Pablo Bayona-Pena,Michele Mazzoni,Lorenzo Piroli*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了自由费米子在广泛区域守恒荷监测下的输运动力学，基于广义流体动力学框架分析了二分协议中的局域电荷和电流分布，揭示了监测导致的分布不连续性及其在芝诺极限下的输运抑制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解自由费米子体系在广泛区域守恒荷（如总粒子数）监测下的输运动力学。重点关注二分协议中监测对系统一半区域总粒子数的影响，探究在流体动力学尺度下局域电荷和电流分布的变化规律。

Method: 采用广义流体动力学（generalized hydrodynamics, GHD）框架，结合数值-解析混合方法求解流体动力学尺度的淬火动力学。研究聚焦于自由费米子体系，考虑对系统一半区域总粒子数进行监测的二分协议，将描述平均动力学的非局域Lindbladian理解为局域杂质效应。

Result: 监测导致局域电荷和电流分布出现不连续性，且不连续性随监测速率增加而增强。在无限监测速率的芝诺极限（Zeno limit）下，系统输运完全被抑制。研究展示了域壁初始态下监测对输运分布的具体影响。

Conclusion: 提出的广义流体动力学框架可自然扩展到相互作用系统，为系统研究可积模型在广泛电荷测量下的输运行为开辟了新途径。该框架为理解监测对量子输运的影响提供了通用方法学基础。

Abstract: We study transport dynamics of free fermions subject to the external monitoring of a conserved charge over an extensive region. Focusing on bipartition protocols, we consider monitoring the total particle number over half of the system, and study the profiles of local charges and currents at hydrodynamic scales. While the Lindbladian describing the averaged dynamics is non-local, we show that the profiles can be understood in terms of localized impurities. We present a general framework based on the generalized hydrodynamics (GHD) picture, allowing for a hybrid numerical-analytic solution of the quench dynamics at hydrodynamic scales. We illustrate our approach for domain-wall initial states, showing that monitoring leads to discontinuities in the profiles that become more pronounced as the rate increases and that lead to the absence of transport in the Zeno limit of infinite monitoring rates. Our GHD framework could be naturally extended to interacting systems, paving the way for a systematic study of transport of integrable models subject to extensive-charge measurements.

### [159] [Dynamical phase diagram of synchronization in one dimension: universal behavior from Edwards-Wilkinson to random deposition through Kardar-Parisi-Zhang](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06040)
*Ricardo Gutierrez,Rodolfo Cuerno*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究通过数值模拟揭示了二维同步（synchronization）系统的完整相图，展示了从随机沉积/线性增长到爱德华兹-威尔金森（Edwards-Wilkinson）再到卡达尔-帕里西-张（Kardar-Parisi-Zhang）普适类行为的交叉转变，并分析了相位滑移（phase slips）对尺度律的扭曲效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管一维同步已被证实具有与表面动力学粗糙化（surface kinetic roughening）和KPZ普适类（KPZ universality class）相关的通用尺度不变性（generic scale invariance），但其临界行为的鲁棒性（robustness）和参数空间中的精确边界仍不明确。这阻碍了向高维度的扩展以及在实验系统中观察非平衡临界性（nonequilibrium criticality）。

Method: 基于具有时间依赖性噪声（time-dependent noise）或柱状（淬火）无序（columnar (quenched) disorder）的相位振子（phase oscillators）系统，通过完整的数值相图（numerical phase diagrams）模拟，包括饱和时间和数值，并特别关注揭示同步动力学逐渐出现的动态特征。

Result: 在非同步区域，动力学表现为预期的随机沉积（random deposition）（针对时间依赖性噪声）或线性增长（linear growth）（针对柱状无序）。在同步区域，随着无序强度或振子间耦合的非奇异性（nonoddity）增加，观察到从爱德华兹-威尔金森（Edwards-Wilkinson）行为到KPZ行为的交叉转变，其组合效应部分由所谓的KPZ耦合（KPZ coupling）所捕获。此外，还讨论了在去同步边界附近相位滑移（phase slips）对尺度律（scaling）的扭曲效应。

Conclusion: 该研究通过详细的数值相图阐明了同步系统中临界行为的参数边界和动态特征，揭示了从不同普适类行为之间的交叉转变机制。对相位滑移效应的分析为实验背景下观察非平衡临界性提供了重要见解，有助于推动该领域向高维度和实验验证的进一步发展。

Abstract: Synchronization in one dimension displays generic scale invariance with universal properties previously observed in surface kinetic roughening and the wider context of the Kardar-Parisi-Zhang (KPZ) universality class. This has been established for phase oscillators and also for some limit-cycle oscillators, both in the presence of columnar (quenched) disorder and of time-dependent noise, by extensive numerical simulations, and has been analytically motivated by continuum approximations in the strong oscillator coupling limit. The robustness and the precise boundaries in parameter space for such critical behavior remain unclear, however, which may preclude further developments, including the extension of these results to higher dimensions and the experimental observation of nonequilibrium criticality in synchronizing (e.g.~electronic or chemical) oscillators. We here present complete numerical phase diagrams of one-dimensional synchronization, including saturation times and values, but, most importantly, also dynamical features giving insight into the gradual emergence of synchronous dynamics, based on systems of phase oscillators with either type of randomness. In the absence of synchronization, the dynamics evolves as expected for random deposition (for time-dependent noise) or linear growth (for columnar disorder), while a crossover from Edwards-Wilkinson to Kardar-Parisi-Zhang behavior (with the corresponding type of randomness) is observed as the randomness strength, or the nonoddity of the coupling among oscillators, is increased in the synchronous region -- their combined effect being partially captured by the so-called KPZ coupling. The distortion of scaling due to phase slips near the desynchronization boundary, a feature that is likely to play a role in experimental contexts, is also discussed.

</details>


### [160] [Mutual Linearity in and out of Stationarity for Markov Jump Processes: A Trajectory-Based Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06162)
*Jiming Zheng,Zhiyue Lu*

TL;DR: 本文基于轨迹层面的线性响应理论，为非平衡响应理论中的互线性关系提供了轨迹层面的推导，并将其推广到非平稳弛豫动力学中的状态可观测量和计数可观测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非平衡响应理论是理解物理系统如何响应微扰的基本框架。最近通过线性代数分析在马尔可夫跳跃过程中发现了互线性关系，该关系描述了当单一边的跃迁速率改变时，两个可观测量在长时间极限下线性相关。这一关系已扩展到电流观测量的非平稳情况。

Method: 采用基于轨迹的方法，利用轨迹层面的线性响应理论推导互线性关系。轨迹方法使得将互线性关系推广到非平稳弛豫动力学中的状态可观测量和计数可观测量成为可能。

Result: 轨迹方法成功推导了互线性关系，并将其推广到更广泛的系统类别，包括扩散过程和开放量子系统。这揭示了远离平衡态的基本响应特性以及互线性关系的轨迹层面起源。

Conclusion: 基于轨迹的方法为互线性关系提供了更基础的推导框架，使其能够扩展到更广泛的物理系统和观测类型，深化了对非平衡响应理论的理解。

Abstract: Nonequilibrium response theory is a fundamental framework for understanding how physical systems respond to perturbations. Recently, a mutual linearity has been discovered for Markov jump processes using linear algebra analysis. This mutual linearity states that two observables are linearly dependent on each other in the long-time limit when the transition rate of a single edge is altered. It has also been extended to non-stationary cases for current observables. In this work, we provide a trajectory-based derivation of mutual linearity utilizing the trajectory-level linear response theory. The trajectory approach allows us to generalize the mutual linearity to non-stationary relaxation dynamics for state observables and counting observables. Our results shed light on the fundamental response properties far from equilibrium and the trajectory-level origin of mutual linearity. Our trajectory-based approach makes it possible to generalize the mutual linearity to a broader class of systems, including diffusion processes and open quantum systems.

</details>

### [161] [Near-Tsirelson Bell-CHSH Violations in Quantum Field Theory via Carleman and Hankel Operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05109)
*David Dudal,Ken Vandermeersch*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究在(1+1)维闵可夫斯基时空的自由旋量场真空态中，构造了具有类空间隔支撑的测试函数，其Bell-CHSH关联函数收敛至Tsirelson界2√2，建立了Bell-CHSH违反与半线上Carleman和Hankel算子谱理论的直接联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究自由旋量场真空态中的Bell-Clauser-Horne-Shimony-Holt (Bell-CHSH)违反，旨在理解量子场论背景下贝尔不等式违反的机制，并探索其与算子谱理论的联系。

Method: 在(1+1)维闵可夫斯基时空中，构造具有类空间隔支撑的光滑紧支集测试函数；在无质量情况下通过时间零切片和对称约化，将问题简化为L^2([0,∞))上Carleman算子的二次型；在有质量情况下，简化为核函数为mK₁(m(x+y))的Hankel算子。

Result: 无质量情况下，近最大Bell违反由谱边缘π控制，从广义本征函数x^{-1/2}的紧支集截断获得显式近极值函数；有质量情况下，无质量测试函数的指数衰减变体同样使Bell-CHSH值收敛至2√2。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了自由(1+1)维旋量场的Bell-CHSH违反与半线上Carleman和Hankel算子谱理论的直接联系，解释了早期小波公式中常数π的出现。

Abstract: We study Bell-Clauser-Horne-Shimony-Holt (Bell-CHSH) violations in the vacuum state of free spinor fields in $(1+1)$-dimensional Minkowski spacetime. We construct explicit smooth compactly supported test functions with spacelike separated supports whose Bell-CHSH correlators converge to Tsirelson's bound $2\sqrt2$. In the massless case, after passage to the time-zero slice and a natural symmetry reduction, the problem reduces to the quadratic form of the Carleman operator on $L^2([0,\infty))$. Near-maximal Bell violation is then governed by the spectral edge $π$, and explicit near-extremizers are obtained from compactly supported cutoffs of the generalized eigenfunction $x^{-1/2}$. This also explains the appearance of the constant $π$ in earlier wavelet-based formulations. In the massive case, the same reduction leads to a Hankel operator with kernel $mK_1(m(x+y))$, where $K_1$ denotes the modified Bessel function of the second kind of order $1$, and exponentially damped variants of the massless test functions again yield Bell-CHSH values converging to $2\sqrt2$. Therefore, we establish a direct link between Bell-CHSH violations for free $(1+1)$-dimensional spinor fields and the spectral theory of Carleman and Hankel operators on the half-line.

</details>


### [162] [Constructive Quantum Field Theory and Rigorous Statistical Mechanics via Operator Algebras and Probability Theory -- Guiding Principles and Research Perspectives](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05300)
*Yoshitsugu Sekine*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出量子系统的算子代数表述的分层观点：C*-代数提供普遍内在描述，冯·诺依曼代数在固定动力学相容状态后提供详细描述。对于玻色多体系统，预解代数（resolvent algebra）比外尔代数（Weyl algebra）更自然，其核性、平凡中心和丰富理想结构忠实反映纯量子力学结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在建立量子系统算子代数表述的分层观点，以统一理解量子系统的普遍描述与具体实现。该框架旨在阐明不同代数结构在描述量子系统时的作用，特别是为玻色多体系统提供更自然的代数表述。

Method: 采用分层观点：C*-代数负责普遍内在描述，冯·诺依曼代数在固定动力学相容状态后提供详细描述。特别强调预解代数（resolvent algebra）作为玻色多体系统的自然对象，并利用其核性、平凡中心和丰富理想结构。通过GNS表示的弱闭包中心捕获宏观变量或相变相关的扇区结构。

Result: 预解代数比外尔代数更自然地描述玻色多体系统，其结构特性忠实反映纯量子力学结构。算子代数表示与泛函积分之间的等价性允许使用强大的概率方法。该框架为构造量子场论和严格统计力学中的具体对象提供了研究视角。

Conclusion: 分层观点为量子系统的算子代数表述提供了统一框架，预解代数在玻色多体系统中具有优越性。该框架将算子代数表示与泛函积分联系起来，为构造量子场论和严格统计力学的研究开辟了新视角。

Abstract: We present a hierarchical viewpoint on the operator-algebraic formulation of quantum systems, in which $C^{*}$-algebras are responsible for the universal and intrinsic description, whereas von Neumann algebras provide the detailed account obtained after fixing a state compatible with the dynamics. From this standpoint, for bosonic many-body systems the resolvent algebra, rather than the Weyl algebra, is the natural object; in particular, its nuclearity, trivial center, and rich ideal structure faithfully reflect purely quantum-mechanical structures. Macroscopic variables or sector structures associated with phase transitions are captured as the center appearing in the weak closure of the GNS representation. Moreover, the equivalence between representations of operator algebras and functional integrals allows powerful probabilistic methods to be employed. Taking these as guiding principles, we outline research perspectives on concrete objects in constructive quantum field theory and rigorous statistical mechanics.

### [163] [On some topological and spectral properties of kinetic Langevin processes driven by L{é}vy noises](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05598)
*T Batisse,A Guillin,B Nectoux,L Wu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了$\mathbb{R}^{2d}$中由纯跳跃Lévy过程驱动的动力学朗之万（kinetic Langevin）过程的基本性质，包括原始过程及其在特定域中被杀灭（killed）的版本。在低正则性（low-regularity）框架下（漂移项$\mathbf{B}$不假设连续），建立了半群的关键结构和谱性质，包括强Feller性质、谱隙（spectral gap）等。对于旋转不变α-稳定（α-stable）噪声驱动的情况（α∈(1,2)），证明了弱解的存在唯一性，并进一步建立了平稳分布（stationary distribution）和拟平稳分布（quasi-stationary distribution）的存在唯一性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究由纯跳跃Lévy过程驱动的动力学朗之万过程的基本性质，特别是在低正则性框架下的分析。研究动机包括：理解这类过程在漂移项不连续情况下的行为特征，分析原始过程及其被杀灭版本的结构性质，以及探索平稳分布和拟平稳分布的存在性问题。

Method: 研究方法基于对动力学朗之万过程系统的分析，该系统定义为$\mathbb{R}^{2d}$中的随机微分方程。研究在低正则性框架下进行，不假设漂移项$\mathbf{B}$的连续性。分析涵盖原始过程及其在域$\mathscr{D} = \mathscr{O} \times \mathbb{R}^d$中被杀灭的版本。对于旋转不变α-稳定过程驱动的情况（α∈(1,2)），建立了弱解的存在唯一性证明。

Result: 主要结果包括：在低正则性框架下，建立了非杀灭和杀灭半群的强Feller性质（strong Feller property）、弱连续性、拓扑不可约性（topological irreducibility）和谱隙存在性。对于α∈(1,2)的旋转不变α-稳定噪声，证明了弱解的存在唯一性，并进一步建立了某些$L^m$空间中的密度存在性以及Feller $C_0(\mathbb R^{2d})$-半群性质。最后证明了平稳分布和拟平稳分布的存在唯一性，以及非杀灭过程的指数遍历性（exponential ergodicity）和条件过程向拟平稳极限的指数收敛性。

Conclusion: 本文成功建立了由纯跳跃Lévy过程驱动的动力学朗之万过程在低正则性框架下的基本性质理论。研究结果表明，即使漂移项不连续，这些过程仍具有良好的结构和谱性质。特别地，对于旋转不变α-稳定噪声驱动的情况，证明了弱解的存在唯一性以及平稳分布和拟平稳分布的存在性。当漂移项光滑时，这些结果可推广到所有α∈(0,1]的情况。

Abstract: We investigate several fundamental properties of kinetic Langevin processes in $\mathbb{R}^{2d}$, defined as solutions to the following system: $$dx\_t = v\_t \, dt, \qquad dv\_t = \mathbf{B}(x\_t, v\_t) \, dt + dL\_t$$ where $(L\_t, t \ge 0)$ is a pure-jump L{é}vy process. Our analysis covers both the original process and its killed counterpart, where killing occurs upon exiting domains of the form $\mathscr{D} = \mathscr{O} \times \mathbb{R}^d$ for an arbitrary open set $\mathscr{O} \subset \mathbb{R}^d$. Operating within a low-regularity framework - where the drift $\mathbf{B}$ is not assumed to be continuous - we establish key structural and spectral properties for both the associated non-killed and killed semigroups. These include: the strong Feller property, weak continuity of trajectories with respect to initial conditions, topological irreducibility and the existence of a spectral gap. Furthermore, we prove, in this low-regularity framework, the existence and uniqueness of a weak solution when the driving noise is a rotationally invariant $α$-stable process, when $α\in (1,2)$. For this specific case, we show that the aforementioned properties hold and further establish the existence of densities within certain $L^m$ spaces as well as the Feller $C\_0(\mathbb R^{2d})$-semigroup property. Finally, we address the existence and uniqueness of stationary and quasi-stationary distributions, proving exponential ergodicity for the non-killed process and exponential convergence to the quasi-stationary limit for the conditioned process. We show that these results extend to every $α\in (0,1]$ when the drift is smooth.

</details>

### [165] [Analyticity, asymptotics and natural boundary for a one-point function of the finite-volume critical Ising chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06011)
*Yizhuang Liu*

TL;DR: 该研究通过Borel重求和（Borel resummation）分析临界周期Ising链中自旋算符单点函数（one-point function）的有限体积期望值，发现其在负实轴存在自然边界（natural boundary），且奇异行为与Lambert型级数在单位圆附近的奇异性相似。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究临界周期Ising链中自旋算符单点函数的解析性质，特别是其作为系统长度N的复解析函数时的奇异性结构。

Method: 通过Borel重求和将自旋算符单点函数的大N展开（large-N expansion）延拓为复解析函数，分析其在负实轴附近的奇异行为，并与Lambert型级数（Lambert-type series）的奇异性进行对比。

Result: 发现单点函数在负实轴存在自然边界，其奇异行为在指数映射后与奇数除数平方和（odd-divisor-squared sum）在单位圆附近的奇异性相同；该除数和也控制着Borel不连续性（Borel discontinuities）的强度。

Conclusion: 临界Ising链中自旋算符单点函数的解析结构具有非平凡的自然边界，其奇异性与数论中的除数和相关，并报告了有限体积自旋算符形状因子（form factor）中腿函数（leg function）的全阶大N渐近行为。

Abstract: This note reports the following observation: the finite-volume expectation value of the spin operator (the one-point function) between the $\mathbb{Z}_2$-even and odd ground states in the critical periodic Ising chain, when continued as a complex-analytic function of the system length $N$ through the Borel resummation of its large-$N$ expansion, has a natural boundary of analyticity along the negative real axis. The singular behavior near the negative real axis, after an exponential map, is the same as that of a Lambert-type series for the odd-divisor-squared sum near the unit circle $|z|=1$. The same divisor sum also governs the strengths of the Borel discontinuities of the one-point function's factorially-divergent large-$N$ asymptotics. We also report the all-order large-$N$ asymptotics of the leg function for the finite-volume spin-operator form factor, and the similarities to certain known quantities in the literature.

### [166] [Global Dynamical Structure of Einstein$-$Scalar Cosmological Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04994)
*Prasanta Sahoo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文对平坦FLRW宇宙学中最小耦合标量场驱动的动力学进行了全局分析，证明了标量场势陡度（potential steepness）的前向有界性，并建立了控制所有物理可接受解晚期动力学的紧致全局吸引子（compact global attractor）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在对平坦FLRW宇宙学中由最小耦合标量场驱动的动力学进行全局分析，建立对爱因斯坦-标量场系统晚期行为的统一理解，特别是研究势函数（scalar field potential）对宇宙演化动力学的影响。

Method: 采用不变流形理论（invariant manifold theory）和耗散动力系统（dissipative dynamical systems）技术，在适当的正则性和渐近性假设下分析标量场势函数。使用Conley指数（Conley index）对渐近动力学进行拓扑分类。

Result: 证明了标量场势陡度不会渐近无界，从而建立了标量场部分的前向有界性。系统存在紧致吸收集（compact absorbing set）和紧致全局吸引子，晚期动力学最多由两个独立自由度控制，对于渐近指数势（asymptotically exponential potentials）可进一步降至一维。

Conclusion: 研究结果为晚期标量场宇宙学提供了全局特征描述，建立了爱因斯坦-标量场系统中渐近捕获（asymptotic trapping）的模型无关动力学机制。渐近结构被证明是法向双曲（normally hyperbolic）且在势函数光滑扰动下结构稳定（structurally stable）。

Abstract: In this work, a global dynamical analysis of spatially flat FLRW cosmologies driven by a canonical scalar field minimally coupled to gravity is presented. Under suitable regularity and asymptotic assumptions on the scalar field potential, it is shown that the Einstein$-$scalar evolution admits no forward trajectory along which the potential steepness becomes asymptotically unbounded. This establishes forward boundedness of the scalar sector and yields the existence of a compact absorbing set for the induced cosmological flow. Using techniques from invariant manifold theory and dissipative dynamical systems, the evolution is shown to admit a compact global attractor governing the late time dynamics of all physically admissible solutions. The asymptotic behavior is further characterized by convergence toward a scalar field dominated invariant manifold, leading to a reduction in effective dynamical dimensionality. In particular, the late time dynamics is governed by at most two independent degrees of freedom, with further reduction to one dimension for asymptotically exponential potentials. The resulting asymptotic structure is shown to be normally hyperbolic and structurally stable under smooth perturbations of the scalar field potential. A topological classification of the asymptotic dynamics is obtained using the Conley index, identifying universality classes corresponding to one and two dimensional invariant sets. These results provide a global characterization of late time scalar field cosmologies and establish a model independent dynamical mechanism for asymptotic trapping in Einstein$-$scalar systems.

Result: 研究表明，足够致密的天体物理对象能够诱导极端的时空曲率，使引力场将光线弯曲到非凡程度，从而在空间的遥远区域产生源天体的"反射图像"或镜像外观。

### [168] [Black holes in rotating, electromagnetic backgrounds and topological Kerr-Newman-NUT spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05017)
*Marco Astorino*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文发现广义相对论和爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦理论中的一大类稳态轴对称黑洞解可以根据其背景性质进行分类。这些背景都属于一个统一的家族，包含所有已知的轴对称规则背景，并可通过双重维克旋转从拓扑推广的（加速）克尔-纽曼-NUT度规导出。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过分析黑洞解的背景性质，发现所有已知轴对称规则背景都属于一个独特的家族。该方法基于双重维克旋转（double Wick rotation）技术，从拓扑推广的（加速）克尔-纽曼-NUT度规（accelerating Kerr-Newman-NUT metric）导出这些背景。

Abstract: We notice that a large class of well behaved stationary and axisymmetric black hole solutions in general relativity and in the Einstein-Maxwell theory can be classified according to the properties of their background. Actually all these backgrounds belong to a unique family which includes simultaneously all the known axisymmetric and regular backgrounds: the swirling, the Bertotti-Robinson, the Bonnor-Melvin universe, the Witten's expanding bubble and also others novel, regular, rotating gravitational or electromagnetic environments. All these can be, fundamentally, re-conducted to the double Wick rotation of the topological generalisation of (accelerating) Kerr-Newman-NUT metric. We present a black hole embedded in an unexplored sector of the general background: Schwarzschild inside a generalised rotating (and possibly electromagnetic) universe. These results indicate that basically all the known analytical and exact single black hole solutions in the four-dimensional Einstein-Maxwell theory belong to the (accelerating) Kerr-Newman-NUT family embedded into backgrounds that are a subcase of the conjugated Kerr-Newman-NUT space-time with an angular manifold of arbitrary topology.

### [169] [Parametrized quasinormal modes, greybody factors and their correspondence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05084)
*Georgios Antoniou*

### [171] [Twisted doughnuts: Thick disk torus around equatorial asymmetric black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05604)
*Che-Yu Chen,Eva Hackmann,Audrey Trova*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了克尔黑洞（Kerr black hole）时空赤道面对称性破缺时，厚环面（thick tori）结构的扭曲效应。当赤道面对称性被超越广义相对论的效应破坏时，不仅开普勒薄盘（Keplerian thin disk）会弯曲，波兰甜甜圈模型（Polish doughnut models）的厚环面中心、尖点和整个结构也会向稳定开普勒轨道相同的方向扭曲。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于探讨超越广义相对论（beyond general relativity）的效应如何破坏克尔黑洞时空的赤道面对称性。当这种对称性破缺时，需要理解其对吸积盘结构的影响，特别是从薄盘扩展到厚环面配置的情况。

Method: 采用非自引力波兰甜甜圈模型（non-self-gravitating Polish doughnut models）来研究厚环面配置。通过分析恒定比角动量分布 $\ell(r,y)=\ell_0$ 的盘流体，明确展示了扭曲环面的形状，并将结果推广到非恒定角动量分布的一般情况。

Result: 研究发现，由于时空的赤道不对称性，环面的中心和尖点会向稳定开普勒轨道相同的方向偏离原始赤道面。整个环面配置也会向该方向扭曲，任何试图产生对称环面配置的不对称角动量分布 $\ell(r,y)$ 要么在赤道面附近定义不良，要么存在精细调节问题。

Conclusion: 结论表明，赤道面对称性破缺不仅影响薄盘结构，也会导致厚环面配置的系统性扭曲。这种扭曲效应是普遍的，不依赖于角动量分布的具体形式，为探测超越广义相对论的效应提供了新的观测特征。

Abstract: The Kerr black hole spacetime is symmetric with respect to a well-defined equatorial plane. When such a symmetry is broken, for instance, by some putative effects beyond general relativity, the Keplerian circular orbits around the black hole are distorted vertically away from the equatorial plane by an amount depending on the orbital radius. As a result, the Keplerian thin disk acquires a curved surface. In this work, we extend such results to thick tori configurations by considering non-self-gravitating Polish doughnut models. We show that due to the equatorial asymmetry of the spacetime, the centers and the cusps of tori are distorted away from the original equatorial plane toward the same direction as that experienced by the stable Keplerian orbits, and the entire tori configurations are twisted toward that direction as well. The shape of the distorted tori is demonstrated explicitly using a constant specific angular momentum profile $\ell(r,y)=\ell_0$ of the disk fluid. However, the result also applies to non-constant profiles of $\ell(r,y)$ generically in the sense that any asymmetric profile of $\ell(r,y)$ that attempts to produce a symmetric tori configuration either turns out to be ill-defined near the equatorial plane or suffers from fine-tuning issues.

Near these loci we compute translated jets, centre(-like) reductions, and normal forms governing persistence and transitions. For the quadratic potential $V(φ)=(1/2)m^{2}φ^{2}$, the effective slope $λ$ is dynamical. This reveals invariant gates, robust equilibrium continua, and vertical $γ$-thresholds for loss and recovery of normal hyperbolicity. We then construct an explicit stratification for the exponential class and a pull-back stratification for the massive case, together with the corresponding physical path maps into unfolding space. The resulting framework also organises slow-roll, ultra slow-roll, and oscillatory regimes.

We then perform a rigorous analytical verification of the Ehrenfest equations to determine whether the critical behavior of the phantom BTZ black hole corresponds to a second-order phase transition. Our results demonstrate adherence to both Ehrenfest relations, thereby confirming the occurrence of a second-order phase transition within the black hole system concurrent with the critical point. Furthermore, we explore the geodesic structure of the obtained solutions to analyze the motion of massive and massless test particles in the $F(R)$-phantom BTZ spacetime. The analysis demonstrates that stable timelike circular orbits exist only in the phantom regime for negative curvature backgrounds, while the phantom configuration also allows for stable circular photon orbits. These results underscore the significant influence of the phantom field and the $F(R)$ correction on the spacetime geometry and orbital dynamics.

Our findings indicate that increasing the monopole parameter gives rise to gravitational waves with slower damping oscillations. ### [175] [Probabilistic Evolution of Black Hole Thermodynamic States via Fokker-Planck Equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05785)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 分析揭示了两种不同的动力学机制：从不稳定最大值初始化的弛豫动力学（relaxation dynamics）和从亚稳态（metastable state）的相变。相变与熵产生率（entropy production rate）的显著峰值完全同步，表明势垒跨越（barrier crossing）过程由最大热力学耗散驱动。

Abstract: Employing the generalized free energy landscape and solving the associated Fokker-Planck equation, we obtain the time-dependent probability evolution of the order parameter for the RN-AdS black hole phase transitions. Furthermore, we characterize the non-equilibrium irreversibility and macroscopic uncertainty using the entropy production rate and the Shannon entropy. The results demonstrate that the phase transition synchronizes exactly with a prominent peak in the entropy production rate, identifying the barrier crossing event as a process fundamentally driven by maximum thermodynamic dissipation.

### [176] [Self-gravitating thin shells are dynamically unstable on all angular scales](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05980)
*Tristan Pitre,Berend Schneider,Eric Poisson*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究证明了广义相对论中静态、球对称、无限薄壳层的动力学不稳定性。壳层由具有正压状态方程的完美流体构成，外部产生史瓦西时空，内部为闵可夫斯基时空。研究发现存在两个纯虚频率模式，分别对应稳定振荡和指数增长，这种不稳定性在所有壳层致密度、绝热指数和多极阶数下均存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究广义相对论中薄壳结构的动力学稳定性，作为对Yang等人先前研究的补充。先前研究受限于小角度尺度的几何光学近似，而本研究旨在建立适用于所有角度尺度的完整理论框架。

Method: 方法包括引入闵可夫斯基时空、史瓦西时空和壳层物质的微扰。通过爱因斯坦场方程控制度规扰动，并利用Israel连接条件在壳层处匹配。物质扰动由流体力学方程控制，并在连接条件中产生源项。

Result: 研究发现存在两个纯虚频率模式：一个负值描述稳定振荡，一个正值描述指数增长。这种不稳定性在所有壳层致密度、绝热指数和多极阶数ℓ≥2的偶宇称扰动中均存在。所有其他准正则模式均描述阻尼振荡。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，具有薄壳表面的致密天体在动力学上是不稳定的，因此不能作为黑洞模拟物的可行模型。即使在牛顿力学框架下，薄壳结构对时间相关扰动也必然不稳定。

Abstract: We establish the dynamical instability of a static, spherically symmetric, and infinitesimally thin shell in general relativity. The shell is made up of a perfect fluid with a barotropic equation of state, and it produces a Schwarzschild spacetime in its exterior and a Minkowski spacetime in its interior. We reveal the existence of two modes with a purely imaginary frequency, one negative (which describes stable oscillations), the other positive (which describes an exponential growth); these modes occur for all sampled values of the shell's compactness and adiabatic index, and all sampled values of the multipolar order $\ell \geq 2$, in the even-parity sector of the perturbation. All other quasinormal modes describe damped oscillations. This study complements a recent analysis by Yang, Bonga, and Pen, which also concluded in a dynamical instability, but was limited by an eikonal approximation to small angular scales ($\ell \gg 1$); our treatment applies to all angular scales. The eigenvalue problem for the mode frequencies is formulated by introducing a perturbation of Minkowski spacetime, a perturbation of Schwarzschild spacetime, and a perturbation of the shell matter. The metric perturbations are governed by the Einstein field equations, and they are matched across the shell with the help of Israel's junction conditions. The matter perturbation is governed by the equations of fluid mechanics, and it produces a source term in the junction conditions. All calculations are carried out in full general relativity, but we also examine a nonrelativistic formulation of the problem; we show that a Newtonian shell also is necessarily unstable to a time-dependent perturbation. Our conclusion suggests that a compact object that features a thin shell at its surface will be dynamically unstable; this makes it nonviable as a model of black-hole mimicker.

### [177] [Quasinormal modes of coupled metric-dilaton perturbations in two-dimensional stringy black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05988)
*Wen-Hao Bian,Zhu-Fang Cui*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了二维弦理论中Mandal-Sengupta-Wadia（MSW）黑洞的本征度规-伸缩子耦合扰动的拟正则模（QNMs）。通过数值计算发现所有模式满足Im(ω)<0，证实了MSW黑洞在线性扰动下的稳定性。与外部标量场扰动不同，本征扰动具有非零实部，揭示了二维弦黑洞的内部动力学自由度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究二维弦理论中Mandal-Sengupta-Wadia（MSW）黑洞的本征度规-伸缩子耦合扰动对应的拟正则模（quasinormal modes, QNMs）。通过分析这些模式，可以探究黑洞的线性稳定性及其内部动力学特性。

Method: 通过适当的场重定义，将引力-伸缩子系统用共形因子和重定义的伸缩子场表示，使线性扰动方程在乌龟坐标中简化为耦合的薛定谔型本征值方程。施加标准的拟正则模边界条件（视界处纯入射波，空间无穷远处纯出射波），数值计算复频率谱。

Result: 所有拟正则模满足Im(ω)<0，证实了MSW黑洞在本征耦合扰动下的线性稳定性。与产生纯虚频率的外部标量场扰动不同，本征扰动通常表现出非零实部，对应于引力-伸缩子扇区的振荡模式。频率实部对泛音数呈现非单调依赖，而增加中心荷参数√k系统地减小阻尼率并延长弛豫时间。

Conclusion: 本征扰动探测了内部动力学自由度，揭示了二维弦黑洞弛豫动力学的特征。这些结果表明，本征度规-伸缩子耦合扰动提供了不同于外部场扰动的物理信息，对理解二维弦黑洞的动力学行为具有重要意义。

Abstract: We investigate the quasinormal modes (QNMs) associated with intrinsic metric-dilaton coupled perturbations of the Mandal-Sengupta-Wadia (MSW) black hole in two-dimensional string theory. Through suitable field redefinitions, the gravity-dilaton system is expressed in terms of the conformal factor and a redefined dilaton field, allowing the linear perturbation equations to be reduced to coupled Schrodinger-type eigenvalue equations in the tortoise coordinate. By imposing the standard QNMs' boundary conditions of purely ingoing waves at the horizon and purely outgoing waves at spatial infinity, we numerically determine the complex frequency spectrum. All modes satisfy Im$(ω)<0$, confirming the linear stability of the MSW black hole under intrinsic coupled perturbations. Unlike external scalar-field perturbations, which yield purely imaginary frequencies, the intrinsic perturbations generically exhibit nonvanishing real parts, corresponding to oscillatory modes of the gravity-dilaton sector. The real part of the frequency displays a nonmonotonic dependence on the overtone number, while increasing the central-charge parameter $\sqrt{k}$ systematically decreases the damping rate and prolongs the relaxation time. These results indicate that intrinsic perturbations probe internal dynamical degrees of freedom and reveal characteristic features of the relaxation dynamics of two-dimensional stringy black holes.

</details>


### [178] [Probing Kerr Symmetry Breaking with LISA Extreme-Mass-Ratio Inspirals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06053)
*Pablo F. Muguruza,Carlos F. Sopuerta*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了极端质量比旋进（EMRIs）作为引力波源，用于探测非克尔黑洞的时空几何结构。通过分析波形模型中的多极矩分量，评估了LISA探测器对克尔度规对称性破缺的约束能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极端质量比旋进（Extreme-Mass-Ratio Inspirals, EMRIs）是低频引力波的主要来源，其大量引力波周期使其成为探测局部时空几何的精确探针。研究旨在利用EMRIs探测克尔黑洞范式之外的广义致密天体，特别是那些具有丰富多极结构的非克尔天体。

Method: 在领先的后牛顿（post-Newtonian）和线性质量比阶次下，将质量四极矩和八极矩的轴对称与非轴对称分量纳入波形模型。采用EMRI解析近似（Analytic Kludge）模型框架研究这些修正对波形的影响，并使用费希尔矩阵（Fisher-matrix）分析评估LISA对多极矩偏离克尔值的约束能力。

Result: 研究表明，利用一年LISA数据（来自10M⊙致密天体旋入10^6M⊙旋转超大质量黑洞，信噪比为30），能够对克尔度规的两个基本对称性破缺施加严格约束。赤道对称性破缺可约束至10^-2水平，轴对称性破缺可约束至10^-3水平。

Conclusion: 未来LISA对EMRIs的观测将为黑洞结构和基础引力理论提供强有力的检验。特别地，LISA能够有效探测超越广义相对论的模型，如弦理论中提出的模糊球（fuzzball）模型等预测视界尺度修正的理论。

Abstract: Extreme-Mass-Ratio Inspirals (EMRIs) are one of the main sources of gravitational waves expected in the low-frequency band, where space-based detectors like Laser Interferometer Space Antenna (LISA) will operate. The large number of gravitational-wave cycles accumulated in the EMRI signal in the strong-field regime makes them precise probes of the local spacetime geometry, highly sensitive to deviations from the Kerr black hole paradigm. In this work, we investigate EMRIs around generic, non-Kerr compact objects characterized by a rich multipolar structure. At leading post-Newtonian and linear mass-ratio orders, we incorporate in the waveform model both axisymmetric and non-axisymmetric components of the mass quadrupole and octupole moments, parameterizing the breaking of two fundamental symmetries of the Kerr metric. We study the impact of these modifications on the waveform following the philosophy of EMRI \emph{Analytic Kludge} models. Then, using Fisher-matrix analysis, we assess LISA's capability to constrain deviations of the multipole moments from their Kerr values and the detection of symmetry-breaking effects. We analyze how effectively LISA will probe models beyond General Relativity that predict horizon-scale modifications, such as the fuzzball model proposed in string theory. Our results demonstrate that future LISA observations of EMRIs will provide powerful tests of black hole structure and the underlying theory of gravity. In particular, with one year of LISA data from the inspiral of a $10 M_{\odot}$ compact object into a rotating supermassive black hole of $10^{6} M_{\odot}$ and signal-to-noise ratio of 30, it will be possible to place tight bounds on deviations from the two fundamental symmetries of the Kerr metric, constraining equatorial symmetry breaking to the $10^{-2}$ level and axial symmetry breaking to the $10^{-3}$ level.

</details>


### [179] [Posterior Predictive Checks for Gravitational-wave Populations: Limitations and Improvements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06090)
*Simona J. Miller,Sophia Winney,Katerina Chatziioannou,Patrick M. Meyers*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究评估了后验预测检验（PPCs）在引力波天体物理模型拟合中的局限性，特别是在测量不确定性大的单事件参数（如自旋倾角）方面。研究比较了不同PPC方法的效果，发现基于最大似然参数的PPC比传统事件级PPC更具辨别力，但在当前探测器灵敏度下，自旋倾角数据仍不足以有效诊断模型误设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当选择模型来描述天体物理群体时，评估模型是否拟合数据以及如何改进至关重要。后验预测检验（posterior predictive checks, PPCs）是推断引力波源群体时广泛使用的模型拟合统计检验方法。然而，PPCs在评估具有大测量不确定性的单事件参数（如LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA（LVK）探测器可观测的双黑洞（binary black holes, BBHs）的自旋倾角）时表现出局限性。

Method: 研究评估了各种替代PPC方法在约束不良参数上的效果。比较了事件级与数据级参数的PPCs（如后验样本与最大似然点），并探索了两种额外的事件级PPC：部分预测检验（partial predictive checks）和分割预测检验（split predictive checks）。研究在模拟的GWTC-3.0类目录上进行了测试，并将PPC套件应用于最新的LVK目录GWTC-4.0的自旋幅度和倾角分布推断。

Result: 研究发现，无论测量不确定性如何，基于最大似然参数（maximum likelihood parameters）的PPC总是比任何事件级PPC更能识别模型误设（model misspecification）。然而，在调查模拟的GWTC-3.0类目录时，所有替代PPC方法相比传统方法均未显示出显著改进，表明在当前灵敏度下，数据中关于自旋倾角的有限信息不足以诊断模型误设。应用于GWTC-4.0目录时，发现其中使用的高斯分量自旋模型（Gaussian Component Spins model）低估了具有大自旋幅度的BBHs，而高估了具有完美反对齐倾角的BBHs。

Conclusion: 研究得出结论，在LVK探测器当前灵敏度下，自旋倾角数据的信息有限，无法有效诊断模型误设。应用于最新LVK目录时，发现现有高斯分量自旋模型对具有大自旋幅度的双黑洞预测不足，而对完美反对齐倾角的双黑洞预测过多。

Abstract: When selecting a model to characterize an astrophysical population, it is crucial to assess whether that model fits the data and, if not, how it can be improved. To this end, posterior predictive checks (PPCs) are a widely-used statistical test of model fit when inferring gravitational-wave source populations. However, PPCs exhibit limitations when assessing single-event parameters with large measurement uncertainty, like the spin tilt angles of the binary black holes (BBHs) observable with the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA (LVK) detectors. When single-event inference is prior-dominated, traditional PPCs fail to flag even very poor model fits. In this work, we assess the efficacy of various alternative PPCs on poorly-constrained parameters. We compare PPCs conducted on event- vs.~data-level parameters (e.g. posterior samples vs. maximum likelihood points), and explore two additional event-level PPCs: partial predictive checks and split predictive checks. Independent of measurement uncertainty, we find that PPCs on maximum likelihood parameters are always more discerning of model misspecification than any event-level PPC. However, when investigating simulated GWTC-3.0-like catalogs, none of the alternative PPCs show significant improvement over those traditionally used, indicating that at that sensitivity, any limited information in the data about spin tilts is insufficient to diagnose model misspecification.Finally, we apply our suite of PPCs to the spin magnitude and tilt distributions inferred in the most recent LVK catalog, GWTC-4.0. We conclude that the Gaussian Component Spins model used therein under-predicts BBHs with large spin magnitudes and over-predicts those with perfectly anti-aligned tilts.

</details>


### [180] [Algebraic approach to quantum gravity IV: applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06118)
*Shahn Majid*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提供了量子时空（quantum spacetime）和量子黎曼几何（quantum Riemannian geometry）在理论物理中应用的相对自洽介绍，包括单格点量子引力模型、卡鲁扎-克莱因理论推导、晶格变分微积分的诺特定理，以及适用于广义相对论的一般协变量子力学新理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在系统介绍量子时空和量子黎曼几何在理论物理中的应用，整合近期重要进展，包括量子引力模型、卡鲁扎-克莱因理论（Kaluza-Klein ansatz）的量子起源，以及发展适用于广义相对论背景的量子力学框架。

Method: 采用量子时空和量子黎曼几何的数学框架，应用单格点模型（single-plaquette model）研究量子引力，通过晶格变分微积分（variational calculus on a lattice）推导守恒量，并发展经典与量子测地线（classical and quantum geodesics）的新理论。

Result: 主要成果包括：计算了量子引力单格点模型中时空曲率涨落的真空能量；从量子时空推导出卡鲁扎-克莱因理论；获得了晶格变分微积分的精确守恒诺特荷（Noether charges）；建立了适用于广义相对论的一般协变量子力学（generally covariant quantum mechanics），并在黑洞案例中获得了初步有趣结果；发现了四星点欧几里得量子引力（Euclidean quantum gravity on a 4-pointed star）的相变。

Conclusion: 量子时空和量子黎曼几何为理论物理提供了富有前景的研究框架，已在多个领域取得实质性进展，包括量子引力、统一理论和协变量子力学。论文还讨论了当前和历史上的开放问题，并展望了未来研究方向。

Abstract: We provide a relatively self-contained introduction to the application of quantum spacetime and quantum Riemannian geometry to theoretical physics. Recent successes include calculation of the vacuum energy of spacetime curvature fluctuations in a single-plaquette model of quantum gravity, derivation of the Kaluza-Klein ansatz as a consequence of quantum spacetime, exactly conserved Noether charges from variational calculus on a lattice, and a new theory of classical and quantum geodesics. The latter leads to a theory of generally covariant quantum mechanics applicable in General Relativity with intriguing first results for the case of a black-hole. We discuss several open problems past and present, and how they might be addressed going forward. New results include a phase transition for Euclidean quantum gravity on a 4-pointed star.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在澄清平坦Friedmann-Robertson-Walker宇宙中宇宙时间t、共形时间η和尺度因子a(t)之间的基本关系，并理解这些关系如何影响粒子测地线和流形曲率。作者选择1+1维设定作为技术透明的教学平台，以提供清晰的物理洞察。

Method: 采用1+1维时空作为分析框架，分别处理辐射主导、物质主导和精确真空de Sitter三种宇宙学情形。建立了适用于任何平坦共形度规的仿射参数形式体系，并记录了向3+1维情况的直接扩展。

Result: 每种宇宙学情形（辐射主导、物质主导、de Sitter）产生不同的共形时间依赖关系，从而形成独特的测地线结构。建立了适用于任何平坦共形度规的通用仿射参数形式体系，并提供了向3+1维情况的扩展。

Conclusion: 论文通过1+1维教学框架澄清了宇宙时间、共形时间和尺度因子的基本关系，展示了不同宇宙学情形下测地线结构的差异。建立的通用形式体系为平坦共形度规下的分析提供了基础框架，保持了基本物理概念的清晰表达。

Abstract: We revisit conformal time $η$ in a spatially flat Friedmann--Robertson--Walker universe and use a $1+1$-dimensional setting as a technically transparent pedagogical arena. Our purpose is to clarify the relation among cosmic time $t$, conformal time $η$, and the scale factor $a(t)$, and then to follow how this relation governs the geodesics of freely moving particles and the curvature of the corresponding manifold. The radiation-dominated, matter-dominated, and exact vacuum-only de Sitter cases are treated separately, because each of them produces a distinct conformal-time dependence and therefore a distinct geodesic structure. We then write the affine-parameter formalism in a form that is genuinely general for any spatially flat conformal metric, and we record the straightforward extension to the spatially flat $3+1$ case. The presentation remains elementary in spirit, but the notation, the curvature formulas, and the de Sitter interpretation are kept explicit.

### [182] [Absorption and quasinormal modes by rotating acoustic black holes in Lorentz-violating background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06137)
*J. A. V. Campos,M. A. Anacleto,F. A. Brito,E. Passos,Amilcar R. Queiroz*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了洛伦兹对称性破缺对(2+1)维旋转声学黑洞的吸收截面和准正规模的影响，发现对称性破缺会增加吸收截面并改变准正规模式的振荡特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探究洛伦兹对称性破缺（Lorentz symmetry violation）对旋转声学黑洞（rotating acoustic black hole）物理特性的影响，特别是在(2+1)维度下对吸收截面（absorption cross section）和准正规模（quasinormal modes）的效应。

Method: 研究方法包括解析分析和数值计算：在低频率和高频率区域进行解析分析，同时通过积分径向方程（radial equation）进行数值计算，以全面考察吸收截面和准正规模的变化规律。

Result: 结果显示洛伦兹破缺在所有能量尺度上均增加吸收截面，旋转参数$B$的贡献甚至在低频率区域也显现；对于准正规模，对称性破缺降低频率实部并增加虚部幅值，表明振荡阻尼更快。

Conclusion: 洛伦兹对称性破缺显著影响旋转声学黑洞的吸收特性和准正规模式行为，表现为吸收增强和振荡阻尼加快，旋转参数在低频率区域的作用揭示了对称性破缺与黑洞旋转的耦合效应。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the effects of Lorentz symmetry violation on the absorption cross section and quasinormal modes of a rotating acoustic black hole in (2+1) dimensions. The absorption cross section was analyzed analytically, using the low and high frequency regimes, and numerically, through integration of the radial equation. The results showed that Lorentz violation increases the absorption cross section at all energy scales, with a contribution from the rotation parameter $B$ appearing even in the low frequency regime. For the quasinormal modes, we observed that symmetry breaking decreases the real part of the frequencies and increases the magnitude of the corresponding imaginary part, indicating a faster damping of the oscillations.

### [183] [Long-time behavior of exact and numerical solutions of stochastic evolution equations on the sphere](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05644)
*David Cohen,Björn Müller,Andrea Papini*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 该研究分析了球面上线性随机演化方程精确解和数值近似的长时间行为，重点关注随机波动方程、随机薛定谔方程和随机麦克斯韦方程组三种经典模型。研究发现前向和后向欧拉-丸山格式无法重现精确解的长时间行为，而随机指数积分器能够保持物理量的正确长时间行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于分析球面上线性随机演化方程的长时间行为，特别关注数学物理中的三种经典模型：随机波动方程（stochastic wave equation）、随机薛定谔方程（stochastic Schrödinger equation）和随机麦克斯韦方程组（stochastic Maxwell's equations）。研究旨在评估不同时间积分器在描述依赖于强迫项的物理量（如能量、质量和动量）演化时的表现。

Method: 研究方法包括对精确解和数值近似的长时间行为分析，重点考察了几种广泛使用的时间积分器。研究通过理论证明和数值实验相结合的方式，分析了这些积分器在保持物理量长时间行为方面的性能，特别关注依赖于强迫项的物理量演化。

Result: 研究结果表明，前向和后向欧拉-丸山格式（forward and backward Euler-Maruyama schemes）无法重现精确解的长时间行为。相反，随机指数积分器（stochastic exponential integrator）能够保持所关注物理量的正确长时间行为。数值实验进一步验证了这些理论发现。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，对于球面上的线性随机演化方程，随机指数积分器在保持物理量长时间行为方面优于欧拉-丸山格式。该发现为选择适当的数值方法求解此类数学物理问题提供了理论指导。

Abstract: We investigate the long-time behavior of exact solutions and numerical approximations of linear stochastic evolution equations defined on the sphere. We focus on three classical models arising in mathematical physics: the stochastic wave equation, the stochastic Schrödinger equation, and the stochastic Maxwell's equations. For these SPDEs, we analyze several widely used time integrators with respect to trace formulas describing the evolution of physically relevant quantities such as energy, mass, and momentum dependent on the forcing term. In particular, we prove that the forward and backward Euler-Maruyama schemes fail to reproduce the correct long-time behavior of the exact solutions. In addition, we prove that the stochastic exponential integrator preserves the correct long-time behavior of the physical quantities of interest. Finally, several numerical experiments are provided to illustrate our theoretical findings.

</details>

### [184] [A Data-Driven Fast Simulation Approach for MAPS-based Detectors and their Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05893)

Conclusion: 本文提出的参数化仿真工具为像素传感器仿真提供了高效替代方案，不依赖专有工艺信息，特别适用于大型系统和高命中率环境。对MALTA2传感器的优化研究为下一代MALTA3传感器的重新设计提供了性能优化基础。

Abstract: A parametric simulation tool for pixel sensors is presented. A realistic pixel response is simulated purely based on measurement input, without requiring detailed knowledge of the underlying manufacturing process. As such, it provides an efficient alternative to the use of Technology Computer-Aided Design simulations, which typically depend on proprietary process information. Due to its parametric approach, the package is fast and thus particularly useful for larger detector systems and high hit rate environments. This work presents measurements, simulation and its validation for the MALTA2 sensor. It is a small collection electrode monolithic active pixel sensor produced in the Tower 180nm Complementary Metal-Oxide-Semiconductor imaging process. Modifications to the sensor's periphery, mainly in the hit merger, are studied in order to optimize the performance for tracking and calorimetry. This optimization is of special interest as part of the MALTA3 sensor redesign in the 65nm Tower Partners Semiconductor Co. process.
