  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 亚赫兹频段（0.1-10 Hz）是引力波探测中基本未开发的领域，主要受地面强噪声源限制。CHRONOS旨在填补这一空白，同时探索连接引力波天文学与地球物理监测的科学潜力。

Method: 采用低温运行（cryogenic operation）、交叉扭杆配置（cross torsion-bar configuration）、三角形萨格纳克干涉仪（triangular Sagnac interferometer）和速度计读数方案（speed meter readout scheme）。通过FINESSE3进行解析和干涉模拟，评估噪声预算并表征量子、热和环境噪声的相对贡献。

Result: CHRONOS在2 Hz处达到约$h \sim 10^{-18} Hz^{-1/2}$的应变灵敏度，随机引力波背景$Ω_{GW}$约为$2 \times 10^{-3}$。在40公里范围内，通过探测即时重力梯度信号，地震预警系统可提前约2.92至6.90秒发出警报。

Conclusion: CHRONOS在低频段实现了有竞争力的灵敏度，展示了连接引力波天文学与地球物理监测的科学潜力，为低频探测器技术的进一步发展提供了动力。

Abstract: CHRONOS is a proposed gravitational-wave detector designed to operate in the sub-Hz frequency range (0.1 to 10 Hz), a largely unexplored band due to strong noise sources that hamper ground-based detectors. It employs cryogenic operation, a cross torsion-bar configuration, a triangular Sagnac interferometer, and a speed meter readout scheme to overcome key noise limitations, targeting a strain sensitivity of $h \sim 10^{-18} Hz^{-1/2}$ around 2 Hz and a stochastic gravitational wave background of $Ω_{GW}$ approximately $2 \times 10^{-3}$ at 2 Hz. Using analytical and interferometric simulations with FINESSE3, we evaluate the noise budget of CHRONOS and characterize the relative contributions of quantum, thermal, and environmental noise sources. Our results demonstrate that CHRONOS achieves competitive sensitivity at low frequencies. The feasibility of using CHRONOS in an earthquake early-warning system by detecting prompt gravity-gradient signals is also investigated, and is predicted to be faster by approximately 2.92 to 6.90 seconds within 40 km. These findings highlight the scientific potential of CHRONOS, bridging gravitational-wave astronomy and geophysical monitoring, and motivating further development of low-frequency detector technologies.

</details>


### [186] [High-Temperature and High-Speed Atomic Force Microscopy Using a qPlus Sensor in Liquid via Quadpod Scanner and Hybrid-Loop Frequency Demodulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04970)
*Yuto Nishiwaki,Toru Utsunomiya,Takashi Ichii*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 开发了配备qPlus传感器的高温高速原子力显微镜（AFM），实现了200°C以上熔融金属/固体界面的原子分辨率成像，成功观测到Ga/PtGa_x界面在210°C下的非对称表面结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 需要实现200°C以上非水液体/固体界面的原子分辨率成像，以研究高温下熔融金属与固体界面的结构特性，这对于注射成型、焊接和液态金属催化剂制备等应用具有重要意义。

Method: 开发了适用于大质量qPlus传感器（2.3 g）的尖端扫描高速Quadpod扫描器，通过高速扫描和热隔离增强热漂移耐受性；建立了混合环路频率解调技术（Hybrid-loop frequency demodulation technique），为低共振频率传感器提供比传统锁相环更宽的带宽。

Result: 在约210°C下实现了Ga/PtGa_x熔融界面的原子分辨率成像，观测到具有超结构的斜方晶格表面，这与室温下放置96小时的样品中观察到的原始矩形晶格明显不同。

Conclusion: 开发的高温高速AFM技术能够可视化200°C以上的非水液体/固体界面，为高温界面研究提供了新的实验手段，在注射成型、焊接和液态金属催化剂制备等领域具有广泛应用潜力。

Abstract: Atomic-resolution imaging on molten metal/solid interfaces at temperatures above 200 °C was achieved using a high-temperature, high-speed atomic force microscope (AFM) equipped with a qPlus sensor. A tip-scanning high-speed Quadpod scanner for a large mass load of qPlus sensor (2.3 g) was developed to enhance thermal drift tolerance by high-speed scanning and thermal insulation from the heated specimen. This scanner has dominant resonant frequencies of 7.05 kHz (lateral) / 29.7 kHz (vertical) without a load. In addition, the Hybrid-loop frequency demodulation technique for low-resonant-frequency ($f_0$) sensors with a wider bandwidth than conventional phase-locked loop was also established, providing a demodulation bandwidth of $B_{Δf_\mathrm{inst}}\sim 0.26 f_0$ without exceeding the theoretical noise of the input deflection signal. Combining these techniques enabled atomic-resolution imaging on the molten $\mathrm{Ga/PtGa_x}$ interface at $\sim$210 °C. The topographic images obtained at $\sim$210 °C showed a relatively low-symmetry surface with an oblique lattice with a superstructure, which differed from the primitive rectangular lattice observed in the non-heated sample left at room temperature for 96 h. This demonstrates that the developed high-temperature, high-speed AFM techniques for qPlus sensors enable visualization of non-aqueous liquid/solid interfaces above 200 °C at atomic resolution, which has various potential applications, such as injection modeling, soldering, and the fabrication of liquid-metal-based catalysts.

### [187] [Hunting Dark Matter with the Einstein Telescope](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06082)
*A. J. Iovino,M. Maggiore,N. Muttoni,A. Riotto*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该论文探讨了过轻的原初黑洞（primordial black holes）通过强团簇形成较重黑洞的可能性，这些较重黑洞可能构成宇宙暗物质（dark matter）的全部，并产生可被爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope）探测到的平坦随机引力波背景（stochastic background of gravitational waves）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过轻的原初黑洞会蒸发，因此受到宇宙微波背景（Cosmic Microwave Background）畸变等多种限制。然而，如果它们形成时具有强团簇性，相应的晕（haloes）可能坍缩成较重的黑洞，这些黑洞可能构成宇宙的全部暗物质。

Method: 论文未在摘要中明确描述具体方法，但基于物理机制分析：研究原初黑洞的强团簇形成及其晕的坍缩过程，探讨由此产生的较重黑洞作为暗物质候选者的可能性。

Result: 该情景的间接信号是产生平坦的随机引力波背景，这种信号可以被爱因斯坦望远镜探测到，为验证该暗物质形成机制提供了观测途径。

Conclusion: 通过强团簇形成的较重原初黑洞可能构成宇宙的全部暗物质，其产生的引力波信号为这一假设提供了可观测的验证手段，绕过了轻质量原初黑洞的蒸发限制。

Abstract: Too light primordial black holes evaporate and are therefore strongly constrained by various bounds, e.g. Cosmic Microwave Background distortion. However, if they are formed strongly clustered, the corresponding haloes may collapse in heavier black holes which may form the entirety of the dark matter of the universe. The indirect signal of such scenario is the production of a flat stochastic background of gravitational waves which is detectable by the Einstein Telescope.

### [188] [Stress network dynamics influence on large particle segregation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05127)
*Alexander J. Navarrete,Leonardo Gordillo,Tomás Trewhela*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过光弹性实验可视化二维颗粒剪切流中的应力链，揭示了挤压排出机制与应力网络动力学之间的关联，表明较大尺寸比导致更长的应力链和更广泛的颗粒参与应力传递。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 颗粒流中的粒径偏析（particle-size segregation）现象普遍存在于自然和工业过程中，其中挤压排出（squeeze expulsion）机制缺乏清晰的力学解释和直接实验证据，主要由于颗粒介质中应力测量的困难。

Method: 研究使用透明双折射圆盘在二维颗粒剪切盒（bidimensional granular shear cell）中进行实验，通过光弹性（photoelasticity）可视化应力链。采用颗粒追踪测速法（Particle Tracking Velocimetry）和G平方分析（G-square analysis）量化颗粒轨迹并识别活跃颗粒，通过间隙因子（gap factor）测量侵入体周围的应力链长度和结构。

Result: 实验结果表明挤压排出机制强烈依赖于应力传递，较大的尺寸比导致更长的应力链和更多颗粒参与全局应力网络。应力波动通过形成各向异性的应力链主导或限制侵入体运动，澄清了力网络动力学与偏析力学之间的联系。

Conclusion: 该研究通过阐明力网络动力学与偏析力学之间的关联，推进了对颗粒偏析的理解，为挤压排出机制提供了直接的实验证据和力学解释。

Abstract: A plethora of natural and industrial shear-driven granular flows exhibit particle-size segregation. Its occurrence is commonly attributed to two primary mechanisms: kinetic sieving and squeeze expulsion. While kinetic sieving is relatively well understood, squeeze expulsion lacks a clear mechanical explanation and direct experimental evidence due to difficulties in measuring stresses in granular media. Here, we investigate force networks around a large intruder in a bidimensional granular shear cell. We use transparent, birefringent disks to visualize stress chains via photoelasticity. Experiments were conducted with two different granular media to study force chains over size ratios between the intruder and surrounding particles of 1.25 to 4.0. Particle Tracking Velocimetry and G-square analysis are used to quantify particle trajectories and identify active grains. These methods enable us to measure force-chain lengths and structures around the intruder through the gap factor. Our results confirm that squeeze-expulsion strongly depends on stress transmission. Larger size ratios lead to longer force chains and greater particle participation in the global stress network. In parallel, stress fluctuations predominate in driving or restraining intruder motion by forming anisotropic force chains. These findings advance the understanding of granular segregation by clarifying the link between force-network dynamics and segregation mechanics.

</details>


### [189] [A Modular 3D-Printed Design to Investigate Prebiotic Chemical Systems in Hot Spring Pools](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05223)
*Arslan Siddique,Dev Chauhan,Alethea Dutton,Kavish Reddy,Soumya Kanti De,Albert C. Fahrenbach,Tracie Barber,Martin Van Kranendonk,Anna Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种模块化3D打印热泉场模拟器，用于模拟生命起源的热泉假说环境，成功观察到脂质囊泡的自发形成及有机物质的封装。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生命起源的热泉假说（hot spring hypothesis）认为原始细胞（protocells）可能在热泉池中形成并封装有机物质。先前研究主要模拟单一池中的干湿循环（wet-dry cycles），无法模拟热泉场的复杂条件，如不同矿物学、温度、pH变化以及多个池之间的水流交换。

Method: 研究设计了一种模块化3D打印热泉场模拟器（hydrothermal field simulator），通过控制一系列相连池的变异性来模拟热泉场的复杂特性，包括干湿循环、温度、pH、矿物学以及不同流体的混合。

Result: 使用癸酸:癸醇（4:1）或磷脂POPC:POPG（1:1）组成的膜结构，在模拟器池中通过多次干湿循环自发形成脂质囊泡（lipid vesicles）。观察到囊泡形态的显著差异，包括厚壁多层、薄壁寡层、单层以及巨型单层囊泡（giant unilamellar vesicles）。有机物质封装（cargo encapsulation）在细胞样巨型单层囊泡和小型寡层囊泡中更为有利。

Conclusion: 热泉模拟器为研究其他热泉过程提供了可定制化途径，如生命起源前的化学反应（prebiotic chemical reactions）、矿物表面催化以及热泉场动力学的复杂性，为生命起源研究提供了更接近自然条件的实验平台。

Abstract: The emergence of membranous compartments (protocells) with encapsulated genetic material was a crucial step life's origin and evolution. The hot spring hypothesis for the origin of life suggests that protocells could have formed in hot spring pools and encapsulated organic matter. Previous investigations have focused on mimicking wet-dry (WD) cycles within a single pool, which precludes simulation of many hydrothermal field conditions, such as differential mineralogy, variable temperature and pH and water flow between multiple hot spring pools. Here, we present a modular 3D-printed hydrothermal field simulator that mimics the complex nature of hot spring fields by controlling the variability of a series of linked pools, including WD cycles, temperature, pH, mineralogy, and mixing of different fluids. Results from using the prototype hot spring field design demonstrate the ability to spontaneously form lipid vesicles that encapsulate organic matter within membranous compartments comprised of decanoic acid:decanol (4:1) or the phospholipids POPC:POPG (1:1). We observed distinct morphological differences in the vesicles, ranging from thick-walled multilamellar, thin-walled oligolamellar and unilamellar as well as giant unilamellar vesicles formed under multiple WD cycles in the simulator pools. Cargo encapsulation was favoured in the cell-like giant unilamellar and small oligolamellar vesicles. Overall, hot-spring simulator offers a customisable avenue for studying other hot spring processes such as prebiotic chemical reactions, mineral surface catalysis, and the complexity of hydrothermal field dynamics.

</details>


### [190] [Ion-Containing Bottlebrush Elastomers as Pressure-Sensitive Electroadhesives](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05247)
*Hao Dong,Intanon Lapkriengkri,Nadia Chapple,Hyunki Yeo,Alexandra Zele,Hiba Wakidi,Thuc-Quyen Nguyen,Michael L. Chabinyc,Christopher M. Bates,Megan T. Valentine*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种基于含离子瓶刷聚合物（ion-containing bottlebrush polymers）的低压压敏电粘合剂（low-voltage pressure-sensitive electroadhesives）材料设计框架，该材料结合了传统电粘合剂按需可逆性与压敏粘合剂可调适性，在低于2V电压下实现高达4.5以上的开关比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统电粘合剂（electroadhesives）缺乏压敏粘合剂（pressure-sensitive adhesives, PSAs）的可调适性，而PSAs又缺乏电粘合剂的按需可逆性。本研究旨在开发一种结合两者优势的新型材料，实现低压操作下的可逆粘合。

Method: 设计了两种互补的瓶刷聚合物，分别带有柔性侧链和独立可调的阴离子或阳离子基团，交联后形成柔软坚韧的弹性体。当两种带相反电荷的瓶刷网络接触时，形成平滑连续的界面，该界面因存在可移动抗衡离子（mobile counterions）而局部电荷中性。

Result: 在低电压（低于2V）下，可移动离子向电极迁移，形成界面异质结（interfacial heterojunction）和显著静电吸引力，增强粘附力，开关比（on/off ratio）可达4.5以上。即使在低至18C/g的电荷密度下，瓶刷电粘合剂仍保持低压操作和PSA类力学性能。

Conclusion: 瓶刷电粘合剂的低压操作特性和类似压敏粘合剂的力学性能，为软体机器人（soft robots）、触觉设备（haptic devices）和生物医学设备（biomedical devices）等应用创造了新机遇。

Abstract: This study presents a materials-design framework for low-voltage pressure-sensitive electroadhesives based on ion-containing bottlebrush polymers that combine the on-demand reversibility of traditional electroadhesives with the tunable conformability typical of pressure-sensitive adhesives (PSAs). Two complementary bottlebrush polymers bearing pendant flexible side chains and independently tunable anionic or cationic groups were designed to form soft and tough elastomers after crosslinking. When the two oppositely charged bottlebrush networks were brought into contact, a smooth, continuous interface formed, which is locally charge neutral due to the presence of mobile counterions. At low voltages (less than 2 V), mobile ions migrate toward the electrodes, creating an interfacial heterojunction and significant electrostatic attraction that enhances adhesion, yielding an on/off ratio of up to more than 4.5. The low-voltage operation and PSA-like mechanics of bottlebrush electroadhesives, even at charge density as low as 18 C/g, create opportunities in applications such as soft robots, haptic devices, and biomedical devices.

</details>


### [191] [Linear Viscoelasticity of Semidilute Unentangled Flexible Polymer Solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05338)
*Amit Varakhedkar,P. Sunthar,J. Ravi Prakash*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过布朗动力学模拟（Brownian dynamics simulations）探究了稀溶液和半稀非缠结（semidilute unentangled）柔性聚合物溶液的线性粘弹性响应，建立了微观链动力学与宏观粘弹性响应之间的联系，并利用连续细粒化技术（successive fine-graining technique）系统性地考虑了有限链长效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在建立柔性聚合物溶液在稀溶液和半稀非缠结区域中，微观链动力学与宏观粘弹性响应之间的关联。这有助于理解不同浓度和溶剂条件下聚合物溶液的流变行为。

Method: 采用布朗动力学模拟（Brownian dynamics simulations）方法，在广泛的浓度范围和链离散化程度下，计算了松弛模量（relaxation modulus）和动态模量（dynamic moduli）。研究涵盖了θ溶剂（$θ$ solvent）和良溶剂（good solvent）条件。

Result: 在稀溶液极限下，模拟重现了预期的类齐姆（Zimm-like）行为，其时间和频率中区的幂律标度依赖于溶剂质量。在半稀非缠结区域，随着浓度增加，由于排除体积和流体力学相互作用的屏蔽，观察到系统性地向类劳斯（Rouse-like）动力学的交叉。与实验测量结果对比，在两种浓度区域下的储能模量（storage modulus）以及低、中频下的损耗模量（loss modulus）均表现出极好的一致性。

Conclusion: 研究通过模拟成功连接了微观链动力学与宏观粘弹性响应，并利用连续细粒化技术（successive fine-graining technique）系统性地处理了有限链离散化效应，从而能够定量预测无限链长极限下的损耗模量。

Abstract: The linear viscoelastic response of flexible polymer solutions in the dilute and semidilute unentangled regimes is investigated using Brownian dynamics simulations. The relaxation modulus and dynamic moduli are computed over a wide range of concentrations and chain discretizations for both $θ$ and good solvents to establish the connection between microscopic chain dynamics and macroscopic viscoelastic response. In the dilute limit, the simulations recover the expected Zimm-like behavior with solvent-quality-dependent power-law scaling in the intermediate time and frequency regimes, while in the semidilute unentangled regime a systematic crossover to Rouse-like dynamics is observed with increasing concentration due to the screening of excluded volume and hydrodynamic interactions. Comparison with experimental measurements shows excellent agreement for the storage modulus across both concentration regimes and for the loss modulus at low and intermediate frequencies, with deviations at high frequencies as a result of finite-chain discretization effects. These finite-chain length effects are systematically accounted for using the successive fine-graining technique, enabling quantitative prediction of the loss modulus in the infinite-chain length limit.

</details>


### [192] [Taylor dispersion in a soft channel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05592)
*Aditya Jha,Masoodah Gunny,Joshua D Mcgraw,Yacine Amarouchene,Thomas Salez*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究发展了软性轴对称通道中溶质分散理论，发现通道壁的柔顺性（softness）通过Winkler响应增强有效对流速度和分散系数，对生物学和微流控技术具有实际意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在微流控应用中，通道边界的柔顺性（compliance）会改变流体动力学流动，从而影响溶质输运。本研究旨在探索软性通道中溶质分散（solutal dispersion）的理论基础。

Method: 基于多时间尺度分析（multiple-time-scale analysis），推导了软性轴对称通道中溶质浓度动力学的修正宏观输运方程（macro-transport equation）。通道壁通过Winkler响应（Winkler response）对流体动压力做出反应。

Result: 主要发现是柔顺性增强了有效对流速度（effective advection velocity）和分散系数（dispersion coefficient）。该理论适用于稳态（steady）和脉动（pulsatile）配置下的溶质输运分析。

Conclusion: 软性通道壁的柔顺性显著影响溶质分散过程，增强了对流和分散效应。这一发现对理解生物学系统中的输运现象和优化微流控技术具有重要应用价值。

Abstract: Diffusion of a solute along a channel is enhanced by hydrodynamic flow, a phenomenon known as Taylor dispersion. In microfluidic applications, the compliance of the channel boundaries modifies the hydrodynamic flow and thus solutal transport. Here, we develop the theory of solutal dispersion in a soft, axisymmetric channel where the channel walls respond to the hydrodynamic pressure through a Winkler response. By deriving the modified macro-transport equation for the solutal concentration dynamics based on multiple-time-scale analysis, we explore the influence of softness on solutal transport for steady and pulsatile configurations. Our main finding is that softness enhances the effective advection velocity and dispersion coefficient, which might have practical implication in biology and microfluidic technology.

</details>


### [193] [Inertial chiral active Brownian particle: Transition from Gaussian to platykurtic distribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05722)
*M Muhsin,S Deion,M Sahoo*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过数值模拟发现，当谐波势阱频率与手性频率匹配时，惯性手性活性布朗粒子的位置分布会从高斯分布转变为低峰态分布，同时均方位移呈现非单调特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索手性活性布朗粒子在谐波约束下的动力学行为，特别是研究约束频率与手性频率匹配时的特殊效应，这对于控制手性微泳体在光学或声学势阱中的输运和空间分布具有重要意义。

Method: 采用数值模拟方法研究惯性手性活性布朗粒子在谐波势阱中的动力学，并通过分析位置分布的峰度（kurtosis）和稳态均方位移（mean square displacement, MSD）作为谐波频率的函数。在旋转过阻尼极限下，推导了峰度和稳态均方位移的精确表达式。

Result: 当谐波频率与手性频率匹配时，位置分布从高斯分布转变为低峰态分布（platykurtic distribution），峰度出现极小值。同时，稳态均方位移呈现非单调特征，仅在谐波频率与手性频率同量级时达到最大值。在旋转过阻尼极限下，定性行为保持一致，但峰度的极小值特征减弱且最小值更高。

Conclusion: 谐波约束频率与手性频率的匹配会导致手性活性布朗粒子分布和输运性质的显著变化，这一发现为通过调节势阱参数优化手性微泳体在光学或声学陷阱中的空间分布提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamics of an inertial chiral active Brownian particle in the presence of a harmonic confinement. Through numerical simulation, we observe that when the harmonic frequency becomes comparable to the chiral frequency, the position distribution transitions from a Gaussian to a platykurtic distribution, corresponding to short tails with a nearly uniform probability near the minimum of the potential. This result is further confirmed by analyzing the kurtosis of the position of the particle as a function of harmonic frequency, which exhibits a dip when the harmonic frequency matches the chiral frequency. At the same time, the steady state mean square displacement (MSD) shows a non-monotonic feature with the harmonic frequency and shows a maximum only when the harmonic frequency is of the same order as the chiral frequency. In the rotational overdamped limit of the same model, we have calculated the exact expression for kurtosis, steady state MSD and find that the qualitative behavior remains the same. Kurtosis still exhibits a dip in the matching of chiral and harmonic frequencies, but the feature is less pronounced with a higher minimum. These findings might be relevant for controlling the transport and spatial distribution of chiral microswimmers in optical or acoustic traps, where confinement can be tuned to optimize particle distribution.

</details>


### [194] [Free chiral self-propelled robots compared to active Brownian circle swimmers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05723)
*Thomas Kiechl,Amy Altshuler,Anton Lüders,Yael Roichman,Thomas Franosch*

TL;DR: 该研究通过视频追踪自由手性hexbug（Nano-Newton系列）的运动，并将其与过阻尼朗之万方程（overdamped Langevin equations）描述的活性布朗圆泳者（active Brownian circle swimmers, ABCs）模型预测进行比较，发现两者在均方位移和中间散射函数（intermediate scattering function, ISF）方面具有良好一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宏观活性物质系统（macroscopic active matter systems）如鬃毛机器人（bristle bots）为研究高度可见尺度上的非平衡动力学（nonequilibrium dynamics）提供了理想平台。为充分利用其可观测性，需要精确数学模型来验证实验。

Method: 通过视频追踪（video tracking）研究自由手性hexbug（Nano-Newton系列）的运动，并将实验结果与基于过阻尼朗之万方程（overdamped Langevin equations）的活性布朗圆泳者（active Brownian circle swimmers, ABCs）模型的理论预测进行比较。

Result: Hexbug动力学与ABC模型预测在均方位移（mean-squared displacement）和中间散射函数（intermediate scattering function, ISF）方面表现出良好一致性。主要偏差出现在实空间传播子（real-space propagator）的短时行为中，该处平动噪声（translational noise）最为明显。

Conclusion: 当平动噪声（translational noise）影响可忽略时，基于过阻尼朗之万方程（overdamped Langevin equations）的模型可作为描述hexbug运动的稳健框架。基于ISF和传播子（propagator）的分析方法在表征活性系统方面表现出高灵敏度，为改进粗粒度模型（coarse-grained models）和推进宏观活性系统理论理解开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Macroscopic active matter systems, such as bristle bots, provide a compelling platform for investigating nonequilibrium dynamics at highly visible scales. To fully leverage their accessibility, accurate mathematical models are needed to corroborate experiments. In this work, we study the motion of a free chiral hexbug (Nano-Newton Series) via video tracking and compare the results to theoretical predictions from overdamped Langevin equations for active Brownian circle swimmers (ABCs). We find good agreement between the hexbug's dynamics and ABC model predictions, particularly for the mean-squared displacement and the intermediate scattering function (ISF). Deviations between the hexbug data and the ABC model arise primarily in the short-time behavior of the real-space propagator, where translational noise is most evident. Our results generally support the use of models based on overdamped Langevin equations as a robust framework for describing hexbug motion when the influence of translational noise is negligible. Moreover, they demonstrate the sensitivity of ISF- and propagator-based analyses in characterizing active systems. Our approach opens new avenues toward refining coarse-grained models and advancing the theoretical understanding of macroscopic active systems.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 盐沿自由表面爬升现象（salt creeping）的动力学机制尚未被完全理解，特别是其动态演化过程需要更深入的研究。

Method: 研究结合理论模型与受控实验，并通过数值模拟（numerical simulations）补充分析微观晶体结构在不同外部条件（湿度和温度）下的演化。

Result: 识别出三个不同的动力学区域（kinetic regimes）：垂直壁上盐结晶沉积高度的初始指数增长、线性增长阶段，以及最终高度饱和而晶体沉积厚度呈对数增长（logarithmically）的阶段。

Abstract: The phenomenon of salt creeping along a free surface remains only partially understood, particularly with respect to its dynamics. In this work, combining a theoretical model with controlled experiments, we identify three distinct kinetic regimes: an initial exponential growth of the height of the crystallized salt deposit on vertical walls, followed by a linear regime, and a final stage where the height saturates while the crystal deposit thickens logarithmically. This unified description makes it possible to follow the macroscopic kinetics of salt growth on a free surface from its nucleation to saturation. In addition, we complement this macroscopic analysis with numerical simulations that shed light on the evolution of the microscopic crystal structure under varying external conditions (humidity and temperature).

### [196] [Collective spatial reorganization from arrest to peeling and migration through density-dependent mobility in internal-state coordinates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05880)
*Yagyik Goswami*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究提出一个最小模型，用于描述相互作用群体在耦合的空间坐标和内部状态坐标中的演化，揭示了仅通过内部状态迁移率即可独立控制大规模空间重组，驱动从停滞聚集态到边界主导剥离迁移态的转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 发育、再生和疾病中的许多问题涉及空间组织和内部状态的同步演化，同时包含局部相互作用和拥挤效应。这促使研究者建立一个最小模型，用于研究相互作用群体在耦合的空间和内部状态坐标中的演化，特别关注从紧凑或停滞状态向边界主导剥离迁移的重组转变。

Method: 研究聚焦于一个具有生物学意义的特定转变：密集集体从紧凑或停滞状态向边界主导剥离和迁移的重组。在模型中，每个粒子携带空间位置和标量内部状态，通过有限范围力相互作用。迁移率定义在空间和内部状态坐标上，具有密度依赖性，并存在不对称交叉耦合。研究者推导了过阻尼极限下的随机动力学更新方程，并进行了数值模拟。

Result: 研究发现，仅内部状态坐标中的迁移率就为大规模空间重组提供了独立的控制轴。具体而言，增加基线内部状态扩散率并调节其密度依赖性，可在保持基线位置扩散率固定的情况下，驱动从停滞聚集态到剥离样状态的转变，该状态具有广泛的空间偏移、强烈的向外径向偏置和边缘局部化活动。转变伴随着空间和内部状态位移的相关展宽、径向密度和密度-曲率剖面的系统性重组，以及对系统尺寸的显著依赖性。

Conclusion: 这些结果确立了该方法的实用性，并推动了一个更广泛框架的发展，旨在用统一的形式体系建模状态变化、空间重新分布和邻域结构。研究支持了生长聚集态可以进入边界主导迁移状态的观点。

Abstract: Numerous problems in development, regeneration, and disease involve simultaneous evolution of both spatial organization and the internal state of the constituents in addition to local interactions and crowding. This motivates us to study a minimal model for interacting populations evolving in coupled spatial and internal-state coordinates. We focus on a specific transition of particular biological interest: the reorganization of dense collectives from compact or arrested states toward boundary-led peeling and migration. In our formulation, each particle carries a spatial position and a scalar internal state, and interacts through finite-range forces. Mobilities are defined on both spatial and internal-state coordinates with a density dependence, and are asymmetrically cross-coupled. We derive update equations for stochastic dynamics in the overdamped limit and perform numerical simulations. We find that mobility in internal-state coordinates alone provides an independent control axis for large-scale spatial reorganization. In particular, increasing the baseline internal-state diffusivity and tuning its density dependence drives a transition from arrested aggregates to a peeling-like regime with broad spatial excursions, strong outward radial bias, and edge-localized activity, while the baseline positional diffusivity is held fixed. The transition is accompanied by correlated broadening of spatial and internal-state displacements, systematic reorganization of radial density and density-curvature profiles, and a pronounced dependence on system size, consistent with the idea that growing aggregates can cross into a boundary-dominated migratory state. These results establish the utility of our approach and motivate a broader framework aimed at modeling state change, spatial redistribution, and neighborhood structure within a common formalism.

### [197] [Diffusion from particle-coated drops: the subtle role of particle size](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05903)
*Alexandros T. Oratis,Matteo Camagna,Timo J. J. M. van Overveld,Valeria Garbin*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管颗粒包覆界面（particle-laden interfaces）在稳定乳液方面表现出色，但量化颗粒如何影响溶解溶质（dissolved solutes）的界面传输仍具挑战性。本研究旨在表征颗粒对界面传质过程的影响机制。

Method: 通过将单个颗粒包覆液滴（particle-coated drop）限制在二维构型中，利用荧光显微镜（fluorescence microscopy）追踪荧光染料扩散过程，提取强度分布以获得浓度场的时空测量数据。同时建立了耦合界面传质与颗粒包覆界面的数学模型。

Result: 在多种颗粒尺寸范围内，颗粒对扩散施加的阻力极小。数学模型表明，颗粒单层（particle monolayer）控制着界面通量（flux across the interface）的时间动态，仅在超过紧密堆积极限（close-packing limit）的极端覆盖分数下才会阻碍传输。

Conclusion: 该框架揭示了颗粒通常无法阻碍扩散的原因，为利用颗粒稳定乳液（particle-stabilized emulsions）中的传质过程提供了新途径。研究结果解释了颗粒包覆界面传质的反直觉现象。

Abstract: Many natural and industrial systems involve particle-laden interfaces. Because interfacial particles prevent the coalescence and coarsening of drops, they hold promise for various applications requiring stable emulsions. Despite their remarkable ability to stabilize emulsions, it remains challenging to characterize how particles influence the interfacial transport of dissolved solutes. Here, we quantify the diffusion from a single particle-coated drop by confining it to a two-dimensional configuration. Using fluorescence microscopy, we extract the intensity profiles of the fluorescent dye as it diffuses from the drop, yielding spatio-temporal measurements of the concentration field. Over a range of particle sizes, the particles impose minimal resistance to diffusion. We rationalize this counterintuitive result with a mathematical model that couples interfacial mass transfer to a particle-coated interface. We show that the particle monolayer controls the temporal dynamics of the flux across the interface, hindering transport only at extreme coverage fractions beyond the close-packing limit. This framework reveals why particles often fail to hinder diffusion, offering new pathways to harness mass transfer in particle-stabilized emulsions.

### [198] [Emergent Rotation of Passive Clusters in a Chiral Active Bath](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05909)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索被动粒子浸入手性活性粒子（chiral active particles）浴中的动力学行为，重点关注集体旋转运动的涌现现象，以理解手性（chirality）和集体相互作用在主动-被动混合物（active-passive mixtures）中的关键作用。

Method: 采用数值模拟（numerical simulations）方法，通过调节尺寸比（size ratio）和活性粒子堆积分数（active particle packing fraction）等参数，系统研究被动粒子在手性活性粒子浴中的动力学行为。

Result: 在特定参数范围内，被动粒子聚集成团簇（clusters）并表现出持续旋转（persistent rotation），其特征包括内部结构有序性、增强的形状涨落（shape fluctuations）以及由周围活性浴产生的相干净扭矩（coherent net torque）。手性异质性（chirality heterogeneity）会破坏旋转相干性，而均匀手性浴则促进强超扩散角动力学（superdiffusive angular dynamics）。

Conclusion: 持续旋转并非普遍现象，而是几何结构、活性（activity）和手性之间微妙相互作用的结果。这些发现为理解手性和集体相互作用在塑造主动-被动混合物涌现行为中的角色提供了新见解。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamics of passive particles immersed in a bath of chiral active particles, focusing on the emergence of collective rotational motion. Using numerical simulations, we show that passive particles aggregate into clusters that can exhibit persistent rotation within a well-defined regime of size ratio and active particle packing fraction. This rotational state is characterized by the coexistence of internal structural order, enhanced shape fluctuations, and a coherent net torque generated by the surrounding active bath. Outside this regime, the dynamics remain predominantly diffusive, highlighting that sustained rotation is not ubiquitous but arises from a delicate interplay between geometry, activity, and chirality. Furthermore, we demonstrate that chirality heterogeneity disrupts rotational coherence, while a uniform chiral bath promotes strongly superdiffusive angular dynamics. These results provide new insights into the role of chirality and collective interactions in shaping the emergent behavior of active-passive mixtures.

### [199] [Long distance attraction between particles in a soap film](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05918)
*Youna Louyer,Megan Delens,Nicolas Vandewalle,Benjamin Dollet,Isabelle Cantat,Anaïs Gauthier*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验和理论模型揭示了水平肥皂膜中毫米级颗粒间的非互易长程吸引力，其不对称性可达150%，源于边界条件导致的界面变形差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究水平肥皂膜（horizontal soap film）中毫米级颗粒的相互作用，该现象与液体表面颗粒的"Cheerios效应"相似，但几何约束导致界面变形延伸至整个系统，预期会产生独特的相互作用特征。

Method: 通过追踪颗粒动力学（particle dynamics）测量颗粒间作用力，并建立理论模型（theoretical model）来解释观察到的现象，特别关注界面变形对颗粒位置的依赖性。

Result: 实验发现颗粒间存在极长程吸引力（extremely long-ranged attraction），导致持续达十秒的复杂轨道运动；作用力在方向和大小上均表现出非互易性（non-reciprocal），当一颗粒靠近膜中心而另一颗粒靠近框架时，不对称性可达150%。

Conclusion: 该研究首次展示了由边界条件引起的非互易有效相互作用（non-reciprocal effective interactions），当两颗粒均靠近膜中心时互易性恢复，为理解受限几何中的颗粒相互作用提供了新视角。

Abstract: Millimeter-sized particles trapped at the surface of a liquid bath attract each other through the deformation of the liquid-air interface, a phenomenon known as "the Cheerios effect". We consider here a situation similar at first sight: the interaction between two millimeter-sized particles trapped in an horizontal soap film. In this geometry, the deformation of the film due to the weight of one particle extends over the entire system size, which induces an extremely long-ranged attraction. Combined with the low viscous friction in the film, this leads to intricate particle orbits, lasting up to ten seconds before the two particles eventually collide.
  By tracking the particles dynamics, we measure the force exerted by each particle on the other, and we develop a theoretical model. Because the interface deformation induced by a particle depends on its position in the soap film, the attractive force has two features that fundamentally depart from classical interaction forces. The force exerted by one particle on the other differs both in direction and magnitude from the reverse interaction, with an asymmetry reaching 150% when one particle is close to the center and the other one close to the frame. Reciprocity is recovered when both particles are close to the film center. These results are a original example of non-reciprocal effective interactions due to boundary conditions.

### [200] [Hydrodynamic Switching Fronts Polarize Deformable Particle Trains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05925)
*Linzheng Huang,Hengdi Zhang,Zaicheng Zhang,Zaiyi Shen*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究展示了在泊肃叶流（Poiseuille flow）中，受限的拖鞋形可变形粒子链通过传播的切换前沿（switching fronts）实现定向状态传输和极性选择。这种集体极化行为源于粒子间方向性偏置的切换，由拖鞋形粒子的前后不对称性驱动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在揭示被动多体悬浮系统中集体极化（collective polarization）的形成机制。传统上，活性系统（active systems）常表现出集体行为，但本研究关注被动系统（passive systems）中是否也能通过局部双稳态（local bistability）和定向耦合（directional coupling）产生类似的极化现象。

Method: 研究采用拖鞋形可变形粒子在泊肃叶流中的受限链作为模型系统。通过分析粒子间方向性偏置的切换机制，建立了包含局部双稳态和定向耦合的最小粗粒度模型（minimal coarse-grained model）。该模型能够捕捉前沿传播和停滞的关键特征。

Result: 研究结果表明，局部从异号对（opposite-sign pair）到同号对（same-sign pair）的转变会启动一个流向传播前沿，将倾斜符号（inclination sign）在粒子间逐级传递。在周期性链中，前沿会粗化（coarsen）形成均匀极化状态；而在长开放链中，前沿会停滞并留下持久的极化域（polarized domains）。

Conclusion: 局部双稳态和定向耦合是被动多体系统中实现集体极化的有效途径。该机制不依赖于活性驱动，为理解被动悬浮系统中的集体行为提供了新视角，并可通过粗粒度模型进行有效描述。

Abstract: We show that propagating switching fronts mediate directional state transmission and polarity selection in a passive many-body suspension. In confined trains of slipper-shaped deformable particles in Poiseuille flow, this behavior originates from directionally biased switching between neighboring particles: owing to the fore-aft asymmetry of the slipper, an upstream particle drives switching of its downstream neighbor more effectively than in the reverse direction. A local transition from an opposite-sign pair to a same-sign pair therefore launches a streamwise front that relays the inclination sign from particle to particle. A minimal coarse-grained model with local bistability and directional coupling captures front propagation and arrest. In periodic trains, the fronts coarsen into a uniformly polarized state, whereas in long open trains they arrest and leave persistent polarized domains. Our results point to local bistability and directional coupling as a route to collective polarization in passive many-body systems.

</details>
